gyis rgyal srid phrogs

nas/ rgyal po'i btsun mo la rta rdzi bcol lo/ /der yum btsun mo des rta mtshor phyin nas/ gnyid log pa'i rmi lam na/ yar lha sham po'i sprul pa mi dkar po zhig dang 'brel ba
rmis/ gnyid sad tsa na/ sngas mgo nas g.yag dkar po zhig long nas song ba mthong / de nas zla ba brgyad song tsa na/ yum btsun mo de la khrag gong po lag mgo tsam 'gul
shes pa zhig skyes byung ba bskyur bar ni sha nas chad snying rje bar byung / gso ba la ni kha mig gang yang mi 'dug nas/ 'brong ru dron mo zhig tu bcug gos thung gi ngar
pas dril bzhag pas/ zhag 'ga' song dus bltas pas/ khye'u zhig byung 'dug de'i ming yang 'jang gi bu ru la skyes zhes grags so/ /des lo bcu lon dus nga'i pha dang / phu bo
rnams gar song zhes/ a ma la dris pas/ a mas sngar gyi lo rgyus rnams zhib par bshad pa dang / ru la skyes kyi thabs sna tshogs kyis nyang chu skya mo nas yab kyi pur btsal
te/ phying yul dar thang du yab kyi bang so brtsig blon po long ngam bsad/ phu bo gsum gdan 'dren phyin pas/ sha khri dang / nya khri gnyis gdan ma drongs te| kong po
dang / nyang po'i rje mdzad nas da lta yang gdung brgyud yod do/ /spo bo'i yul nas/ sras bya khri gdan drangs te/ yar lungs su bzhugs/ sku mkhar bying nga stag rtse brtsigs/
yum gyi sras bya khri la 'jus nas/ lha la dmod bor bas nam mkha' nas sgra byung ste/ khyod kyi bu de kun las rgyal bar 'gyur ro/ / bu de kun las rgyal zer kyang spu
de gung rgyal du grags so/ /rgyal po 'dis rgyal sa bzung ste/ blon po ni ru la skyes kyis byas so/ /rgyal blon 'di gnyis kyi dus su| g.yung drung gi bon byung ste/ ston
pa gshen rab mi bo bya ba stag gzig 'ol

mo'i lung rings su sku 'khrungs/ khams chen po brgyad la sogs pa bon po'i chos thams cad/ zhang zhung gi yul nas bsgyur te dar zhing rgyas par mdzad/ bon la rigs dgu ru phye
ste/ rgyu'i bon po la rigs bzhi/ 'bras bu'i bon po la rigs lnga'o/ /'bras bu'i bon rigs lnga ni/ g.yung drung theg pa bla na med pa la zhugs pa ste/ bde 'gro mtho ris kyi
lus thob par 'dod do/ /rgyu'i bon po rigs bzhi ni/ snang gshen bal thod can/ 'phrul gshen bal tshon can/ phywa gshen ju thig can/ dur gshen mtshon cha can no/ /de la snang
gshen bal thod can gyis phywa dang g.yang 'gug lha dang sman gsol/ dge legs dang dpal bskyed nas mi nor rgyas par byed/ 'phrul gshen bal tshon can gyis mdos dang yas
gtong / srid dang rten 'dzugs/ 'phral phugs kyi 'gal rkyen thams cad sel bar byed do/ /phywa gshen ju thig can gyis/ legs nyes kyi lam ston/ yin min gyi the tshom sel/ zag
bcas kyi mngon shes 'chad par byed do/ /dur gshen mtshon cha can gyis gson gyi bgegs sel/ gshin gyi dur 'debs/ chung gi sri gnon/ gnam gyi rgyu skar blta/ sa'i 'dre btul
ba yin no/ /thams cad rnga shang gi sgra 'khrol ba ste/ chab srid ni sgrub ste lte'u bsgyur ro/ /bon gyi lo rgyus las/ rje gnya' khri btsan po'i dus su bon dar/ rgyal
po gri gum btsan pos bon bsnub/ rgyal po spu de gung rgyal gyi dus su bon dar/ rgyal po khri srong lde btsan gyi dus su bon bsnub/ rting du bon gyi bla ma rnya chen li sho
ka ra bya bas/ khams nas bon gyi me ro bslang nas/ dbus gtsang du phebs/ bon chos thams cad gter nas bton/ ri zhing / dar lding / dge lding / en tsa kha/ bzang ri/ yog
thang la sogs pa bon po'i sde btsug bon rgyas par byas zer/ bon la'ang / bstan pa snga dar/ bar dar/ phyi dar gsum byung

'dug gzhan yang shing bsregs pa'i snying po sol ba/ ko ba bzhu ba'i snying po la spyin byung / lcags rdo/ zangs rdo/ dngul rdo gsum rnyed nas/ sol bas rdo gsum bzhus nas/ dngul
zangs lcags gsum bton/ shing la bug pa phug nas gshol dang gnya' shing bcos/ /mthun gnyis gnya' ru bsdebs pas thang rnams zhing du rmos/ /rgya mtsho yur la drangs nas
zhing la sa bon btab/ /de'i gong na zhing la so nam med/ yab gri gum btsan po dang / sras spu de gung rgyal gnyis la stod kyi steng gnyis zer/ steng gnyis bang so g.ya'
dang spang la btab/ de'i lag dpon ru la skyes kyis byas so/ /spu de gung rgyal gyi sras/ a sho legs/ de'i sras de sho legs/ thi sho legs/ de'i sras gu ru legs/ de'i sras
'brong zher legs/ de'i sras i sho legs/ de rnams bar gyi legs drug zer/ legs drug bang so g.ya' spang mtshams su btab/ /de'ang spang la 'ja' tshon rgyas pa 'dra/ i sho legs
kyi sras/ za nam zin lde de'i sras lde 'phrul nam gzhung btsan/ de'i sras se bsnol nam lde/ de'i sras lde bsnol nam/ de'i sras lde bsnol po/ de'i sras lde rgyal po/ de'i
sras lde sprin btsan/ 'di rnams ni sa'i lde brgyad do/ /lde brgyad bang so chu bo'i gzhung la btab/ /de'ang mtsho la kha ba bab pa 'dra/ rgyal po lde sprin btsan gyi
sras khri btsan nas/ de'i sras khri dgra dpung btsan/ de'i sras khri de thog btsan/ 'di gsum la 'og gi btsan gsum zer/ btsan gsum bang so gangs dkar rtse la btab/ de'ang
gangs la na bun chags pa 'dra/ khri de thog btsan gyi sras/ lha tho tho ri snyan shal zhes bya ba| 'phags pa kun tu bzang po'i sprul pa des/ dgung lo brgyad cu'i bar du

rgyal srid bskyang ste/ ma brtsigs lhun gyis grub pa'i sku mkhar chen po pho brang 'um bu bla mkhar gyi rtse la bzhugs pa las/ sngon bcom ldan 'das kyis 'od ma'i tshal nas
lung bstan pa bzhin/ bod du sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar ba'i rten 'brel la/ nam mkha' nas mdo sde za ma tog snying po yi ge drug ma/ spang skong phyag brgya pa/ gser gyi
mchod rten khru gang pa/ tsindha ma n-i sAtstsha'i skol phor/ mu tra'i phyag rgya rnams nyi ma'i 'od zer la 'grogs te/ rgyal po'i pho brang gi steng du babs pa las/ khyed
nas gdung rabs lnga na 'di'i don shes pa'i rgyal po zhig 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes/ srong btsan sgam po la zer/ nam mkha' nas lung bstan/ rgyal pos kyang rten de rnams ngo
mtshar che bar ni dgongs/ gang yin ni ma mkhyen te/ gnyen po gsang ba zhes mtshan gsol nas/ rin po che'i khri la bzhag nas mchod pa phul bas/ de'i yon tan gyis rgyal po
slar gzhon sha can du gyur nas/ dgung lo brgya dang nyi shu thub ste/ sku lus gcig la sku tshe gnyis thub ces grags so/ /rgyal po des dam pa'i chos kyi dbu brnyes pa yin
no/ /de yi bang so rang gi yul du btab/ /yul gyi ming ni phying lung dar thang zer/ /bang so de yang sa phung sbra 'dra yod/ /lha tho tho ri snyan shal gyi sras khri snyan
gzugs btsan/ des kyang gnyen po gsang ba la mchod pa byas pas chab srid rgyas par byung ngo / /de yi bang so don mkhar mda' ru brtsigs/ /de yang 'phul med sa phung brdal
ba 'dra/ /de'i sras 'brong snyan lde ru/ rgyal po des dwags po'i yul nas mchims bza' klu rgyal/ klu mo yin/ bya ba'i btsun mo zhig blangs pas/ sras dmus long zhig 'khrungs
pas/ ming yang dmus long dkon pa bkra zhes grags

so| |mchims bza' klu rgyal de dang po shin tu mtshar ba zhig yod pa la/ rting du sngo la rid par byung bas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyod dang po shin tu mtshar ba zhig yod pa
la/ na ba ni min nam/ 'di 'dra yod pa ci yin gsungs pas/ nga rang gi yul na zas shig yod pa de/ 'di ru med pas lan pa 'dra zer bas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ 'o na zas de cis
kyang long la zo gsungs pas/ der g.yog mo dam pa zhig zas de len btang bas/ der mos sbal pa'i ro mang po mar gyis btsos te/ khal mang po blangs byung bas/ de rnams mdzod
du sbas/ mis ma mthong bar byas shing lkog tu zos pas/ sha bkrag sngar bzhin rgyas shing 'od dang ldan pa byung ba dang / rgyal po'i thugs la zas de yon tan can zhig 'dug
pa la/ ngas kyang za dgos bsams te/ btsun mo med pa'i shul du/ lde chab kyi sgo phyes nas nang du byon pa dang / mdzod nang na sbal ba'i ro mang po mar gyis btsos pa'i
rkyal pa mang po 'dug nas rnam rtog skyes te/ rgyal po la bsnyung du mdze byung ngo //de nas rgyal po yab yum gnyis ka gson por bang sor bzhugs nas/ sras la zhal chems bzhag
pa ni/ yab mes kyi thugs dam gnyen po gsang ba la mchod pa gyis/ 'a ci'i yul nas sman pa bos la/ mig phye nas rgyal srid zungs shig gsung ngo / /'brong snyan lde ru'i
bang so zhang mdar brtsigs bang so'i ming kyang gson chas zlum por grags/ /zhes so/ /de nas dmul long dkon pa bkras/ gnyen po gsang ba la mchod pa phul zhing mos gus byas
pas/ sman pa bos nas mig phye bas/ skyi shod stag gi ri la gnyan 'gro ba gzigs pas na/ mtshan yang stag ri gnyan gzigs zhes grags so/ / stag ri gnyan

gzigs bzhi bcu lon dus 'das/ /de yi bang so don mkhar mda' ru brtsigs/ /gral ni khri snyan gzung btsan g.yon na yod/ /de yang 'phul med sa phung brdal ba 'dra/ /stag ri gnyan
gzigs kyi sras gnam ri srong btsan yin la| rgyal po 'di'i dus su/ rgya nag nas sman dang rtsis byung / rgya dang gru gu btul/ byang nas tsha rnyed/ sku mkhar khri brtsigs
'bum brdugs bya ba brtsigs/ chab srid lo drug cu bzung nas 'das so/ /de yi bang so don mkhar mda' ru brtsigs/ /gral ni khri snyan gzung btsan g.yas na yod/ /de yang 'phul
che rtsig pa saug khar yod/ /ming kyang gangs ri sog kha lags so skad/ /ces so/ /de ltar phan bde thams cad 'byung ba'i gzhi ma/ bod rgyal po'i gdung rabs/ shes bya
rab gsal nas/ sangs rgyas mya ngan las 'das nas/ lo nyis stong dus/ rje gnya' khri btsan po byon/ nyis stong lnga brgya na/ lha tho tho ri snyan shal byon gsung bar 'dug
rje gnya' khri btsan po nas/ lha tho tho ri snyan shal yan la gdung rabs nyi shu rtsa bdun la lo lnga brgya song 'dug par nges zer na'ang / chos dang 'brel pa'i rgyal por
mi 'dug pas/ lo rgyus rgyas par ma bkod/ lha tho tho ri snyan shal gyi dus su/ dam pa chos kyi dbu brnyes/ lo brgya dang nyi shu thub/ de nas gdung rabs bzhi/ gnam ri srong
btsan yan la/ lo brgya dang bcu gcig lon pa yin zhes ka tshigs chen mo na bshad yod do/ /'di dag ni zur tsam bsdus pa yin gyis/ rgyas par 'dod na ka tshigs chen mo dang
/ bka' chems ka khol ma/ rgyal rabs dpag bsam ljon shing rnams la gzigs shig bod rgyal po'i gdung rabs dang po ji ltar byon pa bstan pa'i le'u ste brgyad pa'o// //

dgu pa/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi sku la 'od zer bzhi 'phros pa las/ chos rgyal 'khrungs pa'i skor/ de nas 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyis bod kha ba can gyi sems can rnams
'dul ba'i dus la bab par mkhyen nas/ sku la 'od zer bzhi 'phros te/ de'ang spyan g.yas pa nas 'od zer gcig 'phros de| bal po'i yul du song ba/ bal po'i yul thams cad
'od zer gyis khyab/ bal po'i rgyal po de ba lha yang 'od zer gyis khyab par byas/ grong khyer kho bom klu'i pho brang yang 'od zer gyis snang bar byas so/ /de nas 'od zer
de rnams 'dus nas/ rgyal po de ba lha'i btsun mo'i lhums su zhugs so/ /der zla ba dgu ngo bcu lon pa na/ lha gcig khyad du 'phags pa zhig 'khrungs te/ lha gcig de ni 'jig
rten las khyad du 'phags pa/ sku mdog dkar la dmar ba'i mdangs chags pa/ zhal nas ha ri tsandan gyi dri bro ba/ rig pa'i bstan bcos thams cad la mnga' brnyes pa zhig sku
'khrungs te/ de ni bal mo bza' khri btsun 'di yin no| |yang spyan g.yon pa nas 'od zer gcig 'phros pas rgya nag gi yul du song ste| rgya nag gi yul thams cad 'od zer gyis
khyab par mdzad/ rgya rje tha'i dzung rgyal po yang 'od zer gyis khyab par mdzad/ pho brang zem shing khri sgo yang 'od zer gyis khyab par mdzad/ de nas 'od zer de rnams
'dus te/ rgya rje btsan po'i btsun mo'i lhums su zhugs so/ /der zla ba dgu ngo bcu lon pa na/ lha gcig khyad du 'phags pa gcig sku 'khrungs te/ lha gcig de ni 'jig rten
las khyad par du 'phags pa/ sku mdog sngo la dmar ba'i mdangs chags pa/ zhal nas utpal sngon po'i dri bro ba/ rigs pa'i bstan bcos thams cad la mnga'

brnyes pa zhig 'khrungs te/ de ni rgya mo bza' kong jo 'di yin no/ /yang zhal nas 'od zer gcig 'phros te/ bod kha ba can gyi rgyal khams su/ brag la chu rgyag pa'i 'phrong
la phog pas/ mtha' 'khob 'dul ba'i gnyen po gsang ba 'bru drug chos sku'i rnam par gyur te/ de ni yar 'phrang gi yi ge drug pa 'di yin no/ / yang thugs ka nas 'od zer zhig
'phros te/ kha ba can gyi rgyal khams su song / bod kha ba can gyi yul thams cad 'od zer gyis khyab par mdzad/ yang bsnon sbra stod tshal yang 'od zer gyis khyab par mdzad/
pho brang byams pa mi 'gyur gling yang 'od zer gyis khyab par mdzad/ rgyal po gnam ri srong btsan kyang 'od zer gyis khyab par mdzad do/ /de nas 'od zer de rnams 'dus
te/ rgyal po gnam ri srong btsan gyi btsun mo 'bri bza' thod dkar ma'i lhums su zhugs pa dang / bkra shis pa'i ltas kyis phyogs thams cad du khyab par gyur to/ /der zla
ba dgu ngo bcu lon pa na/ sras khyad par du 'phags pa zhig me mo glang gi lo la/ pho brang byams pa mi 'gyur gling du sku bltams te/ dbu la sangs rgyas a mi dhe ba bzhugs
pa/ phyag zhabs 'khor los mtshan pa/ dbu skra mthon mthing du yod pa zhig bltams so/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis byin gyis rlabs/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis bkra shis
brjod/ lha rnams kyis me tog gi char phab ste| sa yang rnam pa drug tu g.yos so/ /de yang mthong lugs rnam pa gsum du byung ste/ phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas rnams kyi snang
ba la/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs des/ sngon gyi smon lam gyi mthu la brten nas/ bod kha ba can pa'i sems can rnams smin grol la bkod nas/ mtha' 'khob kyi yul 'dir/ mun

pa'i rum du sgron me sbar ba ltar gyur te/ rin po che'i gling du gzigs so/ /sa bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snang ba la/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyis/ mtha' 'khob
kha ba can pa'i sems can rnams chos la bkod pa'i phyir du/ sprul pa'i rgyal por sku sprul nas/ gang la gang 'dul gyis sems can gyi don byed pa'i snang ba byung ngo / /mi
nag tha mal ba rnams kyi snang ba la/ rgyal po la sras 'gran zla dang bral ba'i ngo mtshar ba zhig 'khrungs par mthong ngo | |der rgyal bu de nar lon dus/ bzo dang / rtsis
dang / sgyu rtsal dang / rig pa'i gnas lnga la mkhas shing yon tan dang ldan par gyur pas/ blon po rnams na re/ 'o cag tsho'i rje 'di ni yon tan du ma dang ldan te/ thugs
shin tu sgam mo zer bas/ mtshan yang srong btsan sgam po zhes grags so/ /de nas rgyal po de dgungalo bcu gsum lon dus/ yab 'das te/ rgyal sar byon pa yin no/ /de nas
chos kyi rgyal po srong btsan sgam po de'i thugs kyi dgongs pa la/ bdag gis kha ba can 'dir sems can gyi don byed pa la/ sa phyogs gang du phyin la bsgom snyam pa dang /
bdag gi yab mes lha tho tho ri snyan shal/ 'phags pa kun tu bzang po'i sprul pa des/ lha sa dmar po ri'i rtse la bzhugs 'dug pa/ bdag gis kyang yab mes kyi zhabs kyis bcags
pa'i sa cha/ bkra shis shing nyams dga' ba'i sa gnas der phyin la/ sems can gyi don byed par dgongs te| der yar bsnon sbra stod tshal du dgongs man la/ nangs par gro bteg
ste/ yar 'phrang yi ge drug pa'i drung du khal phog khal ma rnams bzan la skyel nas/ der gro btab bo/ /de nas rgyal pos chab la sku khrus gsol/ chu'i nang na 'od

zer kha dog sna tshogs pa zhig khra cam me 'dug pa blon po sna chen pos mthong nas/ rgyal po la zhus pa/ rje ci lags/ chu'i nang du 'od zer 'di lta bu 'ong ba shin tu ngo mtshar
che lags zhus pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas zhang blon chen po nyon cig mtha' 'khob kha ba can gyi yul 'dir sems can thams cad smin grol la 'god pa'i lam/ sangs rgyas thams
cad kyi dgongs pa gcig tu bsdus pa'i ngo bo| phan bde dang yon tan thams cad kyi 'byung gnas/ mtha' 'khob 'dul ba'i gnyen po/ kha ba can pa'i chos skal/ yang snying 'dus
pa'i snying po/ gsang ba 'bru drug chos kyi sku'i yig 'bru/ gsung mchog yi ge drug ma gcig brag 'di la 'byon par 'dug 'dis kyang sems can mang po'i don byed par 'dug
go gsungs te/ brag de la mchod pa phul ba dang / brag de las 'od zer sna tshogs pa 'phros te/ pha rol gyi brag de la phog nas/ phan tshun 'ja'i mdangs su 'brel pas na/ grong
de'i ming yang 'ja' mdangs bya ba yod de/ brag de la'ang / spyan ras gzigs khar sa pa Ni/ dpal rta mgrin la sogs pa/ rting du bal po'i lha bzo bas 'bur du brkos/ lha'i
sku rang chas su byon yod do/ /de nas byon te dmar po ri'i steng du pho brang btab nas bzhugs so/ /'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi sku la 'od zer bzhi 'phros pa las/ chos
rgyal 'khrungs pa'i le'u ste dgu pa'o// //bcu pa/ blon po thon mis rgya gar nas yi ge bsgyur ba las/ rgyal pos dge ba bcu'i khrims bcas pa'i skor/ de nas chos dge ba bcu
la brten pa'i rgyal khrims 'cha' ba/ 'dod yon lnga spel ba/ phan tshun du skyes bskur ba/ mnga' 'og gi 'bangs rnams la chos kyi bka' bsgo ba la/ bod na yi ge med

pas/ blon po dbang po rno ba bdun rgya gar du yi ge slob tu btang pas/ mtha' 'dre rnam pa gsum la thug nas log pas/ de nas thon mi a nu'i bu/ thon mi sambho Ta zhes pa yid
gzhungs pa dbang po rno ba/ yon tan du ma dang ldan pa zhig yod pa la/ gser mang po bskur nas rgya gar du yi ge slob tu btang ngo / /der blon pos rgya gar lho phyogs su phyin
te/ yi ge'i sgra la mkhas pa bram ze li byin zhes bya ba yod zer ba thos nas/ bram ze ga la ba der phyin te/ gus par phyag btsal te gsol ba/ thugs rje rab rgyas rnam
'phrul lha yi rigs/ /yon tan ldan pas bram ze'i rigs su 'khrungs/ /tshe sngon yon tan sbyangs pa song ba'i mthus/ /lung rigs yi ge'i sgra la phul du phyin/ /mkhas grub rig
'dzin bram ze chen po khyed/ /cung zad bdag la dgongs shing gsan du gsol/ /bdag ni mtha' 'khob bod kyi blon po yin/ /bdag gi rgyal po thugs rje chen po lags/ / bcu gsum
lon nas rgyal sa rab bzung ste/ /rin chen khri yi steng du bzhugs pa'i dus/ /'khor 'bangs rnams la chos kyis tshim pa dang / /dge ba bcu yi rgyal khrims bca' ba la/ /bdag
gi yul na yi ge'i srol med pas/ /bdag la phyag rten rgya chen bskur nas ni/ khyed kyi yul du yi ge slob tu btang / /mkhas pa khyed kyis sgra tshad yi ge'i tshogs/ /ma
lus bdag la gnang bar mdzad du gsol/ /zhes zhus nas/ gser rnams phyag tu phul ba dang / bram ze chen po des/ gser phyag tu bzhes nas lan mdzad pa/ legs par nyon cig skal
ldan rigs kyi bu/ /thon mi zer ba'i blon po rig pa can/ /bden gnyis don rtogs blon chen khyed la ni/ /yi ge'i sgra dang snyan ngag la sogs dang / /gzhan yang

yon tan ngo mtshar can rnams kun/ /blon chen khyed la bdag gis bslab par bgyi/ khyod kyis mtha' 'khob bod kyi rgyal khams su/ /'gro ba rnams la yi ge'i sgra tshad dang / /lung
rig man ngag rnams kyis tshim par mdzod/ /ces smras te/ rin po che'i gzhal yas khang du khrid nas yi ge'i 'bru bstan pas/ der blon po thon mis rig pa'i rtsal phyes/ shes
rab kyi sgron me bteg nas yi ge bslabs pas/ na ga ra'i sde tshan/ ga ta'i sde tshan rnams mang du yod pa/ bod la mi 'gyur bas dbyangs yig la bkod/ lAnytsha lha'i yi ge
wartu la klu'i yi ge lhun grub tshang ma bod kyi yi ge la bkod/ rgya yi yi ge lnga bcu ni/ /yi ge gtso bo sum cu la/ / 'phul yig bcu dang mtha' rten bcu/ /rgya yi yi ge
re re bzhin/ /rang gang spyod pa ma gtogs pa/ /kun la khyab pa gcig kyang med/ /de dag thams cad khong du bsdus/ /de la dpe byas bsdus pa ni/ /bod yig sum cu gtan la phab/
/yi ge'i 'bru ni re re bzhin/ /bzo'i rnam 'gyur legs par bcos/ /yi ge'i gtso bo nyi shu la/ /ka kha ca cha ja nya ta tha pa pha tsa tsha dza wa zha za ya sha ha a/ med
kyang rung ba'i yig 'bru gcig wa/ 'phul yig lnga dang / ga da ba ma 'a/ mtha' rten bcu/ ga da ba ma 'a nga na ra la sa/ shin tu gces pa'i yi ge lnga/ ga da ba ma 'a/ rkang
pa can gyi yi ge dgu/ ka ga ta da na nya zha sha ha/ rgya la med pa'i yi ge drug ca cha ja zha za 'a/ yi ge bu ni bcu drug la/ ka ga nga da ta na pa ba ma ca ja nya tsa
dza la ha/ yi ge ma ni bdun du bcos/ ka ga ba za/ kun gyi ma ni/ ra la sa/ 'dogs thams cad kyi ma gsum/la la sgos su ma bzhi yod/ ka ga ba za la'i ma/ yig 'bru bzhi po
'di la/ la kho na 'dogs/ la la sgos su bu gnyis yod/ /ca dang ha gnyis la yi bu/ /

tsa dang dza gnyis ra yi bu/ /'phul dang mtha' brten mi byed cing / /ma bu gnyis ka mi byed pa'i/ /rang sa 'dzin pa'i yi ge bcu/ kha cha tha pa tsha wa zha ya sha a/ ga ba
yi ge kun tu rgyu/ /ma dang bu gnyis ka byed/ 'phul dang mtha' brten gnyis ka byed/ steng na zha ltar lding ba gsum/ /na ro gi gu 'greng po ste/ /'di gsum yi ge kun la khyab/
/'og na gdan ltar mdzes pa gsum/ /ya ta ra ta zhabs kyu ste/ /ya ta 'dogs pa'i yi ge bdun/ /kya khya gya pya phya bya mya/ /ra ta 'dogs pa'i yi ge bcu gcig yod/ kra
khra gra pra phra bra mra sra shra dra hra/ zhabs kyu'i yi ge kun la khyab/ kyu khyu kru khru/ ya ta ra ta gnyis la'ang khyab/ 'dogs dang sdeb sbyor blo la shar ro/ / gzhan
yang lAnytsha lha'i yi ge 'dra/ ha dang 'a gnyis kyis yi ge'i bu byed pa dang / na log sha log tha log byed pa sogs ni/ saM skr-i ta'i skad/ bod du gzungs sngags su 'gyur
dus/ yi ge'i rnam dpyod la mkhas pa'i paNDita rnams kyis rting du bcos so/ /de la dpe byas nas yi ge dbu can du byas/ wartu la klu'i yi ge 'dra/ de la dpe byas nas yi
ge zur can du byas so/ /'di ni zur tsam yin gyis/ rgyas par 'dod na thon mis/ dang po yi ge'i rnam 'gyur gyi bzo brtsam/ ka mad sum cur bsgyur/ sdeb sbyor bsgrig pa'i gzhi
ma/ thon mi'i mdo rdzi'i sgra mdo bya ba yod kyis de dag la gzigs shig gzhan yang blon po thon mi des/ paNDi ta lha rig pa'i seng ge la/ sgra'i bstan bcos thams cad bslabs
nas/ rig pa'i gnas lnga la mkhas par gyur te/ 'dus pa rin po che'i tog mdo za ma tog spyan ras gzigs kyi mdo rgyud nyi shu rtsa gcig rnams bod du bsgyur/ lo rgyus gcig
na/ shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa yang bsgyur zer ba'ang 'dug mdor na blon po thon mi de/ bslab shes kyi yon

tan du ma la mkhas par gyur to/ /de nas blon po bod du byon pa'i dus su/ bram ze la gsol ba/ thugs la btags so rgyal ba'i sras/ /bka' drin che'o ngo mtshar che/ /byin gyis
rlobs shig thugs rje can/ /rig pa dri med kyi nam mkha' la||thabs shes gnyis kyi rgyu skar shar/ /smon lam dag pa'i chu 'dzin 'khrigs// sgra tshad yi ge'i nyi zla shar/ /'gro
ba ma rig mun pa sel/ /bde gsal yid kyi rgya mtsho la/ /rig pa blo yi chu bran 'khor/ /smon lam dag pa'i chu bya lding / /sgra tshad yi ge'i nor bu bzhugs/ /'gro ba'i
dbul phongs sel bar byed/ /sgyu lus dri med sdong po la/ /thabs shes gnyis kyi yal ga rgyas/ /bslab shes yon tan me tog shar/ /sgra tshad yi ge'i 'bras bu smin/ /bdag cag
blon po thon mi la/ / ma lus gnang ba thugs la btags/ /rgya gar yul du phyin pa yin/ /mkhas grub khyed dang mjal ba yin/ /yon tan gzhi ma yi ge yin/ /ma lus khong du chud
pa yin/ /bod yul dbus su 'gro ba yin/ /rgyal pos dga' ston mdzad pa yin/ /rgyal srid chos bzhin skyong ba yin/ /rgyal pos dbu mdzad blon 'bangs la| |sgra tshad yi ge
spel ba yin/ /kun la rgyas par byed pa yin/ /thugs la btags so rgyal ba'i sras/ /zhes brjod de/ zhabs spyi bos blangs/ theg pa chen po'i chos du ma dang bcas te bod du phebs/
bsu ba dga' ston bsam gyis mi khyab pa byas/ rgyal po dga' ston gyi gdan sar byon pa la/ blon po thon mis/ na ro/ gi gu/ zhabs kyu sogs sde tshan du byas te/ yi ge'i
phud phul ba/ zhal ras gsal la ngang mdangs gang ba bzang / /gdams ngag zab la ma chad tha dad dang / /las ngan bag chags thams cad bsal mdzad pa/ /'phags pa ma

pham yang dag dam pa lags/ /bde gshegs bden nges ye shes te/ /ting 'dzin zhi nyid rig cing gzigs/ /nyon mongs tshogs bcom mgon po mchog / dug gsum bdud 'dul kun tu thul/ /thon
mi'i yi ge'i phud 'di/ dzen khog sna rdo'i lha khang la brag la brkos nas yod do/ /spyan ras gzigs dbang thugs kyi sras/ /srong btsan sgam por mtshan gsol ba'i/ /chos
rgyal khyed la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes bstod pa dang / rgyal po shin tu dgyes nas/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che la dgongs nas/ bkur sti dang phu dud du mdzad do/ /rgyal
pos blon po la yon tan che ba'i bkur sti mdzad pa dang / blon po gzhan rnams phrag dog gis kun nas bslangs te/ rje yis 'bangs la 'di lta bu'i bkur sti mi 'os so zhes
dril bsgrags pa dang / blon po thon mis de dag gi 'gran sems gcog pa'i phyir du/ 'di skad zer ro/ /nga drin chen gyi blon po thon mi ngas/ /lam bgrod par dka' ba'i rgya
gar du/ /lus tsha grang che yang dka' ba spyad/ khong mkhas pa bram ze li byin la/ /yid gus pa'i tshul gyis mos gus byas/ /nor rin chen gser gyi phyag rten phul/ /don rnyed
par dka' ba'i yig 'bru bstan/ /blo the tshom sel ba'i mdzub khrid byas/ /tshig dbyangs yig rnams la mkhas par bslabs/ /rgya yig lnga bcu tham pa de/ /bod yig sum cur
gtan la phab/ /rang mkhas pa'i nges shes blo la shar/ /'phral yon tan thams cad khong du chud/ /dus da lta dga' la phyi ma skyid/ /yul mtha' 'khob bod kyi rgyal khams 'dir/
/mi mkhas pa sleb pa'i snga ma yin/ /nga mun pa sel ba'i sgron me yin/ /rje rgyal po nyi zla'i tshul du bzhugs/ /grogs blon po'i khrod na nga tsam med/ /bod kha ba

can pa'i mi rnams la/ /nga thon mi bka' drin mi che'am/ /thon mi'i nga rgyal zer/ zhes zer bas/ blon po rnams gcig la gcig lta zhing / 'gran sems med par gyur to| |dus de tsa
na/ yang grags kyi blon po sum brgya la/ phyi nang bar gsum gyi blon po 'di rnams kyi ming thang yig chen mo nas bsdus/ming chen gyi blon po bcu drug yod/ med thabs med
pa'i blon chen bzhi/ zhes pa/ rgyal po'i sku gsung thugs kyi zhabs togaphyi nang bar gsum gyi bya ba byed pa'i blon po/ byang chub sems dpa'i gdung brgyud blon po bcu drug
gi thog drangs pa'i blon po sum brgya yod do/ /de'ang phyi blon btsan po drug nang blon bzang po drug bka'i 'phrul blon bzhi'o/ /de la nang blon bzang po drug ni/ 'phrul
gyi sna chen rig bzang / khra 'brug zhang po rgyal gyi khram bzang / hor yin/ cog ro rigs pa'i skad bzang / cog ro/ lhar gzigs shog po bstan bzang / khams pa/ ka'i gnyags
ston 'phel bzang / rgya ma yar ston/ sbas lcang dpal gyi legs bzang / sbas kyi skyed thag ring mo'ang zer/ la sogs te/ blon po brgya tham pas/ rgyal po'i sku'i zhabs
tog dang / nang gi bya ba thams cad byed do/ /phyi blon btsan po drug ni/ byang gi khyung po yin/ khyung po sbu na bzang btsan/ yar stod pa/ lam khri bde lhag khri btsan/
'phan yul rgyal ba/ mu khri rdo rje gnam btsan/ 'jad pa/ mthing gi byang chub mchog btsan/ mchong rgyas pa/ thar pa klu'i dpal btsan/ yar lung son pa/ rong po 'phrul gyi
lde btsan la sogs pa'i blon po brgya tham pas phyi blon byed/ shar phyogs rgya dang / mi nyag gi yul nas bzo dang rtsis kyi dpe blangs/ lho phyogs rgya gar gyi yul nas
dam pa chos kyi sgra bsgyur/ nub phyogs sog po dang / bal po'i yul nas zas nor longs spyod kyi gter

mdzad/ byang phyogs hor dang yu ge ra'i yul nas khrims dang las kyi dpe blang / mdor na phyogs bzhi la dbang bsgyur zhing longs spyod nas/ 'dzam gling phyed kyi kha lo sgyur
ba'i rgyal po mdzad do/ /thon mi sambho Ta/ mgar stong btsan yul bzung / stod lung ram pa ba/ 'bri se ru gong ston/ 'bri khung ba/ nyang khri bzang / nyang ser ba| yang
ston la sogs pa blon po brgya tham pas bar gyi khod snyoms/ rgyal pos bka' stsal pa bzhin/ dge ba bcu'i khrims bca' ba ste/ bzang la bya dga' ster/ ngan pa la chad pa gcod/
mtho ba khrims kyis gnon/ dma' ba thabs kyis skyong / sku bsrung sde bzhir spyad/ phu chu rdzing du bskyil/ mda' chu yur bar drangs/ bre srang gtan la phab/ zhing la
lhu ru spyad/ mi la yi ge bslabs/ rta la mdongs su bris/ legs pa'i dpe srol btsug ste/ 'thab mo byas pa la chad pa/ bsad pa la che chung gi stong byed pa/ brkus pa la brgyad
'jal ngos dang dgu/ bye byas pa'i yan lag gi phran bcad nas yul gzhan du spyugs pa/ rdzun byas pa'i lce gcod pa'o/ /gzhan yang dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su song zhing
/ dad pa dang mos gus bya ba/ pha ma la drin du gzo zhing bkur sti bya ba/ mi drin chen dang pha khu rgan gsum gyi yi mi gcod cing / bzang po'i lan byed pa/ mi ya rabs dang
rigs btsun pa la mi rgol cing dang du len pa/ las dang spyod pa thams cad ya rabs kyi rjes su 'brang ba/ lha chos dang yi ge la blo 'jug cing don shes par bya ba/ las
rgyu 'bras la yid ches shing / mi dge ba 'ba' zhig la 'dzem pa/ mdza' bshes dang khyim mtshes la phan 'dog cing gnod sems mi bya ba/ gzhi drang por bya zhing blo sems dpang
du 'jog pa/ zas chang la tshod

'dzin cing khrel yod par bya ba/ bu lon dus su 'jal zhing / bre srang la g.yo zol mi bya ba/ ma bskos shing ma bcol ba'i bya ba la rtog 'jug mi bya ba dang / gros kyi nang
du bud med kyi kha la mi nyan cing rang tshugs 'dzin pa/ yin min gyis ma tshang ba byung na/ yul lha bstan srung dpang du btsugs nas mna' byed pa la sogs te/ dge ba bcu la
dpe byas nas/ bod khrims nyi shu/ skyi shod/ sho ma ra ru gtan la phab ste/ rje blon kun gyi phyag rgyas btab ste/ nyi zla'i 'od lta bur khyab par mdzad do/ /de ltar mdzad
pas rje btsan 'bangs rnams skyid/ /bstan pa rgyas shing rgyal srid phyogs bcur 'phel/ /chos kyi bka' khrims mdzad pas 'bangs rnams bka' la nyan/ /mi rje lha yis mdzad
pas rgyal khams thams cad skyid/ /pho dpa' rta mgyogs longs spyod lha dang mnyam/ /blo gtad chos la byas pas 'di phyi gnyis kar skyid/ /'thab dang rtsod pa spangs pas thams
cad pha mar shes/ /kun la yi ge bslabs pas sangs rgyas bstan pa dar/ /mi dge'i bshes gnyen med pas dge bcu'i nor bu rnyed/ /kun gyi gtsug tu khur bas skyid pa'i nyi ma
shar/ /thams cad sprul pa yin pas khral dang 'u lag med/ / nam mkha'i mthong la 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad shar/ /dog mo'i sa la padma 'dab brgyad skyes/ /bar gyi ri la bkra
shis rtags brgyad tshang / /ljon shing thams cad dga' ba'i tshal du 'thibs/ /bya rnams kun kyang ca co du ma sgrogs/ /sa rnams kun kyang rnam pa drug tu g.yos/ /lha rnams
kun gyis me tog char pa phab/ /bkra shis nyams su dga' ba'i brag lha'i tshal/ /ljon shing star kha sdong po'i bsil grib la/ /chos rgyal chen po khri yi steng na bzhugs/
/dpa' mdzangs 'phrul ldan

blon po'i tshogs dang bcas/ /bod 'bangs 'khor dang bcas pas mtha' ma bskor/ kha dog sna tshogs ldan pa 'ja' yi gur/ /rgyal po bzhugs pa'i mkha' la gdugs ltar 'khyil/ /bu ram
rgun 'brum ka ra zhal zas sogs/ /ro brgya ldan pa'i zas kyi tshogs rnams kyang / /rgyal pos gsol zhing 'khor rnams tshim par byed/ /chos rgyal chen po'i sku yi skyo sangs
la/ /'bag dang seng ge g.yag seng stag seng dang / /rnga bro mkhan dang gar mkhan la sogs kyis/ /re re bzhin du gar dang rtsed mo 'bul/ /lha yi rnga bo che dang pi wang
dang / /rol mo sil snyan rnams kyis mchod pa dang / /sman mchog a ga ru dang tsandan dang / /dri zhim bdug spos rnams ni rlung ltar g.yo/ /gdugs dang rgyal mtshan ba dan
lhab lhub dang / /sna tshogs dar gyis nam mkha' gang bar mchod/ /yid 'ong mdzes pa'i bu mo bcu drug gis/ /mdzes pa'i rgyan bcas me tog thogs nas ni/ /glu dang gar gyis
rna ba'i dga' ston 'gyed/ /dga' bde skyid pa'i bka' khrims mdzad pa'i tshe/ /bod 'bangs mi res rta re zhon nas rgyug /shing re'i rtse la dar re phyar gin bzhag /dam pa chos
kyi rnga chen dam pa brdung / /dge ba bcu la bstun pa'i rgyal khrims bcas/ /'dod yon lnga dang bstun pa'i longs spyod spel/ kha ba can pa'i rgyal khams 'di nyid du/ /dge
bcu'i rgyal khrims mkha' la nyi zla bzhin/ /bod yul gangs can khrod 'dir khyab par mdzad/ /blon po thon mis rgya gar nas yi ge bsgyur ba las/ rgyal pos dge ba bcu'i khrims
bcas pa'i le'u ste bcu pa'o// //

bcu gcig pa/ rgyal po'i thugs dam gyi lha rgya gar dang / bal po'i yul nas spyan drangs pa'i skor/ des nas sprul pa'i rgyal po chen po de'i thugs kyi dgongs pa la/ bdag gis
mtha' 'khob kha ba can gyi yul 'dir/ sems can gyi don byed pa la/ yi dam gyi lha zhig bzhengs dgos te/ de'i rgyu ni rin po che gser dngul las byas na ni/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus
su sems can bsod nams dman pas dus kyi tha ma la bshigs pa'i daugs yod/ sa dang rdo las byas na ni rgyu ngan/ shing gi rigs la byas na ni 'gas/ bdag gi yi dam gyi lha
bzhengs pa'i rgyu gang legs dgongs te/ 'phags pa la gsol ba btab pas/ tho rangs kyi dus su sangs rgyas dang / byang chub sems dpa' dang / 'phags pa nyan thos dang / lha'i
bu dang bu mo la sogs pa thams cad sprin 'dus pa ltar/ mdun gyi nam mkha' la byon nas/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal dang / 'phags pa kun tu bzang po gnyis kyis/ rin po che'i bum
pa bdud rtsi'i chus gang ba phyag tu bzung nas/ rgyal po la dbang bskur/ sku khrus gsol lo/ /sangs rgyas thams cad kyis byin gyis brlab par mdzad/ byang chub sems dpa' thams
cad kyis bkra shis brjod/ lha'i bu dang bu mo rnams kyis sprin gyi gseb nas lus phyed thon tsam byas nas/ lha'i rol mo sna tshogs kyis mchod pa byed cing me tog gi char
phab bo/ /de ma thag tu rgyal po'i sku la 'od zer sna tshogs pa zhig 'phros nas/ mtha' 'khob kha ba can gyi yul thams cad 'od zer gyis khyab par byas nas gang la gang
'dul gyi sprul pa re res sems can gyi don byas nas/ mtha' 'khob de yang rin po che'i gling lta bur gyur to/ /de nas lha rnams kyis mgrin

gcig tu rgyal po la 'di skad ces zhus so/ /sprul pa'i rgyal po byang chub sems// mgo nag yongs kyi rje khyed kyis/ /mos gus bsod nams bsags pa'i rten/ / yi dam lha gcig spyan
'dren na/ /rgya gar yul gyi lho phyogs su/ /singga la yi rgya mtsho'i 'gram/ /rang byon kharsa pa Ni'i rgyab/ /glang chen nyal ba'i bye ma'i 'og / tsandan sbrul gyi snying
po las/ /grub pa'i rang byon spyan ras gzigs/ /ngo mtshar can zhig de na bzhugs/ /de ni rgyal po'i yi dam yin/ /zhes zer te/ mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas rgyal po'i
thugs kyi dgongs pa la/ yi dam gyi lha de spyan 'dren pa la/ mis mi rnyed pas/ sprul pa zhig btang dgos dgongs pa dang / de ma thag tu rgyal po'i smin mtshams kyi mdzod
spu nas/ sprul pa'i dge slong a ka ra ma ti shI la zhes pa/ dbu la sangs rgyas 'od dpag med bzhugs pa zhig sprul nas/ yi dam de spyan 'dren pa la btang ngo / /de nas sprul
pa'i dge slong des/ rdzu 'phrul gyis rgya gar lho phyogs su byon pa dang / grong khyer dbus 'gyur bya bar slebs te/ de na rgyal po utpal ge sar zhes pa/ rgyal po de gdung
brgyud nang pa sangs rgyas pa yin pa la/ phyis phyi pa mu stegs pa'i chos lugs bzung nas/ nyin re la ra lnga lnga bsad nas/ dbang phyug chen po'i rten la mchod do/ /rgyal
po'i pho brang de'i g.yon na/ sngon sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig gis rab gnas mdzad pa'i mchod rten padma'i 'khor lo can bya ba bzhugs so/ /der sprul pa'i dge slong des/
mchod rten de'i bum pa'i thad kyi nam mkha' la skyil krung mdzad cing bskor ba mdzad pas/ rgyal po'i pho brang gi yang thog nas gzigs pas ngo mtshar du gyur nas/ rgyal pos
sprul pa'i dge slong de pho brang du gdan drangs pa

dang / dge slong 'byon du ma gnang ste/ nan gyis zhus pas/ dge slong gi zhal nas/ ngas ji ltar zer ba'i kha la nyan na khyed kyi pho brang du 'ong / mi nyan na mi 'ong gsungs
pas/ rgyal pos dge slong gis ji ltar gsungs pa la nyan par mdzad nas/ rgyal po'i pho brang du byon nas mchod gnas mdzad do/ /der dge slong gi zhal nas/ khyed sngar nang
pa sangs rgyas pa yin par 'dug pa la/ phyi rol pa'i chos lugs 'di bsgyur nas/ nang pa sangs rgyas pa'i lugs su gyis la| dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su song shig ces gsungs
pas/ rgyal pos de bzhin du zhal gyis bzhes so/ /yang dge slong gi zhal nas/ rgyal po khyed kyis lha khang brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs shig lha khang de rnams kyi nang du
tsandan sbrul gyi snying po dang / tsandan gor shi Sha'i sku brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs shig ces gsungs pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ tsandan sbrul gyi snying po ni 'og min na
yod pas nga la len pa'i mthu med/ tsandan gor shi Sha ma la ya'i byang phyogs na dug sbrul gdug pa can gyis 'khril yod pas/ ngas len mi nus/ lha khang brgya rtsa brgyad
bzhengs pas chog zer ro/ /yang dge slong gi zhal nas/ tsandan sbrul gyi snying po nga la rgyus yod pas len du 'gro dgos/ khyed kyis 'khor g.yog lag cha dang bcas pa thong
zhig gsungs pas/ der rgyal po yon mchod 'khor dang bcas pa singga la'i rgya mtsho'i 'gram du byon pa dang / rdo'i kharsa pa Ni rang byon de'i sku rgyab na glang po che mang
po nyal 'dug go /der dge slong gi zhal nas/ glang po che 'di rnams kyi nang nas kha shar du lta ba/ sna dmar ba/ 'jing khung na gi wang gi zar bu yod pa 'di'i 'og na/
tsandan sbrul gyi snying po yod do gsungs pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/

glang po che'i 'og tu tsandan 'ong ba ci lags zhus pas/ dge slong gi zhal nas/ dbyar tshad pas gdung ba'i dus su tsandan gar yod rnams bsil ba yin zhing / tsandan gyi lo mas
kyang tshad pa'i sdug bsngal sel ba yin pas/ glang po ches tsandan gar yod ngo shes nas tshad pa byung tshe de'i steng du nyal ba yin gsungs so// der glang po che de rnams
dkrogs nas/ de'i 'og gi bye ma brkos pa dang / tsandan sbrul gyi snying po'i sdong po zhig 'dug go /der yang rgyal po'i zhal nas/ mi'i yul na tsandan sbrul gyi snying
po mi 'ong ba la/ 'dir 'ong ba ci lags zhus pas/ dge slong gi zhal nas/ sngon sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig 'jig rten du byon pa'i dus su/ nyan thos dgra bcom pa zhig gi rdzu
'phrul gyis 'og min du byon nas/ tsandan sbrul gyi snying po'i gang bu zhig blangs byon pas/ de'i nang na 'bru bzhi 'dug pa la/ 'bru gsum sangs rgyas 'khor ba 'jig la phul/
'bru gcig jo bo kharsa pa Ni la phul nas dbu'i spyi gtsug tu bzhag pas/ rlung gis bskyod de sku rgyab tu lhung / de sas non pa'i thog tu tshes bco lnga'i nub mo zhig
mkha' 'gro ma rnams kyis bdud rtsi 'pho bas brlan nas myu gu byung / sangs rgyas gser thub 'jig rten du byon tshe me tog rgyas/ sangs rgyas 'od srung 'jig rten du byon tshe
'bras bu smin/ sangs rgyas shAkya thub pa 'jig rten du byon nas sdong po chen por gyur yod pa las/ shAkya thub pa mya ngan las 'das tshe/ sdong po de 'gyel nas bye mas
non pa yin gsungs so/ /der bye ma'i 'og nas sdong po de bton nas/ yal ga rnams bcad/ sdong po de la srub bzhir 'dug pa la/ de nas 'od zer dpag tu med pa byung ste/ 'jig
rten gyi khams thams cad snang bar byas nas/

slar sdong po de la thim pa dang / dal bus chod cig bya ba'i sgra byung ngo / /der sdong po de tshal pa bzhir gshags pa'i nang na/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs yid bzhin gyi nor
bu zhal bcu pa/ zhi zhal gsum/ khro zhal bdun/ zhi rgyas dbang drag gi phrin las 'grub pa/ de'i steng na a mi dhe ba bzhugs pa/ rtsa phyag bcu po phyag mtshan dang bcas
pa/ 'od dang 'od zer phyogs bcur 'phro ba zhig byon no// tsandan de la tshal pa brgya rtsa brgyad byas/ sku brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs te/ lha khang brgya rtsa brgyad du
bzhugs so/ /de nas yang tsandan gor shi Sha len pa la/ dus skabs dang bstun te glang rdzis bstan nas gor shi Sha blangs/ snga ma ltar byas so// de nas dge slong gis mchod
rten padma'i bum pa'i nang nas/ sangs rgyas rabs bdun gyi ring bsrel bre gang bsnams nas slar rgyas btab bo/ /de nas rgya mtsho'i gling la byon pa dang / 'jag ma re re'i
steng na/ sangs rgyas re bzhugs par gzigs nas/ 'jag ma phon cig kyang bsnams so/ /de nas chu bo nai rAnydza ra'i 'gram du byon pa dang / bye ma 'bru re'i steng na sangs
rgyas re bzhugs par gzigs nas bye ma bre gang yang bsnams so/ /de ltar tsandan sbrul gyi snying po la byon pa'i spyan ras gzigs/ tsandan gor shi Sha byang chub kyi ljon
shing gi yal ga chu bo nai rAnydza ra'i bye ma/ ku sha'i 'jag ma phon gcig dben gnas chen po brgyad kyi sa la sogs te/ rgya gar gyi rdzas yi dam gyi lha la sogs pa dge slong
gis spyan drangs te/ bod du byon nas rgyal po la phul bas shin tu dgyes par gyur to/ /de nas yang rgyal po'i thugs kyi dgongs pa la/ da rung lho bal gyi phyogs na/ sbas
pa'i sprul sku/ phyi rabs sems can gyi don byed pa'i rten ngo

mtshar can yod dgongs nas/ yi dam gyi lha la gsol ba btab pas/ rang byon de'i thugs ka nas 'od zer zhig 'phros te/ bal po'i yul du song ngo / /de la gtad nas gzigs pas/ rgya
gar dang bal po'i mtshams kyi nags khrod chen po zhig na/ tsandan ha ri'i sdong po 'od zer phyogs bcur 'phro ba zhig la rang byon mched bzhi byon par gzigs/ de nas yang
sprul pa'i dge slong de rten de rnams spyan 'dren du btang ngo / /der dge slong gis mang yul gyi grong du byon pa na/ yul de na yams nad kyis mi mang po 'chi ba'i sdug bsngal
mthong / de nas byon pa na/ grong khyer yam bu ya 'gal bya ba na/ mdze nad kyis mi mang po 'chi ba'i sdug bsngal mthong / de nas byon pa na rgya gar dang bal po'i mtshams
na steng gdon zh-ig gis glo bur du mi mang po 'chi ba'i sdug bsngal mthong / de'i nags khrod na/ rdzi bo zhig gis ma he mang po skyong gin 'dug pas/ ma he las dang
skal bar ldan pa zhig gis/ nyin mo'i rigs kyi nags khrod der phyin nas/ tsandan ha ri'i sdong po 'od zer phyogs bcur 'phro ba zhig 'dug pa la bskor ba byed cing nu ma gtor
bas dgongs mo rdzi bo la/ ma he bdag pos na re/ khyod kyis nga'i ma he'i 'o ma bzhos 'dug zer ba la/ rdzi bo na re/ ngas ni ma he'i 'o ma bzhos pa med/ ma he ni nyin mo'i
rigs la nags khrod ya gir 'gro'i 'dug go zer ro// de'i sang rdzi bo dang / ma he'i bdag po gnyis kyis 'grogs te/ nags khrod der bltar phyin pas/ ma he de tsandan ha ri'i
sdong po 'od zer phyogs bcur 'phro ba zhig la skor ba bskor nas/ nu ma gtor gin 'dug pas ngo mtshar du byas so| |de nas sprul pa'i dge slong des rgyal po'i thugs dam
tsandan gyi sku de las

'byon par mkhyen nas/ tsandan de sta res bcad pa dang / sku bzhi las gsum byung ste/ stod kyi de na re/ dal bus chod la nga mang yul gyi grong du zhog cig bya ba'i sgra thos/
de gshags pa'i nang nas/ 'phags pa wa ti zhes bya ba zh-ig byon no| |de'i 'og ma des sgra byung ste/ dal bus chod la nga grong khyer yam bu ya 'gal du zhog cig bya ba'i
sgra byung ngo / /de gshags pa'i nang nas/ 'phags pa dbu gang zhes bya ba zh-ig byon no/ /de'i 'og ma des sgra byung ste/ dal bus chod la nga rgya gar dang bal po'i mtshams
su zhog cig bya ba'i sgra byung ngo / /de gshags pa'i nang nas/ 'phags pa lja ma li zhes bya ba zhig byon no/ /de'i 'og ma des sgra byung ste/ dal bus chod la nga bod
kha ba can gyi rgyal khams su rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i yi dam la 'gro'o zhes bya ba'i sgra byung ngo / /de nas 'phags pa wa ti ni mang yul gyi grong du bzhugs/ 'phags
pa dbu gang ni grong khyer yam bu ya 'gal du bzhugs/ 'phags pa lja ma li ni rgya bal gyi mtshams su bzhugs so| |sku de gsum bzhugs pa'i byin rlabs kyis/ grong tshan
so so'i dus ma yin par 'chi ba'i 'jigs pa gsum las thar ro/ /de nas sprul pa'i dge slong des 'phags pa lo ke shwa ra 'di da ltar po ta la'i rtse la bzhugs/ kharsa pa Ni spyan
drangs te/ bod kyi yul du phebs nas chos rgyal srong btsan sgam po la phul bas/ rgyal po shin tu dgyes par gyur nas/ yi dam gyi lha dang mjal bas/ da ni sems can gyi
don byed pa la tshegs med do dgongs so/ /de nas sprul pa'i dge slong a ka ra ma ti shI la zhes bya ba de'ang / slar 'od du zhu nas/ rgyal po'i smin mtshams su thim par gyur
to/ /rgyal po'i thugs dam gyi lha rgya gar dang / bal

po'i yul nas spyan drangs pa'i le'u ste bcu gcig pa'o// //bcu gnyis pa/ bal mo bza' khri btsun gdan drangs pa'i skor/ de nas yang sprul pa'i rgyal po de'i thugs dgongs la/
bdag gis kha ba can gyi yul 'dir/ theg pa chen po'i chos dar bar byed pa la/ bcom ldan 'das kyi sku gcig rgya gar na bzhugs/ gcig bal yul na bzhugs/ gcig rgya nag na bzhugs/
sku de gsum gang na bzhugs pa'i yul der/ theg pa chen po'i chos dar yod pas/ sku de gsum gang rung zhig ji ltar byas la gdan 'dren dgongs te| tsandan gyi sku rang byon
de la gsol ba btab pas/ de'i thugs ka nas 'od zer gnyis 'phros te/ gcig shar du song / gcig nub tu song / nub tu song ba de la brten nas gzigs pas/ nub phyogs bal po'i
yul na rgyal po de ba lha zhes pa la/ sras mo lha gcig khri btsun zhes pa/ sku mdog dkar la dmar ba'i mdangs chags pa/ zhal nas ha ri tsandan gyi dri bro ba/ rig pa'i bstan
bcos thams cad la mnga' brnyes pa zhig bzhugs par gzigs/ de spyan drangs na bcom ldan 'das dgung lo brgyad pa'i sku tshad dang / theg pa chen po'i chos thams cad bod du
gdan 'drong bar gzigs so/ /shar du song ba de la brten nas gzigs pas/ shar phyogs rgya nag gi yul na/ rgya rje tha'i dzung rgyal po bya ba la| sras mo lha gcig kong jo
bya ba/ sku mdog sngo la dmar ba'i mdangs chags pa| zhal nas utpal sngon po'i dri bro ba/ rig pa'i bstan bcos thams cad la mnga' brnyes pa zhig bzhugs par gzigs so/ /de spyan
drangs na bcom ldan 'das dgung lo bcu gnyis pa'i sku tshad dang / theg pa chen po'i chos thams cad

bod du spyan 'drong bar gzigs so/ /de nas rgyal po de 'jig rten las khyad du 'phags shing / thugs bsgoms pas rmi lam du byung ba ltar mdzad de/ nangs par blon po thams cad
rgyal po'i drung du phyag byed du byung ste/ btsan po'i sku la bsnyung mi mnga' lags sam/ sku zo mdog legs sam/ thugs bde ba dang ldan pa lags sam zhes mgrin gcig tu zhus
pas/ shin tu'ang bde ba dang ldan te/ mdang nga'i rmi lam du nub phyogs nas bal rje'i sras mo bu mo mdzes ma zhig dang / shar phyogs nas rgya rje'i sras mo bu mo mdzes ma
zh-ig dang / 'di gnyis nga'i khab tu byung ba rmis so gsungs pas/ blon po mgar na re/ rgyal po'i mnal lam du byung ba'i lha gcig de gnyis nged blon po rnams kyis spyan
ci 'drong byed pas/ mnal lam de gzhan la mi gsung bar zhu zhus so/ /de nas blon po mgar na re/ nged rang phyi nang bar gsum gyi blon po/ gtso bo mi drug gi 'tshogs rten gyi
zas chang / sha gzugs re dang bcas pa khyer la/ sang snga bar brag lha'i ne'u thang la/ ljon shing star ga sdong po'i rtsa rgyal po'i khri'i drung du 'tshogs shig ces
smras so/ /de'i sang blon po gtso bo drug po 'tshogs pas/ 'tshogs rten gyi sha gzugs drug byung ba/ gnyis la rkang pa re/ gnyis la lag pa re/ gcig la brang so/ gcig la dal
mo rnams byung ba bsgrigs pas/ sha khog ma nyams pa zh-ig byung ba dang / thon mi na re/ rten 'brel legs/ da lan gyi 'dun gros 'di la gros ma byas par blo mthun par byung
bas/ gang bsam thams cad 'grub par 'dug 'dun ma rgya ma chung zhig zer ro/ /mgar na re/ 'dun ma rgya mi chung bar byed do/ /nged rang tsho'i rje 'dis dgung lo bcu drug
bzhes/ gzhan du mi rung

bas rgyal srid 'dzin pa la bal yul na/ bal rje sras mo mdzes ma zh-ig yod par 'dug pa de dang / rgya nag gi rgyal po la sras mo mdzes ma zh-ig yod pa de gnyis 'dir btsun mo
la spyan 'dren pa yin no zhes smras pas/ thams cad kyis legs so zhes kha mthun par byas so/ /de nas mgar gyis rgyal po'i drung du phyin nas/ snga sor bal yul gyi lha gcig
de spyan 'dren pas/ bka' gnang bar zhu byas pas/ rgyal pos gser gyi dong rtse lnga bskur nas/ 'dis zhu rten gyis shig gsung ngo / /rin po che baiDUrya'i rmog la/ padma
rA ga'i phra rgyab pa zhig bskur nas/ 'di lha gcig de'i rin du phul cig gsung ngo / /rgyal po des bka' lung mi 'dra ba gsum btud mar gsungs 'ong gis/ de'i dus su 'di gsum
ma nor bar re re bzhin du phul cig gsungs nas/ bka' shog gi sgrom bu gsum bskur/ 'phral gyi zas gos rgyan la sogs pa bskur te/ rta dang drel/ rnga mo la sogs kyi khal mang
po brdzangs so/ /lam 'phrang gang du'ang / jo mo khro gnyer can la gsol ba 'debs kyin song zhig gsung ngo / /de nas blon po mgar gyis rje la phyag byas te/ rdzong dang
yo byad rnams khyer/ khal rnams ded nas/ blon po rta pa brgya tham pa bal yul du chas so/ /der bal yul rin po che'i gling / grong khyer kho bom klu'i pho brang / rgyal po
de ba lha bzhugs pa'i sgo drung du slebs so/ /der rgyal po'i drung du zhu ba btang ste mjal ba la/ gser gyi dong rtse lnga po zhu rten du phul/ rin po che baiDUrya'i rmog
la/ padma rA ga'i phra btab pa de rgyal po'i drung du bzhag nas/ mgar na re/ rgyal po chen po/ rin po che baiDUrya'i rmog 'di/ yon tan dpag tu med pa dang ldan te/ mi
nad phyugs nad byung ba'i dus su rmog 'di

gon nas grong khyer gyi mtha' bskor na mi nad phyugs nad thams cad chad/ sad ser byung daugs pa'i dus su 'di gon nas zhing rnams mtha' bskor na sad dang ser ba thub/ 'khrug
pa byed pa'i dus su 'di gon nas 'thab na g.yul las rgyal bar 'gyur ro/ /'dzam bu'i gling na rmog 'di las lhag pa'i nor med pas/ gong thang dpyad kyis mi chod/ 'di lha gcig
de'i rin du 'bul lo/ khyed kyi lha gcig mdzangs ma de/ nged bod kyi rgyal po'i btsun mo la bka' gnang bar zhu byas pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyed bod kyi rgyal po de
snying gdon gyis bslus sam/ sems 'khrul pa zhig 'dug nga ni sangs rgyas 'od srungs nas deng sang phan chod la rgyal brgyud ma chad pa yin/ khyod dang gnyen zla min te/ 'on
kyang khyod sa thag ring nas sleb 'dug pa/ khyod rang gi yul du log la/ khyod kyi rgyal po de la/ chos dge ba bcu dang bstun pa'i rgyal khrims 'cha' nus sam mi nus dris
shog de nus na lha gcig ster/ mi nus na mi ster gsung ngo / /der mgar gyis bka' shog gi sgrom bu gsum yod pa'i dang po de/ rgyal po'i phyag tu phul bas/ de kha phyes nas
gzigs pas/ mthing shog la gser gyis bris pa/ bal po'i yi ger 'dug pa 'di ltar ro/ khyed bal po'i rgyal po la dge ba bcu'i khrims yod/ nga bod mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po la
de bzhin med de/ rgyal po khyod khrims yod pa la dga' nas bu mo ster na/ ngas sku lus kyi sprul pa lnga stong du sprul nas/ dge ba bcu dang ldan pa'i khrims snga dro zhig
la 'cha' nus par byed do| |de ngo mtshar mi che'am/ de ltar byas kyang bu mo mi ster na/ ngas sprul pa'i dmag khri phrag lnga btang nas/ khyod gsod/ lha gcig phrogs/ grong
khyer thams

cad bcom la bzhag go bya ba 'dug pas/ rgyal po de shin tu skrag par gyur to/ / rgyal po de skrag kyang mi skrag pa ltar byas nas/ khyod kyi rgyal po de kha tsho shin tu che
bar 'dug khyod kyi yul na gtsug lag khang brtsig pa'i nus pa yod dam med dris shog de yod na bu mo ster/ med na mi ster gsung ngo / /yang mgar gyis bka' shog gi sgrom bu
bar ma de rgyal po'i phyag tu phul nas/ rje gcig lags/ 'phrin re la bal bod kyi lam thag ring la yar 'gro mar 'gro byas na/ lha gcig gdan drang pa'i thabs med/ khyed kyi
gsung de'i lan du/ bka' shog 'di legs pa gzigs par zhu byas pas/ der rgyal pos gzigs pas 'di ltar ro/ khyed bal po'i rgyal po la gtsug lag khang brtsig pa'i nus pa yod/
nga mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po la de bzhin med de/ rgyal po khyod lha khang brtsig pa la dga' nas bu mo ster na/ ngas sku lus kyi bkod pa lnga stong du sprul nas/ lha khang
brgya rtsa brgyad du bzhengs te/ sgo thams cad khyod kyi phyogs su bstan la bzhag go |de ngo mtshar mi che'am/ de ltar byas kyang bu mo mi ster na/ sprul pa'i dmag khri
phrag lnga der btang nas/ khyod bsad/ lha gcig phrogs/ grong khyer thams cad bcom la bzhag go bya ba 'dug pas/ rgyal po de shin tu skrag par gyur to/ / rgyal po skrag kyang
mi skrag pa ltar byas nas/ khyod kyi rgyal po de kha tsho shin tu che ba zhig 'dug ste/ khyod bod kyi yul na 'dod yon lnga la longs spyod rgyu yod dam med/ de yod na bu
mo ster/ med na mi ster/ da lan song la dris la shog zer bas/ yang mgar gyis sgrom bu tha ma de rgyal po'i phyag tu phul nas/ 'phrin re re la yul du log pa mi 'ong bas/
rgyal po khyed kyi gsung de'i lan 'di lags

pas gzigs par zhu byas pas/ de rgyal pos kha phyes nas gzigs pas 'di ltar ro/ khyed bal po'i rgyal po la longs spyod yod/ nga bod mtha' 'khob kyi rgyal po la de bzhin med de/
rgyal po khyed nor longs spyod yod pa la dga' nas bu mo ster na/ ngas sku lus kyi bkod pa lnga stong du sprul nas/ rin po che/ gser/ dngul/ dar zab gos dang rgyan/ bza'
btung la sogs kyi longs spyod dpag tu med pa byed cing / khyad par phyogs bzhi nas las sgo phye ste/ mtha'i nor thams cad nga'i sgo drung du 'ong zhing / longs spyod dang
ldan par byed do/ /de ngo mtshar mi che'am/ de ltar byas kyang bu mo mi ster na/ sprul pa'i dmag khri phrag lnga der btang nas/ khyod bsad/ lha gcig phrogs/ grong khyer
thams cad bcom la bzhag go bya ba 'dug pas/ rgyal po de'i thugs la rgyal po smra ba lan cig yin pa| de bzhin du bden srid snyam nas/ shin tu thugs ma bde bar lha gcig bod
la brdzangs par dam bcas te/ zhal ngo nag par bzhugs pa dang / lha gcig na re| yab ci nyes zhus pa dang / yab rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyod bod rgyal po'i btsun mo la 'gro
dgos par 'dug gsungs pas/ lha gcig na re/ yul ngan pa chos dang longs spyod med pa pha ma dang mi 'phrad pa'i sa thag ring sa der mi 'gro zer bas/ yab rgyal po'i zhal nas/
khyod de skad ma zer 'gro dgos/ bod kyi rgyal po de sprul pa'i rgyal po mngon shes rdzu 'phrul stobs dang ldan pa zhig yod par 'dug ngas ji skad smras kyang / blon po
des yul du ma phyin par yi ger lan yod gin 'dug pa khyod mi 'gro ba de shes nas/ sprul pa'i dmag khri phrag lnga 'ong ste/ nga bsad/ khyod phrogs/ yul khams grong khyer
thams cad 'joms

par 'dug pas 'gro dgos gsungs so/ /der lha gcig gi bsam pa la/ nga rang gi yul 'di bzhag nas/ bod mtha' 'khob yul ngan pa/ chos med pa/ pha ma dang mi 'phrad pa'i sa thag ring
po der 'gro dgos pa/ yab kyi bka' ni bcag tu med bsams nas/ lha gcig gis mchi ma bton nas/ yab la 'di skad ces zhus so/ /kye ma yab gcig rgyal po chen po lags/ kha ba
can ni mtha' 'khob kla klo'i yul/ /dam chos ma dar bod yul mun pa'i gling / /mi ni rigs ngan gdol pa sha za'i rigs/ /bkres shing dbul ba yi dwags rgyal khams 'dra/ /de 'dra'i
gnas su bu mo 'gro dgos na/ /yab kyi mchod gnas dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i lha/ /mthong thos dran reg yon tan bsam mi khyab/ /jo bo mi bskyod rdo rje bdag la zhu/ /thub
pa'i rgyal tshab byams mgon rin po che/ / mtshan dpes rab brgyan phan bde 'byung ba'i gter/ /byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo bdag la zhu/ /tsandan jo mo sgrol ma thugs rje can/
/'gal rkyen bar chod sel phyir bdag la zhu/ /rin chen stag sha de dang ratna de/ /bod yul dbul ba sel phyir bdag la zhu/ /rin chen 'dod rgu 'byung ba'i longs spyod dang
/ /zas skom bdud rtsi'i dpal la spyod pa'i gzhi/ /baiDUrya yi lhung bzed bdag la zhu/ kha ba can ni bkres shing skom pa'i gnas/ /rin chen bang mdzod mang po bdag la zhu/
kha ba can ni bsil zhing grang ba'i yul/ /tshe gcig dros pa'i gos kyang bdag la zhu/ /de ltar mtha' 'khob bod kyi rgyal khams der/ /bdag gi spyod lam bya ba ji ltar bya/
/yab gcig rgyal pos bdag la bka' stsol cig /ces gdung ba'i skad kyis mchi ma phyung nas zhus pas/ yab kyis thugs kyi dkyil du

brtse ba'i tshig phyung nas gsungs pa/ nga yi snying dang 'dra ba'i bu mo khyod/ /bod ces bya ba khyad par 'phags pa'i yul/ /ri mtho sa gtsang gangs ri gnyan gyi mgul/ /bsil
la mdzes pa lha gnas gzhal yas khang / /ngo mtshar rmad byung phan bde 'byung ba'i gzhi/ /chu bo bzhi 'bab rtsi shing nags kyis mdzes/ /'bru sna lnga 'khrungs rin chen
sna tshogs 'byung / /rkang bzhi kun khyab rtsi thog mar la spyod/ /rgyal po lha yin 'khor rnams byang chub sems/ /dam chos med kyang rgyal po'i bka' khrims yod/ /de 'dra'i
gnas su bu mo khyod song shig /bdag gi yi dam mi bskyod rdo rje dang / /rje btsun byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo 'di/ /'dzam bu gling pa tshe lo nyi khri'i dus/ /rgya gar chos
rgyal kri kri'i thugs dam du/ /rin chen sna tshogs 'dus pa'i phung po la/ /sangs rgyas 'od srungs dag gis rab gnas mdzad/ /sprul pa'i lha bzos lugs su blugs pa las/ /thog
mar byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo bzhengs/ /de yi rjes la mi bskyod rdo rje ni/ /ngo mtshar dpag med mtshan dpe'i rgyan gyis spras/ /phan bde'i 'byung gnas dad ldan rten
du bzhengs/ /mthong thos dran reg yon tan bsam mi khyab/ /sa steng 'gran zla kun dang bral ba 'di/ /ma 'ongs sems can bsod nams bsag pa'i phyir/ / lha mi'i ston pa shAkya'i
rgyal po de'i/ /dgung lo brgyad pa'i tshad du lung bstan mdzad/ /de yi dus su 'od kyis 'jig rten khyab/ /lha rnams kun gyis me tog char pa phab/ /de ltar yon tan ldan
pa'i rten mchog 'di/ /bdag gi mig gi 'bras ltar gces na yang / /mdzes pa'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzangs/ /rje btsun byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo 'di/ /'gro kun dge la
bkod phyir bdag

gis brdzangs/ /tsandan jo mo sgrol ma rang byon 'di/ /'jigs pa brgyad sogs bar du gcod pa rnams/ /nye bar zhi nas dge legs rgyas pa'i phyir/ /mdzes pa'i bu mo khyod la bdag
gis brdzangs/ /rin chen stag sha de dang ratna de/ / dbul phongs sdug bsngal sel phyir khyod la bskur/ /rin chen dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i longs spyod gter/ /baiDUrya yi lhung
bzed chen po 'di/ /zas skom bdud rtsi'i char pa 'bebs pa dang / /bkres skom sdug bsngal sel phyir khyod la bskur/ /rin chen gser dngul dar zab rgyan dang bcas/ /glang
chen rnga mo drel dang bcas pa'i khal/ /gzhan yang mkho ba'i yo byad zad gos rnams/ /gang la ci 'dod bu mo khyod la bskur/ /rigs bzang yid 'ong mdzes pa'i bu mo bcu/ khyod
kyi skyo grogs byed pa'i 'khor du brdzangs/ /e ma 'bral bar mi phod bu mo khyod/ /gtam gyi rting ma yin no yid la chongs/ kha ba can gyi rgyal po'i pho brang der/ /blon
po bod 'bangs rnams dang 'grogs pa'i dus/ khyod kyi spyod lam bya ba 'di bzhin gyis/ /gsungs te/ 'jig rten mi chos la dgos pa'i bslab bya dpag tu med pa mdzad do/ /de nas
rgyal pos blon po rnams la gnang sbyin dang / dga' ston bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad do/ /jo bo dang byams mgon gnyis ni shing rta byas na lam bgrod par dka' bas/ khal gyi
steng du bzhugs par 'dod pa la/ gang gis kyang ma khyog nas/ sprul pa'i mdzo mo dkar mo gnyis kyis khyog par gyur nas/ jo bo dang / byams mgon gnyis mdzo mo re'i steng
du bzhugs/ rin po che'i khal du ma dang bcas/ lha gcig khri btsun kyang dre'u dkar mo gcig la chibs/ mdzes ma'i bu mo bcu/ bod blon dang bcas pas bskor te bod du

chas so/ /bal po'i blon po 'khor g.yog rnams kyis mang yul gyi grong bar du skyel thung byas so/ /brag dang chu 'thab pa'i 'phrang la khal rnams phog rin po che rnams phreng
skyed byas/ lha rnams zhabs thang du byon kyang zer/ de nas drel dang / rnga mo/ glang po che sogs la khal bkal/ lha rnams rang rang gi khal la chibs nas byon te/ bod kyi
yul du chags phebs so/ /der bod blon dang bod 'bangs rnams kyis rol mo du ma thogs te/ bsu ba rgya chen po byas so/ /de nas rgyal pos dga' ston gyi gdan sar byon te/ lha
gcig khri btsun dang mjal ba la mthong lugs gsum du byung ste/ phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi snang ba la/ rgyal po dang btsun mo gnyis mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi
tshul gyis sems can gyi don byed pa'i snang ba byung ngo / /sa bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snang ba la/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs rgyal po srong btsan sgam po'i
sku sprul/ jo mo khro gnyer can bal mo bza' khri btsun du sku sprul nas/ sems can gyi don byed pa'i snang ba byung ngo / /mi nag tha mal pa rnams kyi snang ba la/ rgyal
po dang btsun mo gnyis skyems la gsol res byed pa dang / skud pa 'khel res byed pa'i snang ba byung ngo / /de nas rgyal po dang btsun mo gnyis blon po'i tshogs dang bcas
pa pho brang du bzhugs pa la/ rgyal po ni yi dam lha'i drung nas phyir mi 'byon par/ mchod pa 'bul zhing smon lam 'debs so/ /der lha gcig khri btsun gyi thugs kyi dgongs
pa la/ rgyal po 'di rigs gzugs dpal gyis mdzes shing / yon tan du ma dang ldan pa zhig 'dug pa la/ phyi rol du ye mi 'byon pa 'di/ mtha'i dmag la 'jig pa yin thag chod/
de la mi

'jig pa'i thabs cig byed dgos/ rin po che baiDUrya'i lhung bzed la gsol ba btab na/ zas chang dpag tu med pa 'ong bas/ bod 'bangs rnams la byin nas las la bskul te/ mkhar las
rgya chen po zhig bya dgos bsams te/ der rgyal po la'ang zhus/ phyi nang gi blon po bka' la gtogs pa thams cad la'ang gros byas te/ baiDUrya'i lhung bzed zas sna mang
pos bkang / rin po che'i khri la bzhag nas gsol ba btab pas/ zas chang ci 'dod pa byung ba dang / bod 'bangs rnams la byin nas/ shing mo lug gi lo la mkhar las kyi rmang
bting / mtho dman gyi tshad la gyang skor sum cu brtsegs pas mtho zhing rgya che ste/ logs re la rgyang grag re yod pa sgo mo che lho phyogs su bstan pa/ mkhar dmar po dgu
brgya/ rtse mo rgyal po'i sku mkhar dang stong tham pa/ mkhar thams cad kha bad rin po che'i rgyan/ mda' yab/ pu shu/ dril bu g.yer kha'i sgra 'khrol ba/ de'i bkod pa mdzes
shing / legs pa'i dbang du byas na/ lha'i dbang po'i rnam par rgyal ba'i khang bzang dang 'dra ste/ blta bas chog mi shes pa/ rin po che sna tshogs kyis brgyan pa/ dar
sna tshogs kyi dra ba dang dra ba phyed pas brgyan te yid du 'ong ba'o// 'jigs pa'i dbang du byas na/ srin po'i grong khyer langka pu ri dang 'dra bar mkhar thams cad
kyi rtse la mtshon cha dang mdung dar dmar po bcu re 'phyar te dar yug gis sbrel ba'o/ /btsan pa'i dbang du byas na/ mtha'i dmag dpung byung yang / mi lngas bsrungs pas thub
pa'o/ /gzhan yang lho phyogs kyi lcags ri la| zabs su 'dom bcu'i dong brus nas/ de'i steng du spang leb bsgrigs/ de'i steng du so phag bsgrigs pas/ de'i steng du rta
gcig gis rgyugs kyang / rta bcus

lhan du rgyugs pa lta bu'i sgra 'ong ba'o/ /lho phyogs su so phag gi mkhar la dpe blangs nas/ brag lha bkra shis kyi gzhal yas khang bya ba/ khri btsun rang gi sku mkhar dgu
thog yod pa zhig brtsigs te/ mtha' gru che zhing mtho la legs pa/ bkod pas mdzes pa zhig brtsigs so/ /rgyal po'i sku mkhar dang / btsun mo'i sku mkhar gnyis kyi bar lcags
zam gyis sbrel te/ de'i 'og na/ dar dang / rnga yab dang / dril bu g.yer kha'i sgra 'khrol ba/ rgyal po yab yum phar gshegs tshur gshegs mdzad pa'o/ /de lta bu'i pho brang
'gran zla dang bral ba ngo mtshar che zhing mdzes pa zhig legs par tshar nas/ rje blon kun gyis dga' ston rgya chen po mdzad do/ /bal mo bza' khri btsun gdan drangs
pa'i le'u ste bcu gnyis pa'o// //bcu gsum pa/ rgya mo bza' kong jo gdan drangs pa'i skor/ de nas yang blon po mgar gyis/ rgyal po'i drung du phyin te/ rgya nag gi lha gcig
de'ang gdan 'dren pa'i bka' gnang bar zhu zhes zhus so/ /yang rgyal pos gser gyi dong rtse bdun bskur nas/ 'di la zhu rten gyis shig gsungs so/ /rin po che'i khrab la padma
rA ga'i phra brgyab pa zhig bskur nas/ 'di lha gcig de'i rin du phul cig gsungs so/ /gser phye bre gang bskur nas 'di gar dgos su thong zhig gsungs so/ /rgyal po des
bka' lung mi 'dra ba lan gsum btud mar gsung du 'ong gis/ de'i dus su 'di gsum re re bzhin gtod cig gsungs nas/ bka' shog gi shog dril gsum bskur ro/ /'phral gyi yo byad
gos dang rgyan la sogs pa/ rnga mo dang / drel la sogs pa la bkal ba'i khal mang po brdzangs

so| |nyin mtshan dang lam 'phrang gang du'ang rje btsun ma sgrol ma la gsol ba 'debs gin song zhig gsungs so/ /de nas mgar gyis rgyal pos bskur ba thams cad khyer khal rnams
ded/ blon po rta pa brgya dang lhan du me pho spre'u'i lo zla ba bzhi pa'i tshes brgyad skar ma rgyal dang 'dzom par rgya nag tu chas so/ /der rgya nag zim shing / bkra
shis khri sgo/ rgya rje tha'i dzung bzhugs pa'i pho brang gi sgo drung du slebs so/ /de na ni mi khyim 'bum tsho tsam yod pa/ logs re la nyin lam re yod pa sgo mo che bzhi
yod pa/ mthong ba tsam gyis dngangs zhing 'jigs pa zhig 'dug go /der rgya gar chos kyi rgyal po'i blon po rta pa brgya tham pa/ rgya mo kong jo 'dod pa la slebs so/ /ge
sar dmag gi rgyal po'i blon po rta pa brgya kong jo 'dod pa la slebs so/ /stag gzig nor gyi rgyal po'i blon po rta pa brgya yang kong jo 'dod pa la slebs so/ /bha ta hor
gyi rgyal po'i blon po rta pa brgya yang kong jo 'dod pa la slebs so/ /mi rigs mi 'dra ba'i gnye bo rta pa lnga brgya rgya rje'i drung du dus gcig la slebs so/ /der rgya
gar ba rnams shar sgo na yod/ ge sar ba rnams lho sgo na yod/ /stag gzig pa rnams nub sgo na yod/ hor rnams byang sgo na yod/ bod blon rnams byang shar mtshams su bsdad
do/ /der blon po gzhan ma rnams kyis zhu rten phul te mjal phrad byas so/ /bod blon rnams kyis mjal bar zhus pas/ sgug tu bcug zhag bdun song ba dang / rgyal po 'khor dang
bcas pa pho brang gi phyi rol du byon pa la/ mgar gyis gser gyi dong rtse bdun po de/ zhu rten du phul/ rin po che baiDUrya'i khrab la padma rA ga'i phra brgyab pa rgyal
po'i drung du bzhag ste/ mgar na re/ rgyal po chen po rin po che

baiDUrya'i khrab 'di/ yon tan du ma dang ldan te/ mi nad phyugs nad byung ba'i tshe khrab 'di gon nas grong khyer la bskor ba byas na nad thams cad zhi bar 'gyur/ sad dang
ser ba byung ba'i tshe 'di gon nas zhing bskor na/ sad dang ser ba thub/ 'khrug pa byed pa'i tshe 'di gon na g.yul las rgyal bar 'gyur ro/ /'dzam bu'i gling na khrab 'di
la gong thang dpyad pas mi chod/ 'di lha gcig de'i rin du 'bul lo/ khyed kyi lha gcig mdzangs ma de/ nged bod kyi rgyal po'i btsun mo la gnang bar zhu byas pas/ rgyal po
des mgar la mig 'bur tshugs su gzigs nas/ rgyal po 'khor bcas kyis mi 'os pa'i khrel gad chen pos bgad de/ rgyal po de'i zhal nas mi srid pa'i gtam shin tu mtshar che/ nga
ni rgya nag spyi bo rgyal po nas deng sang phan rgyal brgyud ma chad pa zhig yin/ khyod bod kyi rgyal pos nga'i stobs dang mnga' thang gi dod mi pher te/ 'on kyang khyed
rnams thag ring nas phebs 'dug da lan phyir log la/ khyod rang gi rgyal po de la dge ba bcu dang ldan pa'i rgyal khrims 'cha' e nus dris la shog de nus na bu mo ster/ mi
nus na mi ster gsungs pas/ blon po mgar na re/ 'phrin re re la/ rgya bod kyi bar la phar 'gro tshur 'gro byas na/ lha gcig spyan drangs pa'i thabs med/ khyed kyi gsung
de'i lan du/ nged bod kyi rgyal pos 'di bskur ba lags zer nas/ shog dril dang po de rgyal po la phul bas/ rgyal pos kha phye nas gzigs pas/ mthing shog la gser gyis bris
pa/ rgya nag gi yi ger 'dug ste/ khyed rgya nag gi rgyal po la khrims yod/ nga bod kyi rgyal po la chos khrims med de/ rgyal po khyed dge ba bcu'i rgyal khrims yod pa la
dgyes nas bu mo ster na/ ngas sku

lus kyi bkod pa lnga stong du sprul nas/ dge ba bcu'i khrims nyi ma gcig la 'cha' nus pa byed do/ /de ngo mtshar mi che'am/ de ltar byas kyang bu mo mi ster na/ ngas sprul
pa'i dmag khri phrag lnga btang nas/ khyed bsad/ lha gcig phrogs/ yul khams thams cad bcom la bzhag go zhes bya ba 'dug pas/ rgyal po de shin tu skrag par gyur te/ skrag
kyang mi skrag pa ltar byas nas/ khyed bod kyi rgyal po de kha pho shin tu che bar 'dug khyed bod kyi yul na gtsug lag khang brtsig pa'i nus pa'i stobs yod dam med/ de bzhin
yod na bu mo ster/ med na mi ster/ da lan song la dris la shog gsungs pas/ yang mgar gyis bka' shog gi shog dril bar pa de rgyal po'i phyag tu phul nas/ 'phrin re re
la bod du 'gro ba mi 'ong bas/ rgyal po khyed kyi gsung de'i lan 'di lags pas gzigs par zhu byas pa dang / rgyal pos kha phye nas gzigs pas 'di ltar ro/ khyed rgya nag gi
yul na chos dar/ gtsug lag khang brtsig pa'i stobs yod/ nga bod kyi rgyal po la gtsug lag khang brtsig pa'i nus pa med de/ rgyal po khyed gtsug lag khang brtsig pa la dgyes
nas/ lha gcig ster na/ ngas sku lus kyi bkod pa lnga stong du sprul nas/ gtsug lag khang brgya rtsa brgyad bzhengs la/ sgo thams cad khyed kyi phyogs su bstan no/ /de
ngo mtshar mi che'am/ de ltar byas kyang bu mo mi ster na/ ngas sprul pa'i dmag khri phrag lnga btang nas/ khyed gsod/ lha gcig phrogs/ yul khams thams cad bcom la bzhag
gi zer ba 'dug pas/ rgyal po de shin tu skrag par gyur to/ /der skrag kyang mi skrag pa khad byas nas/ khyod kyi rgyal po de kha pho shin tu che bar 'dug khyod kyi yul na
'dod yon lnga la longs spyod pa

yod dam med/ de yod na bu mo ster/ med na mi ster/ da lan song la dris la shog zer bas/ yang mgar gyis shog dril tha ma de rgyal po'i phyag tu phul nas/ 'phrin re la rgya bod
bar la 'gro mi 'ong / rgyal po khyed kyi gsung de'i lan 'di lags pas gzigs par zhu zhes zhus pas/ der rgyal pos kha phyes nas gzigs pas 'di ltar ro/ khyed rgya nag gi
rgyal po nor longs spyod yod/ nga bod kyi rgyal po la longs spyod de bzhin med de/ rgyal po khyed nor longs spyod yod pa la dgyes nas bu mo ster na/ ngas sku lus kyi bkod
pa lnga stong du sprul nas/ gser dngul gyi longs spyod/ 'bru dang / dar zab dang / gos dang / rgyan dang / zas kyi longs spyod rnams lha'i longs spyod la 'gran nus pa tsam
byed la/ gzhan yang phyogs bzhi nas las sgo re phyes nas/ khyed mtha'i nor rdzas thams cad kyang dbang med du nga'i sgo drung du 'du zhing / longs spyod dang ldan par
byed do| |de ngo mtshar mi che'am/ de ltar byas kyang lha gcig mi ster na/ ngas sprul pa'i dmag khri phrag lnga btang nas/ khyod gsod/ lha gcig phrogs/ yul khams thams cad
bcom la bzhag gi bya ba 'dug pas/ rgyal po de sngar bas kyang skrag par gyur te/ rgyal po de'i thugs la nga'i bu mo 'di 'dod mkhan mang yang / phugs su bod kyi rgyal po
'di la ster dgos pa 'dra bsam zhing / thugs ma bde bar pho brang du byon no/ /de nas yab rgyal po dang / yum btsun mo dang / sras rgyal bu dang / lha gcig rnams gros byas
pas/ yab na re/ chos rgya gar nas byung ba yin/ khong drin che bas rgya gar chos kyi rgyal po la ster gsungs so/ /yum ser sna che bas stag gzig nor gyi rgyal po la ster
zer ro/ /rgyal bu lus rtsal

bzang ba la dga' bas/ hor la ster zer ro/ /lha gcig rang skye gzugs legs pa la dga' bas/ mi tshe hril por 'grogs pa'i rten grogs gal che zer nas/ ge sar dmag gi rgyal po la
mos pa byung ngo / /der bod la dga' ba gcig kyang ma byung ngo / /der rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyed gnye bo rnams la nye ring med/ rig pa gang rno ba zhig la ster bas/ rig
pa 'gran zer ro/ /rgyal po de'i bla g.yu bzhag sgor mo bya ba/ che chung ni phub chung tshad tsam pa/ bkrag che ba/ mig gcig mtha' na yod pa/ mig gcig dkyil na yod pa/ nang
gi mig kyang phug gi spa rim lta bur yod pa de dang / dar yug gcig blon po tshan lnga po la gtad nas/ g.yu 'di'i mig tu dar yug 'di sus tshud pa la/ lha gcig ster zer
ro/ /der blon po gzhan rnams dbang che bas/ sngon la khong tshos g.yu khyer te| thabs sna tshogs byas nas/ nyi ma mang po lag 'grim gyis brgyus pas/ sus kyang ma tshud nas/
blon po mgar la gtad de/ nged rnams kyis nu ji ltar byas kyang ma tshud/ khyed rang e tshud ltos shig zer nas/ g.yu dar yug dang bcas pa gtad do/ /der mgar rig pa can
des/ sngar nas rgya'i grog ma gcig zan dang 'o mas gsos te/ mtheb mo tsam du song ba dang / de'i sked pa la dar skud btags te/ dar yug gi spyi bo bsdus nas btsim ste/ grog
ma de g.yu mig tu btsud do/ /dar g.yu de lag tu blangs nas phu btab pas/ rlung gis ded nas/ mtha'i mig tu thon byung ngo / /de nas grog ma'i rked pa nas dar skud dkrol
te/ nur gyis 'then pas/ g.yu mig tu dar yug tshud do/ /nged kyis 'di bzhin byung yod pas/ lha gcig zhu byas pas/ da rung rig pa 'gran no zer

nas/ bod la brnyas pa byas ma byin no/ /yang de'i sang lug lnga brgya gtad nas/ 'di rnams sang gi nyi ma la bsad zin pa/ bshas zin pa/ sha zos zin pa/ pags pa mnyes zin pa
la lha gcig ster zer ro/ /der bod blon rnams kyis mi res lug re bsad/ so sor bshas/ sha logs shig tu spungs/ pags pa logs shig tu spungs te/ sha lcung mo tsam re tshwa la
bsgres shing sgrin la skyur te/ zar bcug pas/ zos zin to/ /pags pa rnams gral mgo nas phur ba re byas btang bas/ gral gzhug tu snum byug ran par byung / yang 'og ma des
snum byug ste phur ba re byas pas gral mgor thul lo/ /gzhan ma rnams la bltas pas gang yang ma zin par 'dug go /nged kyi 'di bzhin byung yod/ gzhan gyis ma byung bar 'dug
pa/ lha gcig zhu'o byas pas/ da rung rig pa 'gran zer nas ma byin no/ /yang chang ben brgya gtad nas/ 'di rnams sang gi nyi ma phyed tshun la 'thung zin pa/ ma bor ba/ ma
bzi ba su byung ba la lha gcig ster zer ro/ /yang mgar gyis bod blon rnams la snod chung chung re btsug nyung re drangs te/ thog mar hub re 'thung cig byas pas/ 'thung
zin pa/ ma bo ba/ ma bzi ba byung nas/ gzhan rnams la bltas pas/ phor pa chen po chang gis bkang ste/ 'thung ma zin dogs nas khrog rgyab pas/ bzi zhing skyugs te bo 'dug
go /yang nged kyis 'di bzhin byung yod/ gzhan gyis ma byung bar 'dug pas/ lha gcig zhu'o byas pas/ da rung rig pa 'gran zer nas/ bod la brnyas pa byas ma byin no/ /yang rta
ma brgya/ bu brgya gtad nas/ 'di tsho ma bu phyogs gcig tu ngo shes pa la lha gcig ster zer ro/ /yang gzhan gyis ma shes/ mgar gyis rta ma bu rnams phyogs

gcig tu bzung nas zhag gcig tu rtswa byin cing chu ma byin no/ /de'i sang rte'u rnams kyi khrod du btang bas/ rang rang gi ma gang 'dug rtsa nas 'o ma 'thungs so| |der ngo
shes/ nged kyis ngo shes/ gzhan rnams kyis ma shes pas/ lha gcig zhu'o byas pas/ da rung rig pa 'gran zer nas ma byin no/ /yang de'i sang bya mo brgya bu brgya gtad nas/
'di rnams ma bu phyogs gcig tu sus ngo shes pa la lha gcig ster zer ro/ /yang gzhan gyis ma shes/ mgar gyis thang yangs cig la/ sbang ma gtor nas bzhag ste/ der bya rnams
kha gtad do/ /de gnyis gnyis lhan du zos so/ /skye'i 'og nas za zhing spyod pa 'tshub pa 'di rnams bu yin/ de min rnams ma yin no byas pas ngo shes/ nged kyis ngo shes/
gzhan gyis ma shes pas/ lha gcig zhu'o byas pas/ da rung rig pa 'gran zer nas ma byin no/ /yang gsam gyi shing ldum po brgyad gtad nas/ 'di rnams kyi mgo mjug sus shes pa
la ster zer ro/ /yang gzhan gyis ma shes so/ /mgar gyis shing de rnams chu 'gram du khyer nas chu la bskyur bas/ rtsa ba lji bas thur du song / rtse mo yang bas gyen du
lus so/ /nged kyis ngo shes/ gzhan gyis ma shes pas/ lha gcig zhu byas pas/ da rung rig pa 'gran zer nas ma byin no/ /der dgong cig pho brang nas rnga bo che brdung ba dang
/ blon po gzhan rnams pho brang du song / bod blon rnams kyi gnas mo de na re/ blon po gzhan rnams pho brang du song / khyed cag tsho yang mi 'gro'am/ phyin pa legs so
zer bas/ mgar na re/ nged la shog kyang mi zer/ rnga de ci yin cha med byas pas gnas mo na re/ blon po gzhan rnams song ba na/ khyed la shog mi zer kyang / 'gro ba yin mod
zer ro/ /

der blon pos rnga de la skyon can du go nas blon po rnams khrid/ sgo re re bzhin 'dren gin/ sgo la rams dang tshos kyi khu bas mtshan ma 'debs gin pho brang du phyin no/ /pho
brang na blon po gzhan rnams 'tshogs 'dug go /der rgyal pos/ do dgong blon po thams cad la ston mo zhig byas nas/ srod kyi mun nag la/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyed rang
blon po thams cad phyir song la/ rang rang gi khang pa rnyed pa gyis shig de sus rnyed pa la bu mo ster gsungs so/ /der mgar gyis pho brang nas mar me g.yar te/ sgo re re
bzhin 'den gin/ sngar gyi mtshan ma rnams bltas phyin pas/ rang gi khang pa rnyed do/ /sang nam langs pa dang / blon po gzhan rnams bltar phyin pas/ la la gzhan gyi khyim
du tshud/ la las sgo ma rnyed nas rgya srang na nyal 'dug go /yang mgar gyis nged kyi khang pa rnyed/ gzhan rnams kyis mi rnyed par 'dug lha gcig zhu'o byas pas/ rgyal
po'i zhal nas da ni zhag gsum gyi nyin shar sgo'i thang la/ bu mo mtshar sdug dang ldan pa sum brgya rgyan gyis brgyan nas gral byed/ de'i khrod du lha gcig 'jog pas/ de
ngo sus shes pa la bskur ba yin gsungs so/ /de nas mgar gyis gnas mo de dang lus 'brel shing mthun par byas/ zas chang gis mgo bskor te dga' ba'i gtam smras nas/ nged blon
po rnams kyis rgya nag tu sleb nas lo gcig 'gro/ rig pa de nged rno/ lha gcig 'di nged kyis thob pa la brnyas pa byas ma byin/ lha gcig 'phrul gyi kong jo 'di ma mthong
ba la sgra che ba g.yu 'brug sngon mo dang 'dra ba zhig 'dug lha gcig de dang khyod gnyis shin tu mthun par yod 'dug pas/ khyod kyis ci 'dra zhig legs par ston dgos/ da
ni shin tu gal che bar yod do//

da ni zhag gsum gyi nyin kong jo bu mo sum brgya'i dkyil du gral bsgrigs nas/ shar sgo'i thang la 'jog pas sur thob pa la ster ba yin gsungs te/ blon po gzhan rnams dbang che
bas sngon la kho tsho 'dom du 'ong / khong tsho gang rung gis ngo shes nas khyer las che/ nged kyi thob par dka'/ gal te khong tshos ngo ma shes par 'dug nas/ nged kyis
ngo shes na'ang / brnyas pa byas mi bskur las che/ gzhan yang las kyi dbang gis thob kyang / ci 'dra zhig yod ma shes pas/ khyod kyis legs par ston dgos/ ngas khyod rang
gi khyo byas la 'dir sdod/ lha gcig blon po gzhan ma rnams la bskur bas chog byas nas/ gser phye bre gang po de brngan pa la byin no/ /der gnas mo na re/ khyed bod blon
rnams bden/ rgyal pos nye ring che/ rgyal po gcig po min te/ khyed bod la dga' ba mi gcig kyang mi 'dug bod yi dwags kyi rgyal khams yin zer gyin 'dug lha gcig 'di blon
po gzhan rnams kyis thob tu re 'dug cing / khong tsho rig pa lan cig rno yang ster bar 'dug lha gcig 'phrul gyi kong jo 'di/ nga'i dpon mo yin pas rgyus nga che ste/ rgya
nag rtsis la mkhas pas/ rtsis kyis ngo shes na/ nga gsod 'ong bas/ ngas 'chad mi nus zer ro/ /der mgar na re/ rtsis kyis ngo mi shes pa'i thabs nga la yod zer nas/ khyim
gyi nang du sgo bsdams te/ sgyed po chen po gsum btsugs/ de'i steng du zangs chen po chus bkang ba gcig bzhag chu de'i steng du bya sna tshogs kyi spu gtor/ phub dmar po
zhig gis kha bcad/ de'i steng du gnas mo bzhag gnas mo'i mgo la rdza ma g.yogs/ rdza ma'i mgo la dra bas g.yogs/ rdza ma la bug pa phug bug pa dang dra mig gi nang du zangs
dung bcug

nas/ 'di nas tshur bshad pa'i rtsis kyis zin kyang yid ches mi 'byung bas/ khyod kyis legs par shod cig byas so/ /der gnas mo na re/ blon po chen po legs par yid la zungs shig
lha gcig 'phrul gyi kong jo de/ bu mo gzhan pas che rgyu med/ /skye gzugs gzhan pas legs rgyu med/ /rgyan gos gzhan pas bzang rgyu med/ /de la mo yi khyad chos ni/ /sku
mdog sngo la dmar ba'i mdangs chags pa zhig yod/ zhal nas utpal sngon po'i dri bro ba/ lus dri zhim pas g.yu'i sbrang ma gcig 'khor gin yod/ mkhur tshos g.yas pa'i steng
na cho lo ris/ g.yon pa'i steng na padma ris/ dpral ba'i dkyil na sindhu ra'i thig le'i steng na/ Arya tA ra nas tsam zhig yod/ so la so zho yod/ og ma la og zho yod/
lha gcig kong jo de/ bu mo sum brgya bsgrigs pa'i tha mar yang mi 'ong / dkyil du yang mi 'ong / g.yon gral nas bsgrigs pa'i drug gi gong du 'ong / lha gcig de lus dang gos
la gya bsrung ste/ lus dang gos la reg sa med pas/ mda' gsar pa zhig la dar leb rgan kha gang thogs la/ lha gcig gi rtsar sleb pa dang / mos dar gos sham bu lnga brtsegs
steng na dri ma lcam me ba zhig gon yod pas/ de'i gong ba nas mda'i ltong gis bzung la 'then cig zer ro/ /der mgar gyis/ chas de rnams bshig lus sems dga' bdes khyab par
gyur nas/ nged bod blon rnams sngon chad kyang mgo thon/ da rung mgo thon pa zhig dgos so/ /nged tshos rgya nag tu tshong la 'ongs pa yang min no/ /bshes gnyen skyong
du 'ong ba yang min no/ /lha gcig 'di spyan drongs na/ nged rnams mgo thon pa yin pas/ brtag pa legs po byed dgos so/ /da ni zhag gsum gyi nyin bu

mo sum brgya'i dkyil nas/ sus ngo shes pa la ster bar thag chod 'dug pas/ spyang glen ma nor ba zhig byed dgos zer ro/ /de nas zhag gsum gyi nyin par bu mo rgyan gyis brgyan
pa sum brgya shar sgo'i thang la bsgrigs so/ /rgya nag gi mi thams cad ltad mo la 'tshogs/ der rgyal po'i zhal nas/ blon po rnams sngar gyi go rim bzhin bdoms shig gsung
ngo / /der rgya gar chos kyi rgyal po'i blon po rnams byung ste/ gral gyi dkyil nas bu mo chas bzang zhing mdzes pa gnyis khrid nas gcig min kyang gcig yin te 'ong zer
nas/ 'u sgra dang bso sgra 'debs kyin song ngo / /de'i rjes la stag gzig nor gyi rgyal po'i blon po rnams byung ste/ bu mo mdzes ma gnyis khrid nas sngar ltar byas nas song
ngo / /de'i rjes la ge sar dmag gi rgyal po'i blon po rnams byung ste/ bu mo mdzes ma gnyis khrid nas/ snga ma ltar byas nas song ngo / /de'i rjes la bha ta hor gyi rgyal
po'i blon po rnams byung ste/ bu mo mdzes ma gnyis khrid nas snga ma ltar byas nas song ngo / /der blon po mgar gyis bltas pas/ de rnams thams cad min par shes te/ rab
tu dga' nas 'dzum mul gyis shor ro/ /der mgar gyis mda' de lag tu khyer/ bod blon rnams khrid de/ g.yon gral du gtad phyin nas/ gral gyi mtha' ma'i bu mo de la/ mgar na
re/ 'di ni bshan pa'i bu mo 'dra/ /lag pa 'di yi dmar lugs sam/ /de yi gong na 'dug pa de/ /rdza mkhan zhig gi bu mo 'dra/ /lag pa'i ser kha mang lugs sam/ /de yi gong na
'dug pa de/ /shing mkhan zhig gi bu mo 'dra/ /gos log 'di yi skya lugs sam/ /de yi gong na 'dug pa de/ khrab mkhan zhig gi bu mo 'dra/ /steng gos 'di yi snum lugs sam/
/de yi gong na

'dug pa de/ /phyis mkhan zhig gi bu mo 'dra/ /'breng bu 'di yi mang lugs sam/ /de yi gong na 'dug pa de/ /mgar ba zhig gi bu mo 'dra/ /gos kyi thu ba'i nag lugs sam/ /de yi
gong na 'dug pa de/ /dar 'thag bu mo yin pa 'dra/ / dar zab lus la gon lugs sam/ /de yi gong na 'dug pa de/ /lha gcig kong jo yin pa 'dra/ /sku mdog sngo la dmar mdangs
chags/ /zhal nas utpal sngon po mnam/ /dri zhim g.yu yi sbrang ma 'khor/ /mkhur tshos cho lo padma ris/ / dpral ba rje btsun sgrol mas mtshan/ /so tshags dam zhing so zho
can/ /'phrul chen bu mo gzhan bas mdzes/ /zhes pa la sogs pa'i yon tan brjod nas/ lha gcig gi gos kyi gong ba nas/ mda'i ltong gis bzung nas 'then pas/ lha gcig ngu zhing
blon po'i phyir 'brangs so/ /der lha gcig bshum pa la/ blon po mgar gyis spro ba bskyed pa'-i glu blangs te/ thon mi sambhoT dang / 'bri se ru gong ston gnyis kyis ram
bu bteg nas 'di skad do/ /e ma ngo mtshar che/ /lha gcig kong jo khyed/ /bdag gi tshig la gson/ /bkra shis nyams su dga'/ / bod kyi rgyal khams na/ /rin chen lnga las grub/
/rgyal po'i pho brang na/ /mi rje lha yis mdzad/ /srong btsan sgam po de/ /rigs gzugs dpal gyis brjid/ / mthong na sems yid 'phrog /thugs rje chen po lags/ /rgyal srid
chos bzhin bskyangs/ /'bangs rnams bka' la nyan/ /rgyal blon 'khor 'bangs rnams/ / dga' skyid glu ru len/ /chos kyi nyi ma shar/ /dpa' gyi sgron me bteg /ri la shing sna
tshang / /sa gzhi yangs pa la/ /'bru sna lnga yi tshogs/ /go mtshams med par skyes/ /gser dngul zangs lcags sogs/ /rin chen du ma yod/ /gnag

rta lug gsum rgyas/ /dga' skyid de ltar yod/ /e ma ngo mtshar che/ /lha gcig kong jo gson/ /zhes glu blangs pas/ lha gcig gi bsam pa la/ de ltar bden na nga rang gi yul dang
'dra bar 'dug bsams nas/ mchi ma phyis te/ blon po'i phyir 'brangs so/ /blon pos rta la bskyon te/ khrom bskor nas/ rgya hor gnyis las lhag pa nged bod yin/ lha gcig nged
kyis spyan 'dren pa yin pas/ thams cad khar mdzub mo chug la sdod byas so/ /der rgya nag gi mi rnams kyis smre sngags bton te/ nged kyi lha gcig mdzangs ma de/ bod ngan
pas khyer zer ro/ / der rgyal po'i zhal nas blon po gzhan rnams la'ang / khyed rnams kyang nged rgya nag pa'i gnyen zla yin pas/ khyed rang tshos 'doms pa'i bu mo rnams
khrid la/ so so'i yul la song shig gsung ngo / /der blon po mgar gyis lha gcig la/ da ni bod du 'gro thabs gyis shig byas nas btang ngo / /der lha gcig gis pho brang du
phyin pas/ yab rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyod bod kyi rgyal po'i btsun mor 'gro dgos gsungs pas/ lha gcig na re/ chos med pa/ yul ngan pa/ pha ming dang mi 'phrad pa'i sa thag
ring ba der nga mi 'gro zer/ yab kyi zhal nas/ khyod de skad ma zer 'gro dgos/ bod kyi rgyal po de mngon shes rdzu 'phrul mthu stobs dang ldan pa gcig yod par 'dug ngas
ji skad smras kyang / khos bod yul du ma phyin par/ lan yi ge'i nang du 'ong gin 'dug khyod mi 'gro ba khong gis shes nas/ dmag khri phrag lnga tsam 'dir byung nas/ nga
bsad/ khyod khyer/ yul mkhar thams cad bcom na ji tshug byed/ blon po de'i byed lugs la ltos dang / de bas phyin pa legs so gsungs pas/ der lha gcig gis yab la phyag 'tshal
te

gsol ba/ yab gcig rgyal pos bka' gnang ngam/ /a ma yum gyis gnang lags sam/ /jo jo ming pos tshig shor ram/ /e ma mi srid ngo mtshar che/ /bod kyi yul der bdag gtong na/ kha
ba can gyi yul phyogs der/ /bsil zhing grang la sa rong rtsub/ /lha klu 'dre srin gdug pa mang / /gangs ri gcan gzan mche ba 'dra/ /brag ri 'brong gi rwa dang 'dra/ /nyams
mi dga' zhing blo mi bde/ /'bru sna mi 'khrungs mu ge'i gnas/ /gdol pa sha zan srin po'i rigs/ /spyod pa rtsing ba kla klo'i mi/ /mtha' 'khob sangs rgyas zhabs ma bcags/
/chos med ma rig mun pa'i gling / /mchod pa'i rten dang gnas med cing / /bsod nams bsog pa'i rten med pas/ /de 'dra'i yul du 'gro dgos na/ /yab kyi mchod gnas yi dam
lha/ /shAkya mu ne bdag la zhu/ kha ba can ni bkres pa'i yul/ /rin chen bang mdzod bdag la zhu/ kha ba can ni bsil la grang / /tshe gcig dros pa'i gos cig zhu/ /bod ni gdol
