ba gtsang btsog med/ /g.yog mo'i skyo grogs bdag la zhu| |de ltar mtha' 'khob yul phyogs der/ /bod kyi mi dang 'grogs pa'i dus// bdag gis spyod lam ji ltar bya/ /zhes
mchi ma phyis nas zhus pas/ yab kyis thugs brtse ba'i bka' gnang ba/ nga yi mig dang 'dra ba'i bu mo khyod/ /bod ces bya ba kha ba can gyi yul/ /yul las khyad par 'phags
pa de yin te/ / gangs ri rang bzhin mchod rten grub pa'i gnas/ /mtsho bzhi g.yu yi maNDal bkram pa 'dra/ /ya mtshan gser gyi me tog rgyas pa'i gling / /bsil la mdzes pa lha
gnas gzhal yas khang / /chu bo bzhi 'bab shing rtsi nags kyis mdzes/ / 'bru sna lnga 'khrungs rin chen sna tshogs 'byung / /rkang bzhis kun khyab rtsi thog

mar la spyod/ /de ltar ngo mtshar che ba'i gnas mchog der/ /rin chen rgyan gyis mdzes pa'i pho brang na/ /mi rje lha yis mdzad pa'i rgyal po de/ /'phags pa thugs rje chen po
dngos su 'dug /thabs mkhas thugs rje ldan pa'i rgyal po yin/ /mi dge bcu spangs dge bcu'i khrims la gnas/ /mnga' thang dpal 'byor 'dod rgu'i dpal la spyod/ /yon tan mtha'
yas rgyal po lha yi sras/ / dpa' mdzangs kun 'dzom 'khor rnams byang chub sems/ /de 'dra'i gnas su bu mo khyod song shig /mdzes ma khyod kyi bsod nams bsags pa'i rten/
/ bdag gi mchod gnas ston pa'i sku gzugs 'di/ /yon bdag lha dbang brgya byin khong gis mdzad/ /rgyu ni rin chen rnam pa bcu las grub/ /'di yi bzo bo bi shwa karmas mdzad/
/rab gnas sangs rgyas nyid kyis mdzad pa lags/ /de ltar 'gran med rgyal ba'i sku gzugs 'di/ /mthong thos dran reg gsol ba btab gyur pas/ /sangs rgyas myur du thob par rgyal
bas gsungs/ /de ltar phan bde 'byung ba'i jo bo 'di/ /bdag gi snying dang 'dra bar phangs na yang / /mdzes pa'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzangs/ /rin chen bang mdzod
mang po nor gyi gter// bdag la gces pa'i rin chen mang po yang / /mdzes ma'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzangs/ /gser g.yu brtsegs pa'i yig tshang chen mo dang / /gtsug
lag yi ge sum brgya drug cu dang / /gser g.yu rgyan gyi rnam pa mang po yang / /mdzes pa'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzangs/ /g.yos sna zas kyi rnam pa mang po dang // btung
ba skom gyi sbyor thabs mang po dang / /gser sga g.yu yi ka leb can la sogs/ /mdzes pa'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzangs/ /za 'og stan thul seng

ge bya brgyad ma/ /ljon shing cho lo nor bu ris su bris/ /rgyal po ngo mtshar skye phyir khyod la brdzangs/ /rgya yi gab tse gtsug lag sum brgya po/ /legs nyes ston pa'i las
kyi me long yang / /mdzes pa'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzangs/ / bkod pa rig byed mdzes par byed pa yi/ /yid 'ong rgyan gyi khyad par 'phags pa dang / /bzo'i rig byed
drug cu tham pa yang / /mdzes pa'i bu mo khyod la bdag gis brdzangs/ /bzhi brgya rtsa bzhi'i nad rnams 'joms pa'i sman/ / brtag thabs brgya dang dpyad lnga spyad drug dang
/ /sbyor sde bzhi la sogs pa bdag gis bskur/ /tshe gcig dros pa'i dar gos za 'og sogs/ kha dog sna tshogs ldan pa'i rgyan gos kyang / /stong phrag nyi shu bu mo khyod
la brdzangs/ / rigs gzugs lta na sdug cing mdzes pa yin/ /sems mthun skyo grogs byed pa'i bu mo yang / /nyi shu rtsa lnga khyod kyi 'khor du brdzangs/ /e ma 'bral bar mi
phod bu mo khyod/ /brtse ba'i snying gtam yin pas sems la zhog kha ba can gyi mi rnams 'dul don du/ khyod kyis bya ba spyod lam 'di bzhin gyis/ /lta ba yangs shing spyod
lam zhib bar mdzod/ /phyi nang bya ba kun la mkhas par mdzod/ /ngag 'jam smra mkhas gzhi ma legs par mdzod/ /rje la gus shing 'khor la byams par mdzod/ khrel yod ngo tsha
bag dang ldan par mdzod/ /ces pa la sogs pa'i 'jig rten mi chos la dgos pa'i bslab bya dpag tu med pa mdzad do/ /yab kyis phyag nas 'jus shing 'bral mi phod pa ltar yod
na yang / bod du 'gro dgos par dgongs te/ lha gcig la rdzong bsam gyis mi khyab pa mdzad do/ /de nas lha gcig g.yog mo de dang 'grogs te/ blon po mgar gyi rtsar byung nas/

blon po chen po khyed kyi yul du jo bo shAkya yang gdan 'dren/ nor dpag tu med pa'ang khyer nas khyed kyi yul du 'gro/ khyed kyi yul na sa kham pa yod dam/ rdo srin zan yod
dam/ shing se ba yod dam/ rtsa dred ma yod dam/ nyung ma yod dam/ zer ba la/ mgar na re/ gzhan rnams yod/ nyung ma med byas nas/ la nyung gi sa bon khyer/ de nas shing rta'i
'khor lo byas/ de'i steng du jo bo shAkya bzhugs/ 'khor lo de rgya nag na stobs che ba'i gyad lha dga' dang / klu dga' gnyis la 'dren du bcug go /gzhan yang rin po che
dang / dar dang gos dang / rgyan dang / 'phral gyi yo byad rnams bkal ba'i rta dang / dre'u rnga mo la sogs pa mang po brdzangs so/ /bod blon rnams la'ang ston mo gnang
sbyin dpag tu med pa mdzad do| |der lha gcig kong jo yang rin po che'i rgyan mang pos brgyan nas/ mdzes pa'i bu mo nyi shu rtsa lnga'i 'khor dang bcas pa rang rang gi rta
la chibs nas/ yab yum blon po'i tshogs dang bcas pas skyel thung byas/ yab yum gnyis kyi thugs la 'phreng bzhin du/ 'jig rten mi chos la phan pa'i bslab bya gal che ba
dpag tu med pa mdzad nas bod du chas so/ /der skyel thung la byon pa'i gral la/ blon po 'bri se ru gong ston zer ba des/ blon po mgar la phrag dog byas nas/ 'dir lha gcig
gi tshab tu/ blon po rig pa can cig bsdad na/ rgya bod gnyis mthun 'ong zer nas/ blon po mgar la mig cer te bltas pa dang / rgyal po'i zhal nas nga'i lha gcig mdzangs ma
de/ khyed bod kyis thob pas nga la mi tshab tu mgar sdod dgos gsungs so/ /der blon po mgar gyis kyang / se ru gong ston gyis phrag dog byas par go nas/ rgya bod gnyis mthun
pa ngas byed do zer nas

sdod par byas so/ /der mgar gyis thon mi dang nyang gnyis zur du khrid nas/ nga rgya nag tu zla ba lnga las mi sdod/ de'i bar ngan 'khyol tshad skyel/ khyed rnams kyis rdzus
ma'i sprang po cig nga'i rtsar thong byas so/ /der blon po thams cad jo bo dang lha gcig la bskor te bod du song ngo / /der rgya nag tu mgar gcig pur lus te/ rgyal pos
mgar la bud med cig blangs/ gzhi ma rab cig phog nas bzhag go /de nas mgar yang shin tu skyo zhing / blo ma bde bar gyur nas bud med de'i rtsar ma phyin/ lto yang ma zos
te/ lus sngo la rid par byas/ mal 'og tu ko ba rul pa bzhag nas/ lus la dri mi zhim pa yod pa byas/ 'gram pa g.yas su mtshal bcug g.yon du rams bcug nas/ mal gyi phyi rol
rnag khrag gi lud pas bkang ste bzhag go /der chung ma rgya mo de na re/ blon po chen po khyed kyi lus la dri mi zhim pa yang snom gyin 'dug mdog kyang sngo bar 'dug pa
ci nyes zer ro/ /blon po na re/ nga la tshad pa'i nad byung ba khyod kyis ma tshor ram zer bas/ der mos rgyal po la zhus pas/ rgyal po yang thugs ma bde bar/ blon po'i rtsar
byon te/ blon po chen po ci byung gsungs pas/ blon po na re/ bdag tshad pa'i nad kyis thebs gda' lags zer nas lud pa cig bskyur bas rnag khrag gi mdog tu 'dug lus kyi
dri mi zhim pa yang tshor te/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ sang sman pa mkhas pa zhig yod pa khrid la 'ong gis gsungs nas bzhud do| |der chung ma rgya mo de la/ blon po na re/ khyod
bud med grib che/ sang sman pa byung tsa na/ nga'i rtsa mi rtogs pas/ khyed rang khyim mtshes gyi gan du nyol bar song zhig byas nas gtong ngo / /de'i shul du/ blon
pos sa phag gi khri mthon po cig

brtsigs nas/ gdung ma la thi gu btags/ pho mtshan thi gus bcings te/ spyi bo sa la btsugs nas rtsa thams cad 'khrug tu bcug go /de'i sang rgyal pos sman pa khrid byung ste/
sman pa mkhas pa des rtsa bltas pas/ sman pa na re/ lus kyi rtsa thams cad 'khrugs par gyur pas na brtag par dka' ste/ rlung las gyur pa yang ma yin/ mkhris pa las gyur
pa yang ma yin/ bad kan kyang ma yin/ 'dus pa'ang min te/ byis pa'i gdon chen bco brgyad kyi nad kyang ma yin/ bgegs rigs stong phrag brgyad cu'i nad kyang ma yin te/ 'byung
po'i gdon gyi nad kyang ma yin/ sems ma bde ba snying gi dkyil du phog pa'i gcong cig 'dra te/ sman dpyad rim gro gang gis kyang phan par dka' zer ro/ /der rgyal po'i
zhal nas/ sman pa de la sang gnang lan re shog la ltos shig gsungs so/ /yang sang sman pa byung dus/ blon pos mchan du zhim bu bcug de'i lag pa la thi gu btags/ thig sna
la rtsa bltar bcug pas/ gcan gzan tha ma zhig gi rtsa las mi 'dug zer te song ngo / /yang blon pos/ de'i sang bya pho cig mchan du bcug nas/ de'i lag pa la thi gu btags/
thig sna la rtsa bltar bcug pas/ 'dab chags tha ma zhig gi rtsa las mi 'dug zer ro/ /de nas rgyal po yang thugs shin tu ma bde bar/ blon po chen po khyed rang rig pa can
yin pas thabs e yod/ de'i thabs gang 'grub byed gsungs pas/ blon po'i bsam pa la/ da ni glags rnyed par 'dug bsams nas/ rgyal po chen po nga'i nad 'di khyed kyis nga bzung
bas/ bod kyi lha srungs ma dga' ba yin/ nga bod kyi ri mthong ba'i ri mtho ba zhig gi khar phyin nas lha gsol na phan/ de'i rdzas la/ dar zab bsregs pa'i thal ba

rkyal pa gang / lug bsad pa'i mcher pa'i khrag grod pa gang / sol ba'i mdung shing gas chag med pa 'dom gsum/ rta mog ro mgo dmar ba zhig rnams dgos/ de rnams ni rnyed par
dka' ste mi 'dzom/ rgyal po yang gsan par dka'/ lar deng nga 'chi las che/ shi bas mi chog par nga'i rjes su ltas ngan pa bco brgyad 'ong / rgya bod gnyis 'brel chad/ bod
kyi rgyal po la mngon shes yod pas nga shi ba mkhyen nas/ dmag btang nas/ rgya yul thams cad phung bar 'ong / sa thag ring sa 'dir sleb/ grogs blon po rnams kyis bskyur/
lus la nad kyis thebs/ nga rang gi rgyal po dang / nye du mdza' bshes rnams yid la dran kyang bya thabs med par song / rang gi nor rdzas bza' btung longs spyod kyis phan
par dka' ste/ tshe 'di yang rmi lam lta bur 'dug go zer nas/ mgo hril gyis gtum nas nyal song ngo / /der rgyal po yang shin tu skrag par gyur nas/ khyed la phan pa'i thabs
gang 'grub byed/ lhod de nyol cig gsung nas bzhud do// der rgyal pos nags thams cad la me brgyab pas/ sol ba'i mdung shing kyang ma byung / dar zab thams cad bsregs pas/
thal ba rkyal pa phyed kyang ma byung / lug thams cad bsad pas mcher khrag phor pa phyed kyang ma byung / rta mog ro mgo dmar de rnyed do/ /der rgyal po'i zhal nas/ rdzas
gzhan rnams ni ma rnyed/ rta mog ro mgo dmar de rnyed yod do gsungs pas/ blon po na re/ rdzas gzhan rnams ma rnyed na thabs zad/ rta mog ro mgo dmar la nga'i ro rta gyis
la nga bskyon/ rgya yul na bzang ba'i rta zhig la nga'i ro zas dang / ro gos bkal nas bod kyi ri mthong ba'i sar lha gsol du 'gro'o zer ro/ /der lha gsol bar

'gro ba'i grabs byed gin yod tsa na/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ blon po chen po nam zla dpyid kar song / so nam byed ran pas ji ltar byas na legs/ khyod rig pa can yin pas ston cig
gsungs so/ /der blon po na re/ nga'i bod yul na sa bon thams cad sla nga'i nang du ser tsam brngos nas btab pas/ lo tshan che ba/ gzugs ring ba/ zla ba gsum song dus smin
'ong zer bas/ der rgyal po'i zhal nas/ bod kyi lugs su gyis shig gsungs nas/ khrims kyi rnga bo che brdungs te/ thams cad kyis nas brngos nas yos zhing la btab bo/ /der
blon pos rang gi lus gud pa de sos/ lha gsol bar 'gro ba'i grabs byed gin yod dus/ bod blon rnams kyis rdzus ma'i sprang po gcig btang byung ngo / /der blon pos log pa'i
skad byas te/ thag ring gi ra pho rgya bo la ngo shes mi bya'o/ kha rog sdod la ku co thong / /nag mo lcags mkhar thug nas yod/ /lung pa phu brdug mda' brdugs su/ /thu
ru co brags khong la zhog /dar dkar dril la dar nag bskyod// zla bas nyi ma'i rtsa ru sleb/ /zer nas/ der sprang po de log go /sprang po des khong rnams la bshad pas ma
go bar/ rgya mo kong jos go nas 'di skad zer te/ blon po des rgya nag tu ngan chen po byas yod par 'dug thag ring gi ra pho rgya bo la ngo shes ma byed zer ba de/ khong rang
rgyal po sma ra can la lab ma shod bya ba yin/ da len kha rog sdod la/ bod blon rnams la shod bya ba yin/ nag mo lcags mkhar thugs nas yod zer ba de/ sa bon yos su brngos
nas 'debs bcug bya ba yin/ lung pa phu brdugs mda' brdugs su/ thu ru co brags khong la zhog bya ba de/ dong par mda' mang po chug bya ba yin/ dar dkar dril la dar

nag bskyod bya ba de/ nyin mo bsdad gin mtshan mo 'ong zer ba yin/ zla bas nyi ma'i rtsar sleb zer ba de/ ngas khyed rnams kyi rtsar mgyogs par sleb bya ba yin zer ro/ /der
blon po mgar bod kyi ri mgo mthong ba'i sar lha gsol du 'gro ba'i chas la rta mog ro mgo dmar la zhon/ rta gzhan zhig la rgyags dang gos bkal/ sha skam la tshwa chu byugs
pa mang po khyer/ rgyal pos blon po bod du bros dogs nas/ gyad mi bzhi bsrung du btang ngo / /der mgar med pa'i shul du/ rgyal po na re/ nga'i lha gcig de ston mkhan zhig
yod thag chod pas/ rtsis gyis shig gsungs so/ /der rtsis byas pas 'di skad zer/ ri gsum gyi steng na mtsho chen po cig 'dug mtsho de'i nang na bya sna tshogs 'dug de'i
steng na thang dmar cem me ba zhig gi kha na/ bud med yin pa la mgo dang lus mnyam pa/ mgo lus thams cad mig gis gang ba/ zangs kyi mchu yod pa zhig gis bstan 'dug zer bas/
rgyal po thugs ma ches par rtsis yig thams cad me la bsregs/ spor thang brgyad cu skor ni bod du bskur nas med do/ /der blon po bod kyi ri mthong ba'i sa ru sleb/ lkog
tu chang mang po nyos nas sbas/ sha skam kyang zhim po byin nas/ nga'i nad la phan pa yin pas zo cig byas te/ lha gsol lo| |de nas gyad bzhi pos kha skom nas bzod thabs
med par byung ba dang / chang mang po byin pas/ khong rnams ra ro ste dbang po med par gyur pa dang / blon pos khong bzhi po'i rta'i sug pa brags/ mtshon cha bcag khong
rang rta mog ro mgo dmar la zhon/ rta gzhan de khrid nas 'di skad zer ro/ /dar zab me la bsregs pa'i thal ba de/ /rgyal po nye ring can de'i na bza' mdzod/ /snye ma 'bru

med thal ba nag po de/ /btsun mo ser sna can de'i rgyags phye mdzod/ /nags la me brgyab sol ba'i mdung shing de/ /rgyal bu lus rtsal can de'i mdung shing mdzod/ /lug la mcher
khrag med par bsad pa de/ /lha yi drung du sdig bshags smon lam bya/ /lus la nad med mal du nyal ba la/ /sngas mgor sman pa bos nas ci zhig bya/ kho bo mi sdod rang gi
yul du 'gro/ /zer te/ rta la lcag brgyab ste song ngo / /der rgya yul du snye nag mo shar ba dang / rgya rnams na re/ snye ma'i nang na 'bru mi 'dug blon po ngan pa des/
dar zab thams cad bsreg tu bcug lug thams cad gsod du bcug nags thams cad la me brgyab/ sa bon thams cad brngos su bcug nas btab pas/ da ni 'bru mi 'dug lha gcig mdzangs
ma de bod kyis khyer/ jo bo shAkya ni bod kyis gdan drangs/ ngan 'di tsam zhig byas/ kye ma kye hud da ni ji ltar bya/ da kho 'dir 'ong ba mi srid do/ / bod du bros pa srid
zer ba'i gtam rgyal po'i snyan du thos so/ /de bden par nges sam snyam nas/ rgya'i rta pa rtsal che ba brgya tham pa 'dzin du btang ngo/ /der gyad bzhi po yang bzi sangs
te 'di snyam du bsam mo/ /rta zhon rgyu med/ mtshon cha yang mi 'dug yul du log na ngo tsha la/ rgyal po'i chad pa yang byung dogs nas/ blon po'i phyir 'brangs so/ /der
rgya chu khug pa'i rtsar sleb dus/ rgya nag gi 'ded mi rnams kyis kyang nye bar sleb bo/ /der blon pos gyad bzhi po bran du bskul nas/ rgya chu khug pa'i 'gram du rta'i
sbangs dang / rta rjes kyi bkang / gna' ba'i rwa me la bsos nas/ gzhu bcos/ gyad bzhi po gda' rgyag bcug pas/ mda' sgro mtshams bar phud bzhag go /de rnams 'ded mis mthong
nas

'di skad zer te/ kho la bsu ba'i rta pa mang la rtsal che ba byung 'dug nged rang rnams kyis mi thub/ log pa 'thad zer te/ de nas log go /de'i bar la rgya mo bza' la sogs pa'i
bod blon rnams kyis ldan ma brag rtsar phebs nas/ brag la byams pa khru bdun pa zhig dang / bzang spyod gnyis brkos mar bzhengs/ der zla ba gcig bsgug der yang blon po
ma byon/ phung po ri la phyag phebs/ la la 'phred lam bcos/ ri dwags bzung nas 'o ma bzhos/ der yang blon po ma byon/ khams kyi padma shang du chag phebs/ zhing btab/ rang
thag chu bskor btsugader zla ba gnyis bsgug der yang blon po ma byon/ de nas sgo dong sgo mo'i rtsar phebs/ rgya nag gi phywa g.yang nyams pas/ rgya nag gi lha srung
rnams kyi mthus sgo mo 'gags pas der zla ba gnyis lus/ der blon po slebs so/ /de nas sgo dong sgo mo 'gags pa de/ rgya nag gi lha srung ma dga' bas lan par shes nas/ shing
sna'i dud pa chen po btang / zas chang gi phud gtor nas 'di ltar byas so/ / gsol lo gsol lo lha la gsol/ /rgya nag rgyal po'i lha la gsol/ /grong khyer zim shi'i lha la
gsol/ /rgya rje btsan po'i lha la gsol/ /bkra shis khri sgo'i lha la gsol/ /nags ma gyen la long du gsol/ /bod blon rnams kyi lha la gsol/ kha ba can pa'i lha la gsol/ /rgya
mo kong jo bsu ru shog /ces gsol mchod di ri ri byas pa'i nub mo nags thams cad gyen la langs te 'gro thub pa byung ngo / /de nas bye ma'i la dgu 'khyags kha bskor/
mun pa'i rum du mar me bteg seng ldeng gi nags ma g.yas su longs/ gla ba'i nags ma g.yon du longs/ bod du gegs med par sleb byung ngo / /de nas rgyal po'i drung du bang

chen pa btang ste/ 'di ltar nged blon po rnams kyis/ jo bo shAkya dang / lha gcig kong jo la sogs pa gdan drangs nas sleb gin yod pas/ bsu ba dga' ston rgya chen po zhu zhus
so/ /der rgyal po'i zhal nas/ 'phags pa sgrol ma'i sprul pa lha gcig de yin par 'dug pas 'phrul che bas/ phyogs gang nas 'ong ngo mi shes pas/ bsu ba legs po gyis shig
gsungs so/ /der phyogs bzhi kha ru mthong snang gi sprul par byung ste/ shar phyogs pa rnams na re/ lha gcig ni shar phyogs nas byon/ de'i rgyu rkyen/ rab kyi ming kyang
rgya mo rab bya ba yod zer/ lho phyogs pa rnams na re/ lha gcig ni lho phyogs nas byon te/ grib kyi phu'i 'khyag rom la/ dung dkar g.yas su 'khyil ba 'dra zer ba de dus byung
zer/ nub phyogs pa rnams na re/ lha gcig ni nub phyogs nas byon te/ sbal pa tshal gyi brag la phag pa'i sna 'dra bas/ mgon po zhig bzhengs zer ba de dus yin zer/ byang
phyogs pa rnams na re/ lha gcig ni byang phyogs nas byon te/ lha gcig dang jo bo la bsu pa byas pas grong gi ming kyang lha bsu ba bya bar yod zer don dam par byang phyogs
sgo la nas byon nas/ ra mo che'i thang la phebs so/ /der ra mo cher shing rta bye ma la bying nas/ gyad lha dga' dang klu dgas ma drongs par lus so| |der jo bo'i phyogs
bzhir ka ba bzhi btsugs/ dar dkar gyi yol bas bres nas mchod pa byas so/ /de'i sang nyin lha gcig kong jo dar sna tshogs kyi gos gon/ gser g.yu'i rgyan du mas brgyan
nas/ mdzes ma'i bu mo nyi shu rtsa lnga yang dar zab dang / rin po che'i rgyan sna tshogs kyis brgyan/ pi wang rol mo dang bcas te/ brag lha'i ne'u thang la gzigs mo la phebs
so/ /der blon po bod

'bangs thams cad ltad mo la 'tshogs nas/ glu gar rtsed mo bsam gyis mi khyab pa byas so/ /der brag lha bkra shis kyi gzhal yas khang rtse nas/ bal mo bzas gzigs pas/ rgya mo
bza' dpon g.yog rnams rgyan du mas brgyan pa/ brag lha'i ne'u thang la 'dug pa mthong / chags sdang gi phrag dog bsam gyis mi khyab pa zhig skyes nas 'di skad zer ro/ /kye
ma rgya mo kong jo khyod/ /de na g.yog 'khor bcas te 'dug /dka' las byas te snye bos bkug /sa thag ring kyang bod du sleb/ /rgya rje'i sras mo yin lags kyang / /nga dang
khyod gnyis khyad par che| |nga ni them pa snga brgal yin/ /bal rje'i sras mo nga yang yin/ /rje yi sku mthong nga snga bas/ /chen ma che rgyu btsun rgyu yin/ /chen ma
mi che mi btsun na/ / 'jig rten chos lugs mi bden rdzun/ /chen ma rgyal po'i btsun mo yin/ /chun ma btsun mo'i g.yog mo yin/ /'on kyang rje la bsam nas 'ongs/ /chen chun
gnyis po 'gran no ang / /dkon mchog dbu 'phang bstod par 'gran/ /chos dang dkon mchog bzhugs pa'i gzhi/ /gtsug lag khang rnams bzhengs par 'gran/ /yar la rje yi zhabs tog
'gran/ /mar la ngan long skyong ba dang / /dad pas dam chos byed par 'gran/ /thad kar skal nor bsog pa dang / /zhing la so nam byed par 'gran/ /yul gyi pha ming che chung
dang / /rang la skal brdzangs ci yod 'gran/ /de rnams 'gran par ma nus na/ khyod kyang rje la ma reg zhig / btsun mo'i rang mthong ma che zhig /chen ma che rgyu'i lha
khang ni/ /bre tshad tsam zhig ma brtsigs par/ /chun ma chung rgyu'i lha khang ni/ /phul tshad tsam yang ma brtsigs shig /zer ba dang / rgya mo bza'i bsam pa la/ lar skyon
che/ rang gi pha ming

dpal 'byor longs spyod rnams rgyab tu bskyur/ yul thag ring nas 'ongs/ sleb ma thag yin pa/ sdod pa'i gnas ma rnyed/ bsten pa'i sa ma rnyed/ rgyal po'i zhal ma mthong / btsun
mo'i ming ma thob/ phyi nang gi blon po rnams dang ma 'dris pa'i gang 'dir/ phrag dog gi 'gran tshig 'di bzhin byed pa 'dra mo min/ nged rang gnyis ka sa thag ring nas/
rgyal po'i btsun mo la 'dir lhan du 'dzom/ gcig snying gcig la gtad skyid sdug bsres nas/ blo sems gcig tu dril te rje'i zhabs tog 'bangs kyi skyong bran/ chen chun gyi
'grogs lugs/ phyi nang gi bya ba kun la thob rim bzhin byas na/ tshe 'di'i spun dang 'dra ste/ de bzhin med par sleb ma khad/ phrag dog gi 'gran tshig 'di bzhin yin na/
nged rang gnyis pha ming / skal brdzangs rang sgo/ 'jig rten gyi bya ba/ gang dang spyi rnams ci'i phyir mi mnyam bsams te/ lan smras pa/ e ma ngo mtshar che ste dgod re
bro/ kho mos sdod pa'i gnas kyang ma rnyed cing / /rkang pa gnyis kyis them pa ma brgal bar/ /rje yi zhal yang mig gis ma mthong bar/ /btsun mo khyed kyi 'gran tshig sngas
pa yin/ /'dab chags mkha' la lding ba'i rtse sgro dang / /rlan drod sa la skyes pa'i smyug ma gnyis/ /rang cha dgos pa'i go gnas mnyam lags kyang / / las kyi dbang gis
mda' mkhan rtsa ru 'dzom/ /steng 'og byung ba ming gi khyad par yin/ /phu gsum spang la skyes pa'i me tog dang / /mda' gsum ldum rar skyes pa'i ha lo gnyis/ /mtshar sdug
blta ba'i cha nas mnyam lags kyang / /rten 'brel dbang gis lha yi drung du 'dzom/ /snga rting byung yang ming gi khyad par yin/ / bal yul mthil nas byung ba'i khri btsun
dang / /bu mo rgya nas long ba'i kong jo

gnyis/ /pha ming skal brdzangs thams cad mnyam lags kyang / /smon lam dbang gis rgyal po'i drung 'dir 'dzom/ /chen chun byung ba ming gi khyad par yin/ / snyan dan tshag pa
mo dang chen chun sogs/ /mthun por 'grogs na tshe 'di'i spun las lhag /chags sdang byed na rang mgo su drung yin/ /rgya dang bal yul sa thag ring ba na/ /yab gcig rgyal
po gnyis ni so sor bzhugs/ /yul gyi pha ming ngom na'ang 'gran pas chog /phan bde'i dge legs thams cad 'byung ba'i gzhi/ /mthong thos dran reg yon tan bsam mi khyab/ /jo
bo rnam gnyis ngom na'ang 'gran pas chog /rin chen gser dngul dar zab sna tshogs dang / /rta dang rnga mo drel la sogs pa yi/ /rang gi skal brdzangs ngom na'ang 'gran pas
chog /'jig rten bya ba bzo'i rnam 'gyur dang / /rgyan gyi bkod pa zas kyi g.yos sna dang / /phyi yi so nam bkal thag yon tan sogs/ /mdzangs ma'i lag rjes ngom na'ang 'gran
pas chog /ces zer ro/ /der blon po mgar gyis kyang / rgya nag rgyal pos nye ring byas pa/ lha gcig kong jos bod la log lta byas pa/ rgya yul du dka' las chen po byung
ba rnams yid la dran te/ zla ba gcig ma lon bar du/ kong jo dpon g.yog rnams la 'khor mkhan mi gcig kyang med pa byas so/ /der rgya mo'i 'khor rnams na re/ bod yi dwags kyi
rgyal khams yin zer ba bden par 'dug bza' btung longs spyod ni mi 'ong bar 'dug zer ro/ /de thos pa dang / rgya mo bza' yang sems la bzod thabs ma byung bar blon po mgar
bos/ blon po chen po khyed rang ji ltar gsungs pa la brten nas 'ong ba yin pa/ khyi bos nas ma brdung / khrel med gdong chung mi byed

par/ nged dpon g.yog rnams la brgyags dang gos skyol/ nged rnams sa thag ring nas sleb pa yin pas nyon mongs par yod par byas pas/ mgar na re/ nga la zas skom skyel ba'i dbang
yang med/ ci byed bal mo bza' dbang che ba yin/ khyed rang mo la de skad zhus zer te/ kho log song ngo / /der rgya mo bza' yang yi chad/ yul gyi pha ming dang longs spyod
rnams yid la dran te/ 'gyod kyang bya thabs med par song nas/ pi wang la ram 'degs bcol nas glu blangs so/ / bu mo mi sdod yul la 'gro/ /jo bo shAkya rdzongs su byon/
/gtsug lag rtsis kyang rdzongs su byon/ /rin chen dar zab rdzongs su khyer/ /'o ma zho ru bsgyur gin 'ong / /zho la mar du 'don gin 'ong / /da ra thud du bsgyur gyin 'ong
/ /se ba zhib par 'thag gin 'ong / /gres ma thag par 'chos kyin 'ong / kham pa rdza ru bsgyur gyin 'ong / /rang 'thag chu bskor 'dzugs kyin 'ong / /nyung ma'i sa bon khyer
nas 'ong / /rgya nag yul du phywa g.yang nyams/ /bod du bde skyid phun sum tshogs/ /bu mo a ma'i go na mdzangs/ /go rgas sems kyi nad du che/ /bod kyi yul du khyim la
'ong / khyi mo nang du bos nas brdung / /bod la khrel gdong mi 'dug go /gri chung yu ba'i rtsa na rno/ /glu chung rang 'thag go na snyan/ /bu mo a ma'i go na mdzangs/ /rje
kha blon pos bsgyur gyin gda'/ /skyes kha mo yis bsgyur gyin gda'/ /thag kha spun gyis bsgyur gyin gda'/ /zhing ngan ram pas bsgyur gyin gda'/ /bu mo nga la sdod thabs
med/ /blon po mgar gyis khrel med byas/ /zhes zer te/ jo bo shing rta'i steng du bzhugs/ rta dang drel rnga mo la sogs la khal bkal/ bod ngan pa'i bya ba mthong bas shes
zer te/ 'gro ba'i

grabs byas dus blon po mgar byung nas/ khyed khyim nas pha ming gi yul du log pa mi 'thad/ ngo yang tsha/ rgya yul du 'gro ba'i lam yang mi shog bod du 'ong dus kyang nga med
par lam du lus 'dus nas lam ma shog par 'dug pa/ da ngas bal mo bza' la'ang gros 'debs/ rgyal po la'ang zhu shig zer te/ khos mjal bar zhus nas/ rgyal po dga' ston gyi
gdan sar byon te/ rgya mo bza' kong jo dang mjal lo/ /der yang mthong lugs rnam par gsum du byung ste/ phyogs bcu'i de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyi snang ba la/ rgyal po dang
/ btsun mo gnyis mdzad pa bcu gnyis kyi tshul gyis sems can gyi don byed pa'i snang ba byung ngo / /sa bcu'i byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi snang ba la/ 'phags pa spyan
ras gzigs rgyal po srong btsan sgam por skur sprul/ rje btsun ma sgrol ma rgya mo bza' kong jo ru skur sprul nas sems can gyi don byed pa'i snang ba byung ngo / /mi nag
tha mal pa rnams kyi snang ba la/ rgyal po dang btsun mo gnyis skyems la gsol res byed pa dang / skud pa 'khel res byed pa'i snang ba byung ngo / /de nas rgyal po yang kong
jo dang zla ba gcig gi bar la ma mjal ba des/ thugs shin tu 'gyod par gyur nas/ kong jo'i sems gso ba'i phyir/ kong jo khyod 'o ma brgyal lam/ nyon ma mongs sam/ bar
chad med par bod du slebs pa ngo mtshar che| jo bo ji ltar byas la gdan drangs/ la 'phrang chu gsum la ji ltar byas gsungs/ lha gcig kong jo na re/ jo bo shAkya shing rta'i
steng du bzhugs/ gyad lha dga' dang / klu dgas 'khor los drangs/ brgya chu khug pa gru yis bcad/ lam sa thag ring yang thabs kyis byon/ bye ma'i la dgu 'khyags kha bskor
nas 'ong /

mun pa'i rum du mar me bteg nas 'ong / seng ldeng gi nags ma g.yas su bsgyel nas 'ong / gla ba'i nags ma g.yon du bsgyel nas 'ong / rgya nag yul du phywa g.yang nyams/ /bod
du bde skyid phun sum tshogs/ /bod la khrel gdong mi 'dug go /zer te bshums so/ /der yang blon po tshos sleb tsa na/ shags che/ yus che ba byas te/ blon po mgar na re/ spyir
rgya nag gi mi thams cad kyis brnyas pa byas/ gnas mo rgya mo gcig min pa/ sems mkhan mi gcig kyang ma byung / sgos su rgya nag rgyal pos nye ring chen po byas/ lha
gcig kong jo khyed rang yin kyang bod la mi dga' ba ji tsam byas zer bas/ der rgya mo bza' skyengs te smra rgyu ma byung ngo / /rgya mo bza' kong jo gdan drangs pa'i le'u
ste bcu gsum pa'o// //bcu bzhi pa/ mtha' 'dul yang 'dul gyi lha khang dang / 'phrul snang ra mo che rnams legs par bzhengs pa'i skor/ de nas lha gcig khri btsun gyis/ rgya
mo bza' rtsis la mkhas par shes nas blon po mgar la ngo chen bcol te/ g.yog mo la gser phye bre gang yon du bskur nas/ lha khang brtsigs pa'i sa cha gang bzang brtsi ba
la btang ngo / /der rgya mo bzas kyang spor thang brgyad cu skor gyi gab rtse bting nas brtsis pas/ kha ba can bod kyi rgyal khams 'di/ srin mo gan rkyal du nyal ba'i gzugs
su shes/ 'o thang gi mtsho 'di srin mo'i snying khrag tu shes/ ri gsum po 'di snying gi rus par shes/ sa cha 'di srin mo'i snying thog rang du 'dug pas/ mtsho 'di bsubs
pa'i steng du lha khang 'di brtsig dgos/ 'di na ngan song gi sgo zhig kyang 'dug ra mo che'i 'og na klu'i pho brang 'dug ste/

jo bo bzhugs pa 'dis non par 'dug go /klu phug na klu bdud nag po'i nyal sa 'dug pa lha khang brtsigs la phrogs shig lho nub zla ba tshal gyi dug shing gi sdong po rkang gcig
gi rtsa ba na the'u rang dang / mi ma yin gyi 'dus sa yod pa gtor cig grib kyi phu nas nyang bran phu ru/ btsan gyi rgyu srang yod pas bar chu khar mchod rten chen po
bzhengs shig shar phyogs na chu srin de'u la 'dring pa lta bu'i sa dgra yod pa lam grum pa ri yin/ de la dung g.yas su 'khyil ba zhig gi kha ston/ shar lho na srin mo mdoms
bzed pa 'dra ba'i sa dgra yod pas/ byang stod seng phug yin/ de la dbang phyug chen po'i kha ston/ lho nub na sdig pa nag po bzan la rub pa 'dra ba'i sa dgra yod/ yug
ma ri'i shar ri 'di yin/ de la bya khyung ke ru zhig gi kha ston/ nub na bdud nag po bya ra byed pa 'dra ba'i sa dgra yod/ shun gyi brag rtse 'di yin/ de la rdo'i mchod rten
zhig gi kha ston/ byang na glang po che g.yul du zhugs pa 'dra ba'i sa dgra yod/ nyang bran dge re gnyis kyi dbus ri yin/ de la rdo'i seng ge zhig gi kha ston/ des nye
ba'i sa dgra thams cad non pa yin no/ /de ltar sa dgra thams cad mnan pa dang / yon tan thams cad phyogs gcig tu tshang ste/ shar na ri mchod rten 'dra ba yod/ ban khos
bang ba ri yin/ lho na rin po che spungs pa 'dra ba yod/ grib kyi rgyab ri 'di yin/ nub na ri manydzi'i steng na dung phor bzhag pa 'dra ba yod/ stod lung brang phu'i ri
yin/ byang na ri padma kha phye ba 'dra ba yod/ dge re lha phu'i ri yin/ gzhan yang nyang bran 'phan dkar gyi ri la dbu la gdugs/ mal grong gi rgyab ri la spyan la nya/
mdangs mkhar gyi brag la ljags la padma/ grib kyi 'khyag khrom

la gsung la dung / rdzong btsan gyi ri la mgul la bum pa/ yug ma'i ri la thugs dpal be'u/ 'phan dkar gyi ri la sku lus rgyal mtshan/ stod lung brang phu'i spang la phyag zhabs
'khor lo ste/ bkra shis pa'i rtags brgyad tshang yod do// gzhan yang gar pa'i jo mo ze ze la lcags kyi gter kha/ ra ga brag la zangs kyi gter kha/ la dong gi brag la
dngul gyi gter kha/ lcags kha ri'i brag la gser gyi gter kha yod do/ /shar na stag skya bo dga' mo gdong 'og ma/ lho na g.yu 'brug sngon mo chu/ nub na bya dmar po shun gyi
brag dmar rte'u'i gdong yin/ byang na rus sbal nag po nyang bran pha bong kha yin/ de ltar srin mo gan rkyal du nyal ba'i yan lag dang nying lag rnams non par byed pa
la/ mi 'gyur ba'i gzer bcu gnyis zer te/ de yang mtha' 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang bzhi ni/ g.yo ru na khra 'brug spu ru na ka tshal/ g.yas ru gtsang 'phrang gi lha khang /
gtsang na grum pa rgyang gi lha khang / des ma thub na/ yang 'dul gyi lha khang bzhi brtsigs/ kong po bu chu'i lha khang / 'khon mthing gser gyi lha khang / byams sprin dge
rgyas kyi lha khang / spra dun tse'i lha khang / des ma thub na/ ru non gyi lha khang bzhi rtsigs shig de yang / khams su klong thang sgron ma/ bum thang skyer chu'i lha
khang / mtshal rigs shes rab sgron ma'i lha khang / tshangs pa rlung non gyi lha khang / de rnams sngon la bzhengs shig ma grub na'ang sa phur thob cig de ltar byas na/
khyod kyis gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa la 'gal rkyen bar chad med do/ /gnam 'khor lo rtsibs brgyad/ sa padma 'dab brgyad/ logs bkra shis rtags brgyad/ sa yul 'di srin mo'i
snying thog rang du 'dug gong gi rten 'brel de rnams rim

pa bzhin du mdzod/ mtsho bsubs pa'i thog ma la/ ra dkar mo la sa khol la bsubs shig de'i steng du lha khang legs par bzhengs shig phrag dog gi log lta ma mdzad cig ces rgya
mo bzas bal mo bza'i g.yog mo la legs par bslabs so/ /der g.yog mo des khri btsun gyi rtsar/ 'phrin gong 'og 'dzol te/ gong gi skyon sel ba/ sa dgra non pa/ yon tan yod
pa/ mtha' 'dul yang 'dul gyi lha khang bzhengs nas/ thabs rten 'brel legs par bshad pa rnams brjed/ der lha khang bzhengs pa'i sa cha gang bzang bar 'dug dris pas/ phyogs
mtha' dag rnams su sngon la lha khang bcu gnyis brtsig dgos zer/ ra la sa khol la mtsho bsubs/ de'i steng du lha khang bzhengs zer gyi 'dug byas pas/ khri btsun the tshom
du gyur te/ 'on kyang g.yog mos zer ba bzhin/ ra la sa bkal nas mtsho bsubs pas/ bye ba stong gi cha yang zub ma 'dod do/ /der rgya mo bzas ngan bslabs par go nas phrag
dog skyes/ shin tu ma dga' bar gyur nas/ rgyal po la yang ma zhus par/ blon po 'ga' zhig gi kha la nyan nas/ la dong gi ne'u thang la sa'i dpyad bzang bar shes nas/ lha
khang rmang bting pas/ nyin par brtsigs pa thams cad nub mo lha 'dres rjes med par bshig 'dug pas/ khri btsun yi mug cing sdug bsngal bar gyur nas/ rgyal po la zhus pas/
rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyod sdug bsngal bar ma byed/ nga la gros 'dri sa cig yod do gsungs te/ de'i mtshan mo rgyal pos yi dam gyi lha la gsol ba btab pas/ yid dam gyi lha'i
thugs ka nas 'od zer zhig 'phros nas mtsho nang du thim par gyur to/ /der rgyal po'i thugs la mtsho bsubs pa'i steng du lha khang bzhengs na

bzang bar dgongs nas/ khri btsun la rgyal po'i zhal nas/ chibs sga stod cig sang nged gnyis skyo sangs la 'gro'o gsungs so/ /de'i sang rgyal po dang btsun mo gnyis mtsho 'gram
gyi ne'u thang la skyo sangs la byon te/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khri btsun la/ khyod rang gi sor gdub phud la nam mkha' la gtor cig de gar babs pa'i thang du lha khang
brtsigs pa yin no gsungs pas/ der khri btsun gyis yi dam gyi lha la smon lam btab ste/ sor gdub nam mkha' la 'phangs pas/ 'od zer gyi gong bur 'dril nas mtsho nang du lhung
bar gyur to/ /der khri btsun gyi bsam pa la/ mtsho'i steng du lha khang brtsig dgos na/ skye ba 'di la grub pa mi srid snyam nas/ rta kha nas babs te sdug bsngal bar byas
pa dang / rgyal po'i zhal nas khyod ma ngu bar mtsho nang du ltos shig yon tan du ma dang ldan par 'dug gsungs so/ /der khri btsun gyis mchi ma phyis nas bltas pas/ mtsho'i
nang na 'od zer sna tshogs las grub pa'i mchod rten khri 'phang dgu yod pa zhig mthong ngo / /de la brten nas mtsho nang thams cad 'od zer gyi dra bas 'brel te/ lha
khang gi ri mo lta bur 'dug pas/ khri btsun yid ches te/ rgyal pos kyang lha khang brtsig grogs mdzad par zhal gyis bzhes so/ /de'i sang rgyal po blon po'i tshogs dang
bcas pas rol mo dang bcas te/ tsandan gyi sku rang byon gdan drangs te mtsho 'gram du byon no/ /der mtsho'i phyogs bzhir sa phur gdab bo/ / dar po che 'phyar te smon lam
btab/ der khri btsun gyis baiDUrya'i lhung bzed la gsol ba btab pas zas chang dpag tu med pa byung ste/ bod 'bangs thams cad las la bskul/ skye chu sbo ba gdong la bsgyur/
mtsho'i phyogs bzhir rdo

bskyed du bcug nas/ mtsho gru bzhir bcos so/ /mtsho'i phyogs bzhir rdo dpe chen po mtsho'i nang du lhags pa bzhi bzhi byas shing / rgyal pos rdo dpe de rnams kyi steng du byon
nas/ mtsho'i dkyil gyi 'od zer gyi mchod rten de la dmigs te smon lam btab/ blon po rnams kyis yi ge drug pa'i sgra dang bcas te/ rdo rnams mtsho nang du bskyur bas/
rgyal po'i smon lam gyi mthu la brten nas/ mtsho de'i dkyil nas rdo'i mchod rten khri 'phang gru bzhir yod pa zhig rang thag gi lte ba lta bur lhun gyis grub ste/ sra zhing
brtan la mi 'gyur bar 'dug pa rgyal po yab yum blon po'i tshogs dang bcas pas legs par gzigs pas/ thams cad yid ches shing mos par byas so/ /de nas shing shug pa'i sdong
po sbom la ring ba bcu drug bcad nas/ rtsa ba phyogs bzhi'i rdo dpe chen po rnams la gtad/ rtse mo mtsho'i dkyil gyi rdo'i mchod rten rang byon la gtad de/ gdugs kyi rtsib
mang bzhin du byas so/ /de'i steng du shing gla ba'i sdong po sbom la ring ba mang po bcad nas/ de'i steng du mig mangs ris su byas so/ /de yang sprul pa'i dge slong
a ka ra ma ti shI las/ klu'i yul du rdzu 'phrul gyis byon te/ rdo rje'i 'jim pa blangs shing rnams la byugs pas/ bskal pa'i bar du chu nang na gnas kyang mi rul cing / mes
kyang mi tshig cing / bcad kyang mi chod do/ /de'i steng du spang leb bsgrigs/ de'i steng du so phag bsgrigs te khro chus bsdams/ de'i steng sa khod snyoms par byas nas/
de ltar sa pho khyi la 'o thang gi mtsho bsubs pas legs par tshar te/ chos rgyal dgung lo nyi shu rtsa gsum gyi steng du/ lha sa'i rtsig rmang bting pa lags/ sa mo phag
la lha khang rmang bting / rked pa tsam brtsigs tshar

nas thams cad dga' bar gyur pa dang / sang nyin lha 'dres bshig 'dug go / yang khri btsun sdug bsngal bar gyur nas/ rgyal po'i drung du byung ste/ rgyal po chen po mtsho bsubs
pa'i steng du lha khang brtsig mi btub par 'dug pa/ bdag gi lha khang la gzigs dang zhes zhus pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyod sdug bsngal ma byed cig nga la gros 'dri
sa zhig yod do gsungs so/ /der rgyal pos yi dam gyi lha la gsol ba btab pas/ nam mkha' nas gzugs med pa'i sgra zhig byung ste| rgyal po khyed rang gi sku 'bag jo bo bcu
gcig zhal zhig bzhengs na/ khyed kyi lha khang bzhengs pa la 'gal rkyen mi 'byung bar 'gyur ro zer te mi snang bar gyur to/ /der rgyal po'i zhal nas bal po'i lha bzo ba la/
khyod kyis nga'i sku 'bag tu ming btags pa'i/ 'phags pa bcu gcig zhal zhig bzhengs nus sam gsungs pas/ nus lags zer te/ de'i bzo rgyu la tsandan sbrul gyi snying po'i
dum bu/ tsandan gor shi Sha'i dum bu/ byang chub shing gi yal ga rgya mtsho gle'i 'jag ma/ chu bo nai ranydza ra'i bye ma/ dben gnas chen po brgyad kyi sa la sogs pa rgya
gar nas spyan drangs pa'i ngo mtshar che ba'i rdzas mang po bsags te/ legs par brdar nas/ ba dmar po'i 'o ma dang / ra dkar mo'i 'o ma la sbyar te| 'jim pa'i phung po chen
po zhig byas/ rgyal po rin po che'i khri'i steng du gzims pa'i dbu sngas su bzhag ste/ rgyal pos yi dam gyi lha la gsol ba btab nas/ nga'i yi dam gyi lha 'di la/ spyan
ras gzigs la rigs mang po yod pa ji lta bu zhig bzhengs dgongs pa dang / de rnams kyi nang nas bcu gcig zhal yid bzhin gyi nor bu lhag pa yin pas bzhengs dgos dgongs pa
dang /

sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad nyi zer gyi rdul tsam du lhags te| 'jim pa'i phung po la thim pa rgyal pos gzigs pas/ rgyal po'i thugs la/ nga'i yi dam 'di
la byin rlabs can zhig 'byon par 'dug go dgongs nas/ rin po che'i khri'i steng du gzims so/ /nangs par gung langs pa dang / bcu gcig zhal yid bzhin gyi nor bu rang byon du
snang ste/ lha bzos bzhengs ma dgos so/ /de la rtsa ba'i zhal gsum dkar po rab tu 'dzum pa zhi ba'i phrin las/ de'i steng gi zhal gsum gser gyi mdog rngams pa'i khro zhal
rgyas pa'i phrin las/ de'i steng gi zhal gnyis byi ru'i mdog bzhad pa'i khro zhal dbang gi phrin las/ de'i steng gi zhal gnyis nag pa khros shing gdangs pa'i khro zhal
drag po'i phrin las/ de'i steng du a mi dhe ba li khri'i mdog can a mi dhe ba man rgyal po'i sku tshad dang mnyam pa/ chos sku'i rtsa ba'i phyag bcu'i phyag mtshan ni/ dang
po gnyis thugs kar thal mo sbyar ba/ g.yas kyi gnyis pa na bgrang phreng / gsum pa na 'khor lo/ bzhi pa na mchog sbyin/ lnga pa na 'od dpag med bsnams pa'o/ / g.yon gyi
gnyis pa na padma dkar po/ gsum pa na ril ba spyi blugs/ bzhi pa na rin po che/ lnga pa na mda' gzhu bsnams pa'o/ /sprul pa'i phyag rnams ni lha bzo bas bzhengs/ rang
byon du byon dus/ rtsa phyag bcu po las mi 'dug longs spyod rdzogs pa'i yan lag sum cu so brgyad yod pa ni/ g.yas phyogs kyi phyag bcu dgu'i rim pa bzhin du/ dang po na rin
po che/ gnyis pa na zhags pa/ gsum pa na lhung bzed/ bzhi pa na ral gri/ lnga pa na rdo rje/ drug pa na me shel/ bdun pa na chu shel/ brgyad pa na gzhu/ dgu pa na lcug
ma/ bcu pa na rnga yab/ bcu gcig na phub/

bcu gnyis na bum pa/ bcu gsum na dgra sta/ bcu bzhi na phreng ba/ bco lnga na padma sngon po/ bcu drug na spyi blugs/ bcu bdun na nyi ma/ bco brgyad na chu skyes dkar po/ bcu
dgu na 'bras kyi snye ma 'dzin pa'o/ /g.yon gyi yan lag bcu dgu'i rim pa bzhin du/ dang po na sprin dkar/ gnyis pa na spyi blugs/ gsum pa na padma/ bzhi pa na ral gri/
lnga pa na dung / drug pa na thod pa/ bdun pa na phreng ba/ brgyad pa na dril bu/ dgu pa na rdo rje/ bcu pa na lcags kyu/ bcu gcig na 'khar gsil/ bcu gnyis na sangs rgyas
sprul sku/ bcu gsum na lha khang / bcu bzhi na glegs bam/ bco lnga na 'khor lo/ bcu drug na sangs rgyas kyi sku/ bcu bdun na shing thog bco brgyad na padma ge sar/ bcu
dgu na rin po che bsnams pa'o/ /sprul pa'i nying lag stong tham pa rab tu mdzes pa/ phyag re re'i mthil na ye shes kyi spyan re re yod pa/ phyag dang zhabs la gser gyi gdu
gu dang sbrul gyis brgyan pa/ khro zhal rnams ni spyan gsum re dang ldan pa/ dbu skra kham pa gyen la 'khyil ba/ sku lus la rin po che'i rgyan du mas brgyan pa/ 'od dang
'od zer phyogs bcur 'phro ba/ sku stod la ri dwags kyi lpags pas g.yogs nas nu ma g.yon pa bkab pa/ mtshan dang dpe byad gyis brgyan pa zhig 'od du khrong nge byon 'dug
pa rgyal pos gzigs pas shin tu dgyes par gyur to// de nas rgyal po'i zhal nas/ bal po'i lha bzo ba la khyed kyi rten 'di/ ngo mtshar che la mgyogs pa zhig bzhengs tshar
'dug na'ang / rgya gar nas byon pa'i tsandan gyi sku rang byon 'di dang / sangs rgyas rabs bdun gyi ring bsrel rnams rten 'di'i thugs kar bzhugs su 'jug rgyu yin lags gsungs
pas/ lha bzo ba na

re| rten 'di bdag gis bzhengs pa ma lags/ rang byon du gda'o zhus pa dang / de ma thag tu sku g.yos par gyur te/ zhabs g.yon pa'i sham thabs pus mo'i gong du brdzes/ thugs
ka nas 'od zer byung ste/ sangs rgyas kyi ring bsrel dang / tsandan gyi sku rang byon rnams spyan drangs te/ thugs kar ye shes sems dpa'i tshul du bzhugs so/ /a mi dhe ba
g.yon phyogs su cung yo ba dang / sham thabs kyang pus mo'i gong du lus pa rnams/ phyi rabs su yang de ltar du yod do/ /de la tsandan sbrul gyi snying po de dbu'i srog shing
du gyur/ byang chub kyi shing gnyis zhabs kyi srog shing du gyur/ sngar gyi rdzas rnams la sku lus su gyur te/ me tog gtor ro/ /de nas bal po'i lha bzos 'khor rnams
bzhengs pa ni/ 'jig rten dbang phyug dang / kharsa pa Ni dang khro gnyer can dang / sgrol ma dang 'od zer can dang / dbyangs can ma dang / bdud rtsi 'khyil ba dang / dpal
rta mgrin rnams bzhengs so/ /der bkra shis pa'i ltas kyis phyogs thams cad du khyab par gyur nas/ sa yang rnam pa drug tu g.yos so/ /der rgyal po yab yum blon po'i tshogs
dang bcas pas/ mchod rdzas du ma thogs te/ smon lam btab bo/ /de nas rgyal po'i rten de'i drung du/ lha khang brtsig pa'i 'gal rkyen bzlog cing/ mthun rkyen sgrub pa'i
gsol ba 'debs kyin yod tsa na/ nub phyogs zla ba tshal gyi dug shing gi sdong po rkang gcig gi rtsa na/ 'dre srin dang mi ma yin mang po 'tshogs nas/ khong rnams na re/ srong
btsan sgam po zer ba'i mgo gnyis yod pa 'dis/ nged rang tsho'i 'dug sa bshig rgyu srang bkab/ nged rang tsho yang kho'i lha khang brtsig tu mi 'jug dge ba byed pa'i
srog gcod/ sad ser ba dang / nad

yams gtong zer gin 'dug pa rgyal pos mkhyen nas 'phags pa la gsol ba drag tu btab pas/ 'phags pa bzhad pa'i zhal nas 'od zer byung ba me ru gyur/ khros pa'i zhal nas 'od zer
byung ba rta mgrin dang bdud rtsi 'khyil ba gnyis su gyur te/ khro bo gnyis ye shes kyi me dang bcas pas zla ba tshal gyi dug shing gi sdong po la brgyab/ sran phung dkyil
du thog babs pa bzhin byas te/ 'dre la la ni brgyal/ la la ni bog la la skad ngan 'don par gyur to/ /der khro bo gnyis kyis ye shes kyi me dang bcas pas de rnams ded
de/ phyi'i rgya mtsho chen po la bsgral nas phyir mi ldog pa byas so/ /der ye shes kyi me zla ba tshal gyi brag la phog pas brag de la kharsa pa Ni rang byon du byon par
gyur to/ /de'i sang rgyal po blon po'i tshogs dang bcas pas rang byon de'i drung du byon te/ mchod pa phul zhing smon lam btab nas/ bstod pa mdzad pa/ spyan ras gzigs dbang
'jig rten mgon/ /thub pa'i dbang pos spyi gtsug brgyan/ /sku mdog dkar gsal gangs ri 'dra/ /nyon mongs ma gos padmo bzhin/ /thugs rje che zhing mthu ldan pa// sems can
nyam thag phongs rgu yi/ /nad dang sdug bsngal zhi mdzad pa/ /mgon du gyur la phyag 'tshal lo/ /zhes gsungs so/ /rang byon de brag la gsal bar byon na'ang / ma 'ongs pa'i
sems can bsod nams bsog pa'i phyir du/ bal po'i lha bzos gsal bar brkos so/ /de nas lha khang brtsigs pa la bgegs med par dgongs nas/ rje blon kun gyis mtsho bsubs pa'i
steng du byon/ sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs nas thig gdab bo/ /de'i dus su klu'i rgyal po sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das sku mdog dkar po sbrul gyi gdengs ka can/ spyan gsum

dang ldan pa byon te/ rgyal po la sbrul zhags dkar po zhig phul nas/ rgyal po'i lha khang 'di la stong chung ngu'i bar gyi gnod pa byung na ngas srungs shig nga'i gzugs zhig
mdzod cig zer ro/ /yang klu'i rgyal po dga' bo byung nas/ rgyal po'i lha khang 'di la stong gsum gyi bar du chu'i gnod pa byung na ngas srungs shig nga'i gzugs zhig mdzod
cig zer ro/ /yang srin po'i rgyal po langka mgrin bcu byung nas/ rgyal po la gser gzhong pa gang phul nas/ rgyal po'i lha khang 'di la me'i gnod pa byung na ngas bsrung
zhing nga'i gzugs zhig mdzod cig zer ro/ / yang gnod sbyin na ga ku be ra byung nas/ gser gyi thags bzangs shig phul nas/ rgyal po'i lha khang 'di la 'byung ba bzhi'i gnod
pa byung na ngas srungs shig nga'i gzugs zhig mdzod cig zer ro/ /yang ma hA kA la byung nas/ rgyal po'i lha khang 'di la mtha' dmag dang mi ma yin gyi gnod pa byung na
ngas srungs shig nga'i gzugs zhig mdzod cig zer ro/ /yang dpal ldan lha mo byung ste/ lcags kyi bre ba zhig phul nas/ rgyal po khyed kyi lha khang 'di la mi dang ma mo'i
gnod pa byung na ngas srungs shig nga'i gzugs zhig mdzod cig zer ro/ /yang bla ma rnams byon te/ rgyal po'i lha khang 'di bla ma'i lugs su bzhengs shig gsung ngo // yang
sngags pa rnams byung ste/ rgyal po'i lha khang 'di nged sngags pa'i lugs su bzhengs shig zer ro/ /yang bon po rnams byung ste/ rgyal po'i lha khang 'di bod 'bangs kyi
lugs su bzhengs shig zer ro/ /der rgyal po shin tu dgyes nas thams cad zhal gyis bzhes so/ /der rgyal pos bod 'bangs rnams la zas chang gis tshims par byas te las la bskul
nas/ la las so phag btang /

la las rtsig pa byas/ la las 'jim pa btang ste/ 'og khang gi rtsig pa zin par byas so/ /lha sa'i rtsig rmang bting pa man/ tshal pa kun dga' rdo rjes rab byung mdzad pa yan
la lo bdun brgya dang bzhi bcu zhe lnga 'gro ba rtogs ldan sngo nyal ma gsungs/ de nas shing shug pa'i sdong po mang po bcad nas/ rgyal pos sku lus kyi sprul pa brgya rtsa
brgyad mdzad de/ lha khang gi sgo bsrung ste/ nang du shing bzo ba ste'u thogs pa brgya rtsa brgyad du sprul nas shing bzo mdzad/ bsang bu yang bal mo bza' min pa gzhan
gyis mi skyel lo| |dus nam zhig khri btsun yi dam la mchod pa 'bul ba dang dus 'dzom nas/ rgyal po'i bsang bu g.yog mo la bskur ro/ /g.yog mos sgo phyes nas phyin pas/
rgyal po med par shing bzo ba cha lugs dbyer mi phyed pa'i ste'u thogs pa brgya rtsa brgyad du 'dug ste/ seng ge brgya rtsa brgyad kyi sna'i bzo byed kyin 'dug pas/ bsang
bu gang la 'dren ngo ma shes par phyir log nas/ bsang bu bal mo la gtad do/ /der g.yog mo'i bsam pa la/ rgyal po 'dis sprul pa mkhyen zer ba de e bden bsams nas/ khri btsun
rgyal po la bsang bu 'dren song ba'i rjes la| g.yog mos sgo phag nas bltas pas thams cad sprul par 'dug pa/ he he zer bgad pas/ rgyal po spyan yengs pa dang ste'u kha
'chor bas shing bzo ba thams cad kyi ste'u kha 'chor nas/ seng ge rnams sna chad do/ /der yang la las ka ba bcos/ la las gdung ma gzhog la las lcam gru bzhir bcos/ yang
la las ka ba btsug la las gdung bkal/ la las lcam bsgrig la las spang leb btang / thog phub nas mdzes par byas so/ jo bo rje'i gter yig chen mo na/ lha sa'i 'og khang la
nyin zhag gnyis la zin pa byas zer bar 'dug ste/ thog phub pa der 'dug de ltar rgyal

pos sprul pa mdzad pas/ rtsig pa la nyin zhag bzhi/ shing bzo la nyin zhag drug thog 'bub pa la nyin zhag gnyis/ dril bas nyin zhag bcu gnyis la/ ra sa'i 'og khang yongs su
rdzogs par zin par byas so/ /de yang sgo bzhi dkyil 'khor ris su byas pas bla ma dga'/ ka ba phur pa ris su byas pas sngags pa dga'/ zur bzhi g.yung drung ris su byas pas
bon po dga'/ re'u mig ris su byas pas bod 'bangs dga'/ gyis zer ba'i gzugs thams cad byas pas/ chos skyong klu dang gnod sbyin srin po la sogs pa rnams dga'o/ /de yang
dga' bzhi 'phrul gyi lha khang gi sgo yang nub phyogs bal po'i yul du gtad do/ /de'i 'phro la khri btsun gyis bal po'i yul nas rig byed la mkhas pa'i bzo bo mang po bos nas
steng khang bzhengs so/ /lha sa'i steng khang dang / ra mo che gnyis la zla ba bcu gnyis re 'gor te lhan du tshar ro/ /de dang dus mnyam du rgya mo bzas kyang rgya yul
nas shing bzo ba dang / lha bzo ba mang po bos nas/ rgya stag ra mo che'i lha khang bzhengs te/ lha khang gi sgo shar du bstan no/ /de'i bar la rgyal pos sprul pa mdzad
nas mtha' 'dul dang / yang 'dul dang / ru gnon gyi lha khang bzhengs pa ni/ srin mo'i dpung pa g.yas gnon pa'i phyir/ sbu ru ka tshal mi 'gyur ba'i lha khang bzhengs/ de'i
yan lag tu gser shang gi rti'i lha khang bzhengs/ de'i sgrub pa rtse mo gdong gi brag phug tu byas so/ /dpung pa g.yon gnon pa'i phyir/ g.yo ru khra 'brug bkra shis byams
snyoms kyi lha khang bzhengs/ de'i yan lag tu tsan thang gi lha khang btab/ de'i sgrub pa phug mo cher byas so/ /dpyi mgo g.yas gnon pa'i phyir/ g.yas ru gtsang 'brang
byang chub dge gnas kyi lha khang bzhengs/ de'i

yan lag tu dge drung gi lha khang btab/ de'i sgrub pa rtse'i brag phug tu byas so/ / dpyi mgo g.yon gnon pa'i phyir du/ grub pa rgyal dri med rnam dag gi lha khang bzhengs/
de'i yan lag tu 'bre'i lha khang btab/ de'i sgrub pa rgyang gi brag phug tu byas so/ /de nas yang 'dul gyi lha khang bzhi brtsigs pa ni/ gre mo g.yas gnon pa'i phyir/ shar
stag gi mgo steng du/ kong po bu chu'i lha khang bzhengs/ gre mo g.yon gnon pa'i phyir/ lho 'brug gi ze steng du/ lho brag mkhon mthing gi lha khang bzhengs/ pus mo g.yas
gnon pa'i phyir/ nub phyogs bya dmar po'i sgal steng du/ byams chen dge rgyas kyi lha khang bzhengs/ pus mo g.yon gnon pa'i phyir/ byang rus sbal gyi dpral steng du/
pra ngan tse'i lha khang bzhengs/ des kyang ma thub dogs na/ ru gnon gyi lha khang bzhi bzhengs te/ lag mthil g.yas gnon pa'i phyir/ khams su glang thang sgron ma'i lha khang
mi nyag gis lag dpon byas nas bzhengs/ lag 'thil g.yon gnon pa'i phyir/ lho phyogs su bum thang skyer chu'i lha khang tho dkar gyis lag dpon byas nas bzhengs/ rkang
mthil g.yas gnon pa'i phyir/ nub dpal kha che'i gnas su/ mtshal rig shes rab sgron ma'i lha khang bal pos lag dpon byas nas bzhengs/ rkang mthil g.yon gnon pa la/ byang phyogs
su tshangs pa rlung non gyi lha khang hor sba dpal dbyangs kyis lag dpon byas nas bzhengs so/ /gzhan yang shar du ka chu/ kang chu/ gling chu gsum/ nyi zla gza' skar
gtan la 'bebs pa'i phyir du bzhengs so/ /lho ru snyal snang gro lha khang / gling thang gnyis/ me lha drang srong bsgrubs te me'i kha gnon du bzhengs/ nub tu gu lang shing
khun gnyis/ bal bod kyi so mtshams

bsrungs te chu'i kha gnon du bzhengs/ byang du dge ri dang dpal ri gnyis/ lha klu 'dre srin dam la btags te rlung gi kha gnon du bzhengs/ de rnams bzhengs pa'i byin rlabs kyis/
nyi 'og gi rgyal khams zil gyis mnan te/ ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa la/ 'gal rkyen bar chad med par lhun gyis grub pa'o/ /de nas khri btsun dang
kong jo gnyis kyis/ ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang dang / rgya stag ra mo che'i gtsug lag khang gnyis kyi ri mo gang dang spyi yongs su rdzogs pa rnams la zla ba
bcu gnyis re 'gor te lhan du tshar ro| |rgyal pos kyang mtha' 'dul yang 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang rnams yongs su rdzogs pa tshar te/ slar khra 'brug tu phebs nas/ sangs rgyas
kyi bstan pa rin po che la bkur sti dang / phu dud du mdzad nas/ rab tu byung ba'i rtags yod pa tsam la yang / mgo'i thod ltar du khur zhing gus pas phyag byed la/ nga'i
blon 'bangs rnams kyis kyang de bzhin gyis shig gsungs te/ phyi rol du byon pa dang / sbrul bsad pa'i sdig bshags su bzhengs pa'i mchod rten rtse lnga de'i drung na|
sprang ban rgan po gcig bla gos hrul po zhig bting nas shig thu gin 'dug pa rgyal pos gzigs pa dang / sprang ban de la rab tu byung ba'i rtags 'dug par mkhyen nas/ rgyal
pos phyag mdzad do/ /der rgyal po'i zhal nas/ bdag ni rgyal khams la dbang thob pa'i rgyal po zhig yin na'ang mtha' 'khob kha ba can gyi ljongs 'dir sangs rgyas kyi bstan
pa nyi ma shar ba lta bu zhig byed par 'dod nas/ gtsug lag khang mang po brtsigs/ de rnams kyi nang du sangs rgyas kyi sku gsung thugs kyi rten mang po bzhengs nas mchod
pa byas/ rab tu byung ba'i

rtags yod tsam la'ang phyag byed par dam bcas pa yin pas de ngo mtshar mi che'am gsungs pas/ sprang ban de langs te bla gos hrul po de dpung pa la gzar nas/ rgyal po khyed
sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la dgongs nas rab tu byung ba la mos gus mdzad de/ bdag sprang ban la phyag mdzad pa de ngo mtshar che ste/ nga'i 'di'ang ngo mtshar mi che'am gsungs
nas/ mchod rten rtse lnga de lag pa g.yas pa'i sor mo lnga'i steng du blangs te bskor ba gcig byas so/ /der rgyal po cung zhig skyengs par gyur nas/ dbu'i la thod phud
de/ a mi dhe ba'i zhal bstan nas/ khyed kyi de ngo mtshar che ste/ nga'i 'di'ang ngo mtshar mi che'am gsungs pas/ yang sprang ban des brang sgo phye/ mtshon chas brang
gshags te/ kun rig rnam par snang mdzad kyi lha thams cad byang khog nang du bzhugs pa bstan nas/ rgyal po khyed la lha gcig las mi 'dug nga la 'di tsam yod/ 'di ngo mtshar
mi che'am zer bas/ rgyal po shin tu dgyes shing dad par gyur nas mchod gnas su mdzad do| |der rgyal po'i zhal nas/ rab tu byung ba rnams ni bla gos hrul po'am cha lugs
dang spyod lam ci 'dra na'ang / log par lta ba ma byed par mos gus gyis shig dper na 'di lta bu'o zhes zhal gdams so/ /mtha' 'dul yang 'dul gyi lha khang dang / 'phrul
snang ra mo che rnams legs par bzhengs pa'i le'u ste bcu bzhi pa'o// //bco lnga pa/ lha sa gnyis dang / mtha' 'dul yang 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang tshar nas rab tu gnas par
mdzad pa'i skor/ de nas khri btsun dang kong jo gnyis kyis gtsug lag khang legs par bzhengs pas yongs su rdzogs par

tshar te/ rgyal po spyan drangs nas/ po ta la'i rtser phebs so/ /de'i sang khri btsun gyis gtsug lag khang gzigs par 'bul ba la/ spos dang rol mo sna tshogs pa dang bcas te/
rgyal po blon po'i tshogs dang bcas pa 'phrul snang du spyan drangs so| |der khri btsun gyis lha khang gi sgo phyes nas/ rgyal po nang du byon par bzhed pa la mthil gyi
zha la chu'i mdog lta bu/ steng phyogs kyi gzugs brnyan thams cad de la shar ba gzigs pas/ sngar gyi mtsho 'di brdol 'dug dgongs nas/ nang du 'byon ma nus pa dang / khri
btsun gyis sor gdub phud de gtor bas/ khyag thog khar rde'u bskur ba bzhin khrol gyis song ba dang / rgyal pos gzigs pas thugs ches te nang du byon no/ /der khri btsun la
khyed kyi lha khang 'di 'phrul du snang ngo gsungs/ dang po ra la sa bkal nas mtsho bsrubs/ de nas rgyal pos 'phrul du snang ngo gsungs pas/ ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug
lag khang zhes yongs su grags so/ /de ltar rgyal pos lha khang nang gi ngo mtshar che ba rnams gzigs pas/ 'di lta ste/ ngo mtshar 'gran med rgyal ba'i gzhal yas khang /
/ yon tan mtha' yas rab tu mdzes pa ste/ /gzhi ma gru bzhi lhun gyis grub pa la// zur chen bzhi ni g.yung drung ris su byas/ /sgo yi ri bzhi dkyil 'khor lta bur bzos/ /mthil
gyi zha la baiDUrya yi mdog /steng gi ri mo nya dang chu srin rnams// me long nang gi gzugs brnyan ji bzhin no/ /steng 'og gnyis kyi ka ba thams cad ni/ /rab tu mdzes
pa rdo rje phur pa'i bzo/ /ka gzhu gdung dang gdung khebs mchod rten brtsegs/ /bzo yi rnam 'gyur ngo mtshar 'gran zla med/ /phyi nang gab spangs ka gzhu thams cad la/ /sngon
gyi sgrung brgyud gsal bar 'bur

du brkos/ /steng 'og gnyis kyi mthongs kha'i lcam sna la/ /seng ge dkar mo g.yu ral rgyan dang bcas/ /brgya rtsa brgyad ni mchong ba'i tshul du gzigs/ /de yi steng du mu tig
dra ba can/ /g.yu pad sngon po indra nI la'i mdog /steng gi rtsig pa pha gu dra phyed dang / /mda' yab pu shu rin chen rgyan gyis mdzes/ /'od zer stong ldan gser gyi gandzi
ra/ /sna tshogs dar gyi cod pan du ma dang / /rnga yab dril bu g.yer kha'i rgyan dang bcas/ khor yug kun tu lcags kyi thag pas sbrel/ /de ltar ngo mtshar dpag med rgyan
bkod pa'i/ /'og gi btsan khang dbus ma'i gzhal yas na/ /'gro ba skyob mdzad skyabs sbyin phyag rgya can/ /de dus kyi gtso bo de sangs rgyas mi 'gro gsung byon yin/ mtshan
dpes rab brgyan tshogs gnyis dpal gyis brjid/ /sangs rgyas mar me mdzad ni sprul sku la/ /'khor ni nye ba'i sras brgyad bzhengs pas bskor/ khro bo gnyis kyis sgo srung
mdzad pa gzigs/ / btsan khang g.yas na sangs rgyas 'od dpag med/ /li khri'i mdog can mnyam gzhag phyag rgya can/ /ngo mtshar dpag med mtshan dpe'i rgyan gyis mdzes/ /spyan
ras gzigs dang mthu chen thob la sogs/ /nye ba'i sras brgyad 'khor gyis bskor ba ni/ /pad zla'i gdan la rdo rje phyed krung bzhugs/ /sgo 'gram g.yas na gsang ba'i bdag
po ni/ /nam mkha'i mdog can rdo rje mkha' la phyar/ /sgo 'gram g.yon na khro rgyal sme brtsegs ni/ /byi ru'i mdog can grib sel tshul du bzhugs/ /btsan khang g.yon na rje
btsun byams pa ni/ /chos kyi 'khor lo bskor ba'i phyag rgya can/ /gur gum mdog can mtshan dpe'i dpal gyis brjid/ /phyi nang mchod pa'i lha mos bskor ba ni/ /ngo mtshar
dpag med rab mdzes 'gying

ba'i tshul/ /pad zla'i gdan la rdo rje phyed krung bzhugs/ /btsan khang lho na mi bskyod rdo rje ni/ /mtshan dpes rab brgyan sa gnon mnyam gzhag can/ /'od stong 'bar ba gser
gyi lhun po ltar/ /rab tu brjid pa'i 'khor gyis bskor ba ni| |stong chen rab 'joms zhal gcig phyag bzhi ma/ /so sor 'brang ma zhal gcig phyag drug yin/ /gshin rje mthar
byed zhabs drug brkyang bskum tshul/ / sku mdog mthing nag zhal drug shin tu khros/ /phyag drug mtshon cha du ma bsnams pa'o/ /shes rab mthar byed sku mdog dkar po ste/
/zhal bzhi phyag brgyad brkyang bskum tshul du bzhugs/ /padma mthar byed padma rA ga'i mdog /zhal gcig phyag bzhi rab tu khros pa'i tshul/ /bgegs mthar byed ni mthing nag
rngams pa'i tshul/ /zhal gcig phyag bzhi bgegs dpung 'joms par mdzad/ /sgo 'gram gnyis na rnam sras dzaM bha la/ /sku mdog ser po dbul phongs sel ba'i phyir/ / phyag g.yas
rin chen g.yon na ne'u le 'dzin/ /phyi sgo'i 'gram gyi klu yi khang pa na| |klu chen gsum ni zhal gcig phyag gnyis te/ /sbrul gyi gdengs ka sems dpa'i skyil krung bcas/
/sku mdog dkar dang dmar dang dmar ser yin/ /sgo 'gram g.yas kyi gnod sbyin khang pa na/ /srin mo langka mgrin bcu dbu dgu ste/ / rta mgos dpang bstod sku mdog mthing ga'o/
/gnod sbyin dri za gnyis ni sku mdog dmar/ /zhal gsum phyag bzhi sems dpa'i skyil krung bcas/ /sgo khang steng na sangs rgyas rabs bdun ni/ /mtshan dpes rab brgyan sprul
sku'i tshul du bzhugs/ /'og khang logs la rgyal ba'i sku gzugs ni/ /lha yi ri mo gang la ci 'dul gling / /thugs rje chen po 'jigs pa brgyad skyob dang / /'jam dbyangs

gtso 'khor lnga yi zhing bkod dang / /bde ba can gyi zhing gi bkod pa gzigs/ / lho nub g.yu drung khug na rigs gsum mgon/ /nub phyogs ka tshigs rgyal ba rigs lnga dang / /'gro
don mtha' yas rgyal po'i mdzad pa bris/ /dus gsum sangs rgyas 'khor gyis bskor ba ni/ /nub byang g.yu drung khug gi ri mo yin/ / byang dang byang shar mtshams kyi ri
mo la/ /thub pa'i mdzad pa bcu gnyis rdzogs par yod/ /shar gyi logs la sgrol ma spyan ras gzigs/ /thub pa bdud 'dul sems dpa'i tshogs dang bcas/ /shar lho g.yu drung khug
gi ri mo la/ / bcom ldan sman gyi rgyal po'i lha tshogs bzhugs/ /sgrol ma rta mgrin dkar po la sogs pa'i/ /bar khang nang gi ri mo phal cher ni/ /be bum brgya dang rtsa
brgyad ji bzhin bris/ /sna tshogs tshon gyi ri mo khra ba sogs/ /de rnams rgyal pos gzigs pas dgyes par gyur/ /shar lho'i lcog la seng gi gru skas byas/ / g.yung drung khug
der dpal lha'i rten zhig btsugs/ /btsan khang byang ma ngo mtshar mdzes pa la/ /de na lha yi bdag bzung mi 'dug pas/ /sprul pa'i rgyal po de yi dgongs pa la/ /po ta ri
nas rang byon bcu gcig zhal/ /shing rtar spyan drangs rol mo'i rgyan dang bcas/ /btsan khang byang mar bzhugs dgos dgongs pa la/ /de yi nub mo rang byon gtso 'khor rnams/
/lha yi rol mos bsu ba byas nas ni/ /rdzu 'phrul stobs kyis mkha' la gshegs nas kyang / /btsan khang byang mar gdan khri med par bzhugs/ /'jig rten dbang phyug rgyan gyis
mdzes pa dang / /jo mo khro gnyer can dang dbyangs can ma/ /bdud rtsi 'khyil ba sgo 'gram g.yas su bzhugs/ kharsa pA Ni mgrin pa sngo ba dang / /rje btsun sgrol ma lha
mo

'od zer can/ /rta mgrin rgyal po sgo 'gram g.yon du bzhugs/ /de yi mod la ri dang bcas pa yi/ /rgya mtsho'i gos can rnam pa drug tu g.yos/ /lha rnams kun gyis me tog char pa
phab/ /de nas rgyal po yab yum blon po'i tshogs/ /dad pa'i shugs kyis mchi mas gdong g.yogs shing / /rang rang mchod pa'i yo byad thogs nas ni/ /rab gus gdung bas phyag
'tshal mchod pa 'bul/ /thun mong mchog gi dngos grub thob par gyur/ /'di yi gzhi bdag bstan pa bsrung ba la// klu rgyal dga' bo dang ni nye dga' bo/ /srin po'i rgyal po
lang ka mgrin bcu dang / /gnod sbyin dri za'i tshogs dang ku be ra/ /ma hA kA la dpal gyi lha mo sogs/ /lha khang bstan pa srung ba'i bdag por bskos/ /zhes so/ /de nas rgya
mo bzas kyang / rgyal po ra mo cher gdan drangs te/ lha khang gzigs su phul bas shin tu dgyes par gyur to/ /de nas rgyal pos 'phrul snang dang / ra mo che gnyis la rab
tu gnas pa mdzad par dgongs nas/ dga' ston gyi chas rgya chen po dang / mchod pa'i yo byad bsam gyis mi khyab pa bshams te/ gdugs dang rgyal mtshan dang / rol mo sna tshogs
pa dang bcas nas/ de nas rgyal pos dkyil 'khor gyi steng du byon/ phyag tu me tog bzung / thar mo sbyar te bden pa'i tshig brjod pa ni/ rkang gnyis gtso bo thub dbang
shAkya'i sras/ /grangs med sprul pas 'gro ba'i don mdzad pa/ /ston pa bde bar gshegs pa la sogs pa'i/ / phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas rnams kyis bde legs stsol/ /thabs mkhas
thugs rje ldan pa'i chu rgyun gyis/ /gang la gang 'dul smin cing grol bar mdzad/ /rje btsun spyan ras gzigs dbang la sogs pa/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams

kyis bde legs stsol/ /rnam dag dri ma med pa rgyal ba'i bka'/ /bsdu ba rnam bzhis dam chos rgyas mdzad pa'i/ /rgyal sras gnas brtan rab 'byor la sogs pa'i/ /'phags pa'i nyan
thos rnams kyis bde legs stsol/ /gzhan yang phyogs bcu'i zhing khams thams cad na/ /'das dang ma byon da ltar bzhugs pa yi/ /sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' thams cad
kyis/ /gnas 'dir dbang bskur byin gyis brlab tu gsol/ /zhes gsol ba btab pas/ skad cig nyid la sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang dpa' bo dang dpa' mo/ dam pa chos
skyong srung ma dang bcas pa thams cad nyi zer gyi rdul tsam lhags te/ sprin dang na bun bzhin du 'thibs par gyur to/ /de nas sangs rgyas thams cad kyis me tog gtor nas
byin gyis brlabs par mdzad/ byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis bkra shis brjod nas rab tu gnas par mdzad do/ / tshangs pa dang brgya byin la sogs pa'i lha rnams kyis me tog
gi char chen po phab cing / lha'i bu dang bu mo rnams kyis kyang gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / ba dan dang / lhab lhub dang / rin po che'i phreng ba la sogs pa'i rgyan
du ma dang / lha'i rnga bo che dang / gling bu dang / khar rnga dang / cang te'u dang / rol mo'i tshogs du ma 'khrol zhing / lha'i spos dri zhim po rnams kyang / ma la
ya'i rlung dal bus khyer ba ltar phyogs bcur khyab pas dri zhim mo/ /lha'i bu dang bu mo de rnams kyis mgrin gcig tu sgra phyung ste/ sangs rgyas kun gyi dgongs pa gcig bsdus
pa'i/ / spyan ras gzigs dbang thugs rje'i bdag nyid can/ /mtha' 'khob yul der bstan pa rgyas bya'i phyir/ /'phags pa khyed ni mi yi bdag por 'khrungs/ /rig

gzugs yon tan dpal gyis mngon par mtho/ /srong btsan sgam po sangs rgyas sprul pa'i sku/ /chos rgyal khyed kyi gtsug lag khang gnyis la/ /sangs rgyas rnams kyis rab tu gnas
par mdzad/ /byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis bkra shis brjod/ /lha rnams kun gyis mchod pa rgya chen phul/ /nam mkha' la ni me tog char pa phab/ /bar snang la ni bdug spos
sprin bzhin gtibs/ /sa gzhi thams cad rin chen gcal du bkram/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan legs par btsugs/ /dam pa chos kyi rnga chen dam pa brdung / /de ring
mkha' la chos kyi nyi ma shar/ /de ring dpal gyis sgron mes kun la khyab/ /de ring rgyal pos dbang bskur byin rlabs thob/ /nyi ma'i 'od kyis madmo'i kha bye ltar/ /de ring
blo yi mun pa rab tu bsal/ /dbul pos nor gyi gter kha rnyed pa bzhin/ / chos rgyal byang chub sems dpa' khyed kyis ni/ /thugs kyi dbang po dga' bdes tshim par mdzod/ /ces
zer te mi snang ba gyur to/ /de ltar 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang dang / ra mo che'i gtsug lag khang gnyis la/ rab tu gnas pa lhan gcig tu lhun gyis grub par mdzad
do/ /tshul de lta bu'i gsal la ngos bzung med pa me long nang gi gzugs brnyan lta bu'am/ chu nang gi zla ba lta bur/ rje blon 'bangs dang bcas pa thams cad kyis mngon sum
du mthong bar gyur te/ dga' zhing mgu la yi rangs bar gyur to/ /de ltar dga' ston rgya chen po mdzad nas/ bod 'bangs thams cad dang mthun par/ glu gar la sogs pa ltad mo
bsam gyis mi khyab par mdzad do/ /de'i dus su rgyal po dga' ston gyi gdan sar rin po che'i khri steng na bzhugs pa las/ yar la bzhengs te/ tshangs pa'i

dbyangs lta bu'i gsungs phyung nas/ rgyal po dgyes pa'i glu blangs pa/ /thugs rje'i bdag nyid dkon mchog gsum/ /thar pa'i lam ston spyan ras gzigs/ / gus pas yid kyis gsol
ba 'debs/ /bkra shis glu la dgongs su gsol/ / de ring mdun gyi nam mkha' la/ /sangs rgyas byang chub sems dpa' rnams/ / sprin phung lta bur bzhugs pa mthong / /bkra shis
rab gnas lhun gyis grub/ / tshangs pa la sogs lha rnams kyis/ /sil snyan rol mo'i sgra yang 'khrol/ /me tog padma'i char bab pas/ /bkra shis rab gnas lhun gyis grub/ /sangs
rgyas bstan pa'i rgyal mtshan btsugs/ /nag po'i phyogs las rnam par rgyal/ /bdud dpung bcom pa'i mthu dpal gyis/ /bkra shis rab gnas lhun gyis grub/ / dam pa chos kyi
rnga chen brdung / /dug lnga'i gti mug rang sar zhi/ /dkon mchog gsum gyi rnga sgra yis/ /bkra shis rab gnas lhun gyis grub/ /de ring skyid pa'i nyi ma shar/ /rang dbang
med pa'i dga' sems skyes/ /'dod rgu'i longs spyod char bzhin babs/ /bkra shis rab gnas lhun gyis grub/ /yi dam lha yi bkra shis kyis/ /srong btsan sgam po bkra shis pas/
/bkra shis glu ru blangs pa yin// nga yi bod 'bangs rnams la bkra shis shog /ces gsungs pa dang / btsun mo dang blon po bod 'bangs dang bcas pa thams cad dga' zhing mgu la
yi rangs par gyur nas/ rgyal po la phyag byas shing mchod pa phul lo/ /de nas yang rgyal pos brag lha klu sbugs su lha khang bzhengs te/ rten gyi gtso bo thub pa brag lha
mgon po/ de'i g.yas na shA ri'i bu dang / g.yon na mau gal gyi bu/ de'i g.yas na byams pa/ g.yon na spyan ras gzigs te/ gtso 'khor lnga brag la gsal

bar byon na'ang / ma 'ongs pa'i sems can bsod nams bsog pa'i phyir du/ bal po'i lha bzos 'bur du brkos/ bskor khang brag la brko ba la/ bod 'bangs rnams kyis legs par brkos
te/ tshwa la drug cu bed yod pa'i skabs su| brag phye bre re phed pa la/ rgyal pos tshwa bre re brngan par byin/ bre phyed tsam phed kyang / brag phye dang tshwa brje po
byas te/ lha khang du lha'i ri mo la sogs pa legs par tshar nas rab tu gnas pa mdzad do/ /lha sa rnam gnyis dang / mtha' 'dul dang yang 'dul gyi gtsug lag khang la sogs
pa legs par tshar nas rab tu gnas pa mdzad pa'i le'u ste bco lnga pa'o// //bcu drug phan pa dang bde ba 'byung ba'i phyir/ gter sbas pa dang bod 'bangs thams cad chos la
bkod par mdzad pa'i skor/ de nas rgya mo bza' dang bal mo bza' gnyis la sras ma 'khrungs par/ zhang zhung bza' bya ba khab tu bzhes/ de la sras ma 'khrungs/ des thim bu skog
pa'i lha khang bzhengs/ 'di lcags kha khong na yod/ de nas ru yong bza' bya ba khab tu bzhes/ de la sras ma 'khrungs/ des mig mangs tshal gyi lha khang bzhengs/ 'di go
sha gling na yod/ de nas mi nyag bza' bya ba khab tu bzhes/ de la'ang sras ma 'khrungs/ des kha brag gser gyi lha khang bzhengs/ 'di mkhar sna gdong na yod/ de nas stod
lung mang gi nang nas/ mang bza' khri lcam bya ba khab tu bzhes/ de la sras gcig 'khrungs par lung bstan te/ zla ba dgu ngo bcu lon pa na/ sras gung ri gung btsan zhes pa/
rgyal po'i gdung brgyud 'gran zla dang bral ba gcig lcags mo sbrul gyi lo la brag lha bkra shis kyi gzhal yas khang du 'khrungs te/ btsas ston

rgya chen po mdzad nas thams cad dga' bar gyur to/ /yum sras de gnyis kyi thugs dam du yer pa'i gnas ri brag gi dbyibs ni 'phags ma sgrol ma bzhugs pa 'dra ba'i pang du lha
khang dang mchod rten bzhengs te/ rab tu gnas pa mdzad nas ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang dang / bstan pa'i srog rtsa gcig par yab kyis smon lam btab bo/ /de nas
rgyal pos bod 'bangs rnams dge ba bcu'i khrims la gnas par mdzad pa'i phyir du/ skrag cing 'jigs pa'i khrims rar 'chas te/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la gnod pa byas pa dang
/ bod khrims las 'gal ba byas pa rnams la chad pa gcod pa yin no zhes bsgrags nas sprul pa mdzad de/ mi ma yin rnams la bcing ba dang / brdeg pa dang / mig 'don pa dang
/ sgyid pa gcod pa la sogs pa mdzad de/ don la grub pa med kyang / thams cad dngangs skrag bskyed pa'i thabs mdzad nas/ dge bcu'i khrims la bkod do/ /de'i tshe li yul lcang
ra smug po na/ dge tshul gnyis kyis 'phags pa 'jam dpal lo brgyad kyi bar du bsgrubs pas/ ma 'grub par nam mkha' nas sgra byung ste/ dge tshul khyed gnyis dang 'jam dbyangs
las 'brel med pas dngos grub brnyes par dka'/ khyed gnyis kyi lha 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs yin pas/ 'phags pa de da lta bod kha ba can gyi rgyal khams na| bod kyi
rgyal po ru sku sprul yod/ der song dang zhal dngos su mjal bar yod do zhes lung bstan te mi snang bar gyur to/ /de thos pa tsam gyis dge tshul gnyis po'i lus kyi ba spu
rab tu g.yos par gyur to/ /lus dang srog la mi blta bar rgyags phye khur nas bod du 'ongs so/ /der stod lung mda' brgal ba'i

'phrang la slebs pa dang / chu'i 'gram na mi'i ro mgo med pa dang / mig med pa mang po bya khyis za gyin 'dug pa mthong ngo / /der dge tshul gnyis the tshom du gyur te| bod
kyi mi la gtam byas nas/ rgyal po gang na bzhugs/ ro 'di rnams la ci byung ba yin byas pas/ bod kyi mi na re/ rgyal po lha sa na bzhugs/ ro 'di rnams khrims las 'gal ba
la rgyal pos chad pa bcad pa yin zer bas dge tshul gnyis log lta skyes te/ spyan ras gzigs bdud du 'dug pa/ mi 'di tsam gsod pa/ nged rang gnyis log la 'dong zer te log go
/der rgyal pos khong gnyis kyi bsam pa mkhyen nas/ blon po 'bri se ru gong ston la/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ rta zhon la mgyogs par song shig stod lung mda' na rab tu byung
ba'i rtags mgo la skra med pa/ gos ngur smrig gru bzhi gon pa'i mi gnyis nga'i drung du 'ong rgyu yin pa log lta skyes nas phyir log song yod pas/ zhi ba'i thabs kyis 'dir
khrid shog gsung ngo / /der blon pos rjes zin te/ khong gnyis shin tu skrag par gyur pa la/ zhi ba'i gtam smras nas rgyal po'i drung du khrid 'ongs so/ / der rgyal pos
dge tshul gnyis la phyag mdzad de/ de nas rgyal pos zhal 'dzum pa dang bcas te/ dge tshul khyed gnyis kyis bod du ci la 'ong gsungs pas/ dge tshul gnyis na re/ nged gnyis
li'i yul nas 'ongs pa yin te/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal lo brgyad kyi bar bsgrubs pas ma 'grub par nam mkha' nas sgra byung ste khyod gnyis kyi lha 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs
yin pas/ 'phags pa de da lta bod kha ba can gyi rgyal khams na rgyal po zhig tu sprul yod/ der song dang zhal dngos su mjal bar yod gsungs pas/ nged gnyis kyis lus dang

srog la ma bltas par bod du 'ong ba yin/ lam kha na mi ro mang po 'dug pas bod kyi mi la dris pas/ rgyal pos khrims las 'gal ba la chad pa bcad pa yin zer bas/ nged gnyis skrag
nas phyir log pa yin zer ro/ /der rgyal pos khong gnyis la bza' btung gis tshim par byas nas/ dbu'i thod phud de/ a mi dhe ba'i zhal bstan nas/ nga ni bod kyi rgyal
po thugs rje chen po yin/ ngas rgyal srid bzung nas da lta phan la sems can la phan btags nas/ thar pa byang chub kyi lam la 'khod pa ma gtogs/ gnod pa khab rtse gang yang
skyel ma myong / bod kyi mi 'di rnams spre'u dang brag srin las chad pa yin pas/ drag po'i sprul pa byas pa yin gsungs te/ se gol brdab pas/ ro rnams 'ja' yal ba bzhin
song ngo / /der dge tshul gnyis dad cing gus par gyur te/ rgyal po chen po nged gnyis lam thag ring nas dka' ba spyad 'ongs pa chos go sla ba'i phyir/ don gsum la 'dus pa'i
gdams pa zhig zhu zhus pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas dge tshul gnyis nyon cig chos thams cad kyi rtsa ba hril gyis dril na don gsum la 'dus te/ lus kyi sgo nas srog gcod pa
dang / ma byin par len pa dang / mi tshangs par spyod pa la sogs pa spangs te/ dkon mchog gsum gyi drung du phyag dang bskor ba gyis la bde 'gro mtho ris thob pa'i rten
du tshul khrims kyi nor bu gces par 'dzin cig bslab pa rin po che'i rgyan dang nam du yang mi 'bral bar gyis shig ngag gi sgo nas rdzun phra ma/ tshig rtsub mo smra ba la
sogs pa spangs te/ sangs rgyas thams cad kyi dgongs pa gcig tu bsdus pa'i ngo bo/ chos thams cad kyi rtsa ba bsdus pa'i snying po/ dge legs dang yon tan thams

cad kyi gter mdzod/ phan bde'i dngos grub thams cad kyi rtsa ba/ gsung mchog yi ge drug pa la bzlas brjod gyis shig yid kyi sgo nas brnab sems/ gnod sems/ log par lta ba la
sogs spangs te/ dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su 'gro zhing / khams gsum rig drug na gnas pa'i sems can thams cad rang gi pha mar ma gyur pa gcig kyang med pas/ de rnams kyi
sdug bsngal bzod thabs med pa rnams rang gi rgyud thog tu len pa'i 'dun pa drag po dang bcas shing / rang gi phan bde gang yod de rnams la ster la/ bdag bas gzhan gces bsgom
pa'i bsam pa bzang po dang ldan te/ mdor na byams snying rje byang chub kyi sems rin po che dang skad cig kyang ma bral bar gyis shig chos bzang las bsam bzang lhag
pa yin no/ /don 'di gsum dang ldan na tshe gcig lus gcig la sangs rgyas par 'gyur ro/ /don 'di gsum rang rgyud la med na/ bka' mdo rgyud lung man ngag thams cad blo la yod
kyang / kha chos yin zhing snying po med gsungs so/ /de nas rgyal pos dge tshul de gnyis la thugs rje chen po'i chos skor gsum dang / mdo padma dkar po dang / yi ge drug
pa'i phan yon rnams gsungs nas/ thar pa byang chub kyi lam la 'khod par mdzad do/ /de nas dge tshul gnyis po/ dga' zhing mgu la yi rangs par gyur nas/ rgyal po'i zhabs
la phyag byas te/ 'di skad ces gsol to/ /kye ma chos rgyal sprul pa'i sku// Arya pA lo thugs rje can/ /yul du 'gro bas skyel ma zhu/ /zer bas rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyed gnyis
gegs med par skad cig la yul du sleb par 'dod dam gsungs pas/ dge tshul gnyis na re/ ci nas kyang dka' tshegs med par

yul du sleb par 'dod lags zer bas/ rgyal pos khong gnyis kyi thu bar bye ma bre re blugs nas gser 'gyur gyi byin gyis brlabs te/ khong gnyis kyi mgo la phyag bzhag nas yo byad
gang yod sngas su chug la/ khyed rang gnyis kyi yul yid la dran pa gyis la nyol cig gsung ngo / /der khong gnyis kyis de ltar byas nas nyal bas gnyid thum pa zhig song
ba dang / khong rang gnyis kyi yul na sleb 'dug go /thu ba'i bye ma de gser du song / skye ba phyi mar de gnyis kyis dgra bcom pa'i 'bras bu thob par gyur to/ /de nas sras
gung ri gung btsan dgung lo bcu gsum bzhes nas/ rgyal srid bzung btsun mo khab tu bzhes pas/ sras mang srong mang btsan bya ba me pho khyi'i lo la 'khrungs so/ /gung
ri gung btsan gyis rgyal srid lo lnga bzung / dgung lo bco brgyad bzhes dus/ po ta la ru sku gshegs so/ /gung ri gung btsan yab kyi gong du 'das/ /de yi bang so don mkhar
mda' ru brtsig /gral ni gnam ri srong btsan g.yon na yod/ /ming ni gung chen gung ri lags so skad/ /de nas slar yab rgyal pos rgyal srid bzung ste| bde skyid dang ldan par
mdzad do/ /de nas yang rgyal po'i thugs la nga'i ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang dang / rgya stag ra mo che'i gtsug lag khang gnyis la/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa
ji srid gnas kyi bar du yon tan dpag tu med pa dang ldan dgos te/ rin po che'i gling lta bu sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' dang / dpa' bo dang / dpa' mo ye shes kyi
mkha' 'gro ma re yang tha mal pa'i gzugs su sprul nas rgyun du gnas pa dang / bod yul gyi gtsug lag khang thams cad las mngon par mtho zhing mtha' yas pa'i yon tan du ma

dang ldan pa/ gdul bya longs spyod nam mkha' dang mnyam shing / gang la gang 'dod yid bzhin du 'byung ba/ mtha'i nor thams cad gnas 'dir 'du zhing / mtha' bzhi las rnam par
rgyal ba/ bod yul na 'gran zla dang bral zhing / 'od dang 'od zer phyogs bcur khyab pa/ snyan pa dang grags pas ni sa'i steng thams cad khyab ste/ byin rlabs ni nyi zla'i
'od dang mtshungs/ rin po che dang / nor dang / 'bru dang / gser dang / dngul dang / dbyig dang / rgyan dang / gos dang / zang zing gi long spyod ni char bzhin du 'bab
pa/ yon tan du ma dang ldan par byed pa la sa'i yon tan bltas nas gter sbed dgos te/ de yang dper na yid bzhin gyi nor bu 'dod rgu 'byung ba'i rgya mtsho'i 'gram na/ grong
dang grong khyer ci yod kyang / de'i mthu la brten te/ 'byor pa dang ldan pa yod pa ltar/ rin po che'i gter yod pa'i gnas der yang / 'byor pa longs spyod rang bzhin gyis
'ong bas/ ma 'ongs pa'i bod 'bangs rnams kyi don du gter sbas pa ni/ ka ba bum pa can dang nye ba'i sar/ dam pa chos kyi gter sbas so/ /de'i yon tan ni bod kyi yul 'dir
ma 'ongs pa'i dus su/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa nyi ma shar ba bzhin 'byung ste/ dam chos la longs spyod par 'gyur ro/ /ka ba shing lo can dang nye ba'i sar/ /gser dngul
rin po che'i gter sbas so/ /de sbas pa'i yon tan ni/ mtha'i nor thams cad dbus su 'du zhing / gser dngul la longs spyod par 'gyur ro/ /ka ba sbrul mgo can dang nye ba'i sar/
drag sngags mthu'i gter sbas so/ /de sbas pa'i yon tan ni/ mtha' dmag dang / bgegs dang log 'dren thams cad mi 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /ka ba seng mgo can dang nye ba'i

sar/ byol song phyugs kyi g.yang yig rnams sbas so/ /de sbas pa'i yon tan ni/ bzhon phyugs 'phel ba dang / dkar thog bcud dang ldan par 'gyur ro/ /rin po che ratna de ba/ gzi'i
sgrom bur bcug nas dar zab sna lngas dril la dzambha la'i 'og tu sbas so/ /de'i yon tan ni/ rgyan dang / gos dang / nor dang / 'bru la sogs pa gang la ci 'dod pa thams
cad 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /rin po che stag sha de ba sbrul gyi lpags pas gtums nas klu khang du sbas so/ /de'i yon tan ni/ lo phyugs rtag tu legs shing char chu dus su
'bab ste/ sa bdag klu'i gnod pa mi 'byung bar 'gyur ro/ /baiDUrya'i lhung bzed zas sna dpag tu med pas bkang ste| gnod sbyin khang par sbas so/ /de'i yon tan ni/ bza' btung
gi longs spyod gang la ci 'dod pa thams cad 'byung zhing / zas bcud dang ldan par 'gyur ro/ /ra sa'i gtsug lag khang la zhig ral byung na gso ba dang / mchod pa rgyun
ring por bya ba'i phyir/ gser dang dngul dang rin po che sna tshogs las zangs chen po zhig bkang ste/ dkyil 'khor chen po'i 'og tu sbas so/ /las dang skal bar ldan pa'i gang
zag la smon lam btab bo/ /gzhan yang sa cha 'od dang ldan pa dang / char chu dus su 'bab ste/ 'bru sna smin pa/ than pa dang / sad dang / ser ba dang / btsa' dang / mu
ge mi 'byung ba dang / nad yams dang / mtha' dmag gi gnod pa mi 'byung zhing / dus dang gnas skabs thams cad du bkra shis shing / dge legs kyis khyab par bya ba'i phyir/
rin po che gser dngul la sogs pa rnams rin po che'i snod du dar zab sna tshogs kyis dril nas bcug gnod sbyin khang pa dang / klu khang dang / lha khang gi nang skor thams
cad

du sbas so/ /'di dag ni zur tsam yin gyis/ gter sbas lugs rnams rgyas par shes 'dod na/ rgyal po bka'i thang yig la gzigs shig de nas rgyal po'i zhal nas/ gter 'di rnams sbas
pa'i yon tan ni/ nga'i gtsug lag khang 'di la snyan pa dang grags pa ni nyi zlas slebs pa'i gnas su khyab ste/ 'dzam bu gling na 'gran zla dang bral ba yin no/ /gdul bya
dang zhabs tog mtha' nas rgyas te/ mtha' mi thams cad dbang du 'dus nas/ dpal 'byor nam mkha' dang mnyam pa yin no/ /ma 'ongs pa'i dus su nga'i dbon sras dang / btsun
mo blon po bod 'bangs thams cad kyis gtsug lag khang bzhengs par 'dod na/ nga'i ra sa 'phrul snang gi gtsug lag khang 'dir sa phud dang / rdo phud bskyal nas rab gnas lhun
gyis grub cing bdud dang log 'dren gyi bgegs med par bkra shis shing yon tan du ma dang ldan par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs so/ /de nas rgyal pos lha sa ne'u thang du dbon sras
mang srong mang btsan gyi dbu la phyag bzhag nas/ spang skong phyag brgya pa dang / mdo padma dkar po dang / dam chos zla ba sgron ma dang / spyan ras gzigs kyi sgrub
skor bshad rgyud rnams dang / ma 'ongs pa gab pa mngon du phyung ba dang / lha sar zhabs tog byas pa/ phyag dang mchod pa bskor ba byas pa/ mthong thos dran reg gi yon tan
bstan pa/ phyi'i rag gso ba dang / nang gi lha la zhabs tog byas pa la phan yon yod pa rnams legs par gsungs te/ sras kyis yi ger bris nas gnod sbyin khang par gter du
sbas so// gzhan yang nga nas gdung rabs lnga pa na/ rgyal po khri dang lde zhes bya ba 'byung ste/ de'i dus su rgya gar nas paNDi ta mang po byon nas dam pa'i chos thams
cad

bsgyur zhing yang dag par gtan la 'bebs/ gtsug lag khang mang po bzhengs/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar zhing rgyas par 'gyur te/ rab tu byung ba bslab pa gsum gyi rgyan gyis
rab tu mdzes pa/ ngur smrig gi rgyal mtshan gsol ba mang po 'byung bar 'dug ste/ nga'i dbon sras rnams kyi dbu'i mchod gnas byed/ 'tsho ba blang nas sbyor phan bde dang
dge legs thams cad 'byung bar 'gyur ro zhes gsungs pas/ blon po mgar gyis de ma thag tu zangs kyi byang bu la bris nas/ 'ching phu'i dkor mdzod du sbas so/ /gzhan yang phyi
blon/ nang blon/ bod 'bangs kyi skyes pa dang bud med/ byis pa yan la rim pa bzhin du 'jig rten la dgos pa'i zhal gdams dpag tu med pa gsungs nas/ thugs rje chen po'i
bskyed rim gyis/ yi ge drug pa'i chos la bkod do/ /'di yang blon po 'bri se ru gong ston gyis/ ma 'ongs pa'i bod 'bangs rnams la phan pa'i phyir yi ger bris bzhag go /gzhan
yang rgyal po nyid kyi rnam thar rnams la rgyas 'bring gsum du mdzad/ shog dril gsum byas nas ka ba bum pa can gyi 'og tu sbas te/ las dang skal bar ldan pa'i gang zag
la smon lam btab bo/ /de nas rgyal po dang btsun mo'i mdzad pa thams cad yongs su rdzogs te/ bod kha ba can pa'i re zhig ltos pa'i pha ma lta bu| 'gro ba sgrol ba'i ded
dpon lta bu/ dgos 'dod 'byung ba'i nor bu lta bu/ mun pa sel ba'i sgron me lta bu/ nye ring med pa'i nyi zla lta bur mdzad de/ las thabs mkhas pas phyi na dgra med/ bka'
drin bzang pos nang gi 'bangs rnams skyongs/ mnga' 'og gi bod 'bangs thams cad 'byor pa dang ldan zhing / dga' bde la longs spyod do/ /phan pa dang bde ba thams cad 'byung
bar bya ba'i

phyir/ gter sbas pa dang bod 'bangs thams cad chos la bkod par mdzad pa'i le'u ste bcu drug pa'o// //bcu bdun/ rgyal po yab yum gyi mdzad pa yongs su rdzogs te/ rang byon bcu
gcig zhal gyi thugs kar thim pa'i skor/ oM ma Ni padme hU~M/ lha thugs rje chen po la phyag 'tshal lo/ /thugs rje chen po'i sprul pa chos skyong ba'i rgyal po srong btsan
sgam po la/ sras gung srong gung btsan gyis/ nangs par nyi ma shar ba dang dbu rtse'i yang thog tu yab rgyal po chen po la rang gi na bza' la bzhugs gdan byas nas zhal
zas mang po drangs/ phyag dang bskor ba mang du byas nas zhu ba 'di skad ces gsol to/ /e ma ho/ sangs rgyas kun gyi phrin las/ /snang ba mtha' yas kyi thugs rje/ /bde ba
