can gyi pho nya/ /bod 'bangs yongs kyi skyabs gnas/ /bdag cag kun la thugs rjes gzigs pa yi/ /rgyal ba'i sku dang tha mal mjal/ /zab mo'i thugs dgongs snang mod kyang /
/chos nyid don gyi thugs rje de/ rgyal ba'i thugs la mi gab par/ gab pa mngon du phyung nas ni/ /rang snang yul med bstan du gsol/ /blo 'das byar med bstan du gsol/ /ma
bcos ngang nas bstan nas kyang / /byar med ngang gis gnas pa la/ /sku gsum shugs las 'char ba yi/ /bdag cag blo la sbyar du gsol/ /zhes phyag 'tshal te zhus pa dang / der
yab rgyal pos bka' stsal pa/ lha sras chen po nyon cigabadag ni sangs rgyas kun gyi phrin las yin/ /snang ba mtha' yas drung du dam yang bcas/ /byang chub sems kyi bod 'bangs
don la 'ong / /nga dang rgyal ba gnyis su med/ /'gro ba nga yi gdul bya yin/ khyed kun 'phags pa'i byin

rlabs yin/ /rgyal ba'i dgongs rgyud zab mo rnams/ /'phags pa'i lam steg yin mod kyang / /chos nyid don gyi thugs rje de/ /blo dman rnams la bstan par mi 'os kyang / /brtse
ba'i sems kyis gab pa mngon phyung 'di/ /ma rtogs sgro dang skur ba'i gzhi/ /skyabs med rnams la ye gsang chod/ /tsitta snying gi dkyil du chongs/ /chos nyid zad par skyel
ba yang / /nga yis legs par bstan gyis nyon// sna tshogs dag kyang rang snang yin/ /yul med de ni blo las 'das/ /blo 'das de ni byar med yin/ /ji bzhin pa yi ngang gnas
yin/ /gnas pa med par lhod pa'i mchog /de ltar go ba'i gang zag gis/ /mtha' bral spros pa chod pa la/ / lta ba'i ming du btags pa yin/ /rang gsal 'dzin pa stong pa la/ /sgom
pa ming du btags pa yin/ /don dang bral ba med pa la/ /spyod pa ming du btags pa yin/ /spang blang 'dzin pa zhig pa la/ /'bras bu ming du btags pa yin/ /rtsol med 'gro
don byed pa la/ /thugs rje ming du btags pa yin/ /de la skyo dub med pa la/ /chen po ming du btags pa yin/ /'gro don mdzad kyang skyon ma gos/ / 'phags pa ming du btags
pa yin/ /snying rje dbang du 'dus pa la/ /rgyal po ming du btags pa yin/ /'gro ba'i kha lo snyoms pa la/ /srong btsan ming du btags pa yin/ /blo la gang phan bshad pa la/
/gdams ngag ming du btags pa yin/ /brjed tho shul du bzhag pa la/ /bka' brgyud ming du btags pa yin// 'gro ba dang ba 'dren pa la/ /gtsug lag ming du btags pa yin/ /rnam
rtog rang sar grol ba la/ /sangs rgyas ming du btags pa yin/ /'gro ba lam du 'dzud pa la/ /dam chos ming du btags pa yin/ /byar med blo la sbyor ba la/ /

dge 'dun ming du btags pa yin/ /rtsol med rang lugs gnas pa la/ /byar med ming du btags pa yin/ /tha mal rtog pa bsgyur ba la/ /bskyed rim ming du btags pa yin/ /blo yi khrid
thabs sna tshogs pa/ /chos spyod ming du btags pa yin/ /rtsa bral nang du shes pa la/ /go ba ming du btags pa yin/ /don go gcig las med pa la/ /nyag gcig ming du btags
pa yin/ /du ma ngo bo gcig pa la/ /chos sku ming du btags pa yin/ /dag snang lha ru snang ba la/ /longs sku ming du btags pa yin/ /sna tshogs thabs kyis 'dren pa la/ /sprul
sku ming du btags pa yin/ /rtog med rang sa zin pa la/ /mngon 'gyur ming du btags pa yin/ /btags pa thams cad ming yin gyis/ /ming ni 'dzin pa med par zhog /bsam pa thams
cad blo yin gyis/ /blo yi byed pa zhog la spong / /zhog ces bya ba tshig yin gyis/ /tshig gi 'dzin pa bor la thong / /thong zhes bya ba blo yin gyis/ /blo yi byed pa
dbyings su sbos/ /sbed pa bya ba bzang rtog yin/ / bzang ngan med par khad de ba/ /gab sbas med par lha nge ba/ /'gro 'ong med par gsal le ba/ /spang blang med par lhug
ge ba/ /phyogs ris med par phyam me ba/ /btang bzung med par khyil le ba/ /gsal 'grib med pa lhang nge ba/ / brjed yeng med par tur re ba/ /gtang bzhag med par wal le ba/
/blo las 'das pa'i yul la ltos/ /tshig las 'das pa'i don la ltos/ /bzang ngan med pa'i yul la ltos/ /phyi nang med par sems la ltos/ /pho mo med pa'i sems la ltos/ /gnyis
'dzin bral ba'i don la ltos/ /don zhes bya ba blo las 'das/ / 'das pa'i rjes su ma 'brang bar/ /blo tshig bral ba'i ngang la ltos/ /bltas pas

mthong ba'i yul med kyis/ /ma bltas bzhag pas chos nyid mthong / /ma bsgrub bzhag pas sems nyid grub/ /ma bzung ma glod rang sar grol/ /de ltar mthong ba'i gang zag la/ /'khor
'das gnyis su ngas ma mthong / /dge sdig gnyis su ngas ma mthong / /bzang ngan gnyis su ngas ma mthong / /rtag chad gnyis su ngas ma mthong / /pho mo gnyis su ngas ma
mthong / /bde sdug gnyis su ngas ma mthong // yin min gnyis su ngas ma mthong / /nye ring gnyis su ngas ma mthong / /mtho dman gnyis su ngas ma mthong / /gsal 'grib gnyis
su ngas ma mthong / / mthong ba med pa'i rang nyid nas/ /sna tshogs shar ba rang nyid yin/ /sna tshogs 'gag pa med par zhog /sna tshogs 'dzin pa med par zhog /sna tshogs
spang blang med par zhog /sna tshogs 'dzin bral chos sku yin/ /ma 'gags gsal ba longs sku yin/ /sna tshogs bral ba sprul sku yin/ /tha mal rtog med chos sku yin// chos
nyid 'dod pa tha mal yin/ /blo las 'das pa de nyid yin/ /'dod pa bral na don dang bral/ /gnyis 'dzin grol na gnas su rtogs/ /spang blang med na dngos grub thob/ /'gro don
byed na phrin las rdzogs/ /blo thag chod na 'gro sar phyin/ /phyin pa med na brdol ba yin/ /de lta bu yi gang zag la/ /rig pa thams cad rang rig yin/ /shes pa thams cad
rang shes yin/ /grol ba thams cad rang grol yin/ /gsal ba thams cad rang gsal yin/ /stong pa thams cad rang stong yin/ /'dug pa thams cad rang 'dug yin/ /gnas pa thams cad
rang gnas yin/ /bde ba thams cad rang bde yin/ /sdug bsngal thams cad rang sdug yin/ /thams cad rang rig rang snang yin/ /sgom du med pas bsam

du med/ /rgyud la bya med yengs su med/ /bzhag rgyu med de btang rgyu med/ / brjed rgyu med de nor rgyu med/ /ye shes de la rgyun chad med/ /ting nge 'dzin la thun mtshams
med/ /dmigs pa la yang btang bzung med/ /rnam rtog la yang bzang ngan med/ /yid yul la yang phyi nang med/ /dngos med la yang phyi nang med/ /re dogs spangs na skyon dang
bral/ /'dod pa med pas thob pa med/ / rtsol ba med pas skyon rnams sangs/ /'bras bu la re mkhan med pas sangs rgyas kyi dgongs pa zhig bsam brjod blo las 'das pas smra ba'i
ngag dang bral/ de ltar du rang dbang thob tsa na/ brgyud pa rang gis zin/ grol cha nang nas rnyed/ gzung 'dzin mtshan ma zhig snang srid bka' brgyud du shes/ byed spyod
chos spyod du 'gro/ mthong thos sku gsum du byon/ ye shes nang nas brtol/ nyon mongs kun rang sar dag dad gus rang la tshud do/ /'khor 'das kyi rtsa ba rang rig tu shes/
skyid sdug gsal 'debs su shes/ bdag 'dzin chos skur grol lo/ /gzhi mthong bas lta ba med/ rtsad chod pas sgom du med/ rang sa zin pas sgrub tu med/ rang sems ngo shes
pas sangs rgyas med do/ /shes rab rang brdol du byon pas/ wal le brjed med du 'dug pa/ sna tshogs 'gag med du grol ba/ tshor ba rjes med du sangs pas/ rig pa glan sar chags
pas/ chos sku gcer mthong du grol ba/ rig pa rkyang ded du 'dug pas gnyis su med pa'i sku| rang snang chen po'i ngang la lus so/ /rang byung du yin pas lhun grub tu byung
/ rang gsal yin pas gting gsal du shar/ rang snang yin pas 'od gsal du snang / rang rig yin pas chos skur byung / rang grol yin pas zangs thal du byung

ngo | |de yang rang gis ma byas par gzhan byed dam/ rang la bsam du med par gzhan la mtshon du rnyed dam/ rang ma rig par sems can thul lam/ 'du 'bral med par btsal bas rnyed
dam/ phyin pa med par bsdad pas zin nam/ dngos po med par lag tu lon nam/ bstan rgyu med par mig gis mthong ngam/ da lta nga la yod pa'i steng la tshol lam/ gsal ba'i
steng la lta'am/ grol ba'i steng la bshigs sam/ dag pa'i steng la 'khru'am/ ngoms pa'i steng la 'thung ngam/ 'grang pa'i steng la za'am/ dros pa'i steng la sreg gam/ shes
pa'i steng la 'thams sam/ de ltar sems la rgyu rkyen bral bas rtsol sgrub kyi blo dang bral te/ dngos med la gnyen pos bcos su 'dug gam/ long med kyi snang ba ma thos pas/
rtag chad kyi snang ba rang sar dag gnyis 'dzin rang sar grol bas re dogs kyi mtha' spang / zhen 'dzin nang nas grol bas skye med rang sa zin/ rtog med nang nas mthong
bas dgra bgegs rang sar thul lo/ /'o de ltar du rig pa rgya yan gnyen po med pa la ye shes rang snang gi spyod pa zer ba yin no/ /rtog med rang lugs gnas pa la spang blang
med pa zer ba yin no/ /ye shes nang nas shar ba la rnam rtog rang grol zer ba yin no/ /yin min blo las 'das pa la dgag sgrub bral ba zer ba yin no/ /'bad rtsol ngos zin
pa la chos nyid klong brdol zer ba yin no/ /lhun grub skye ba med pa la 'bras bu rang shar zer ba yin no/ /'o de ltar du go ba dang rtogs pa dus mnyam/ shes pa dang grol
ba dus mnyam/ gsal ba dang mthong ba dus mnyam/ 'byar dang reg pa dus mnyam/ brlan pa dang gsher ba dus mnyam/ 'o de ltar shes pa'i gang zag gis/ lta ba

la phyogs ris med kyis nam mkha' gon/ sgom pa la gsal 'grib med kyis nyi ma khur/ spyod pa la thog brdug med kyis rlung la zhon/ 'bras bu la blang dor med kyis gser gling ltos/
de ltar rtogs pa'i rnal 'byor la/ lta ba la lta rgyu gda' ye/ bsgom pa la bsgom rgyu gda' ye/ spyod pa la spyod rgyu gda' ye/ 'bras bu la bsgrub rgyu gda' ye/ des na
rig pa gshis thog tu sgyel/ mtshan ma rang grol du thong / phyi nang gi 'dzin pa shigs/ bzang ngan gyi blang dor spangs/ chags zhen gyi 'dzin pa khrol/ bzang 'dod kyi nga
rgyal thong / 'gran sems kyi phrag dog khrol/ zhe sdang gi me chen gsod/ gti mug gi ma rig pa sangs/ byar med kyi ngang la yengs med du zhog gnyis 'dzin gyi blo ni nam
mkha'i dbyings su rgyas thob/ don la bsgom rgyu med kyis rang sar zhog 'o de lta bu'i gang zag gis/ bskyed rim bsgom na yi dam lha ru 'gyur/ /rdzogs rim dran na gzung 'dzin
mtshan ma zhig /zung 'brel 'dod na bar snang 'ja' tshon ltos/ /don go mthong na tha mal chos mi ltos/ /ma mthong bar du bka' brgyud bla ma bsten/ / chos spyod byed na
rang 'dod zhen pa spangs/ /mi 'jig go cha 'dod na sgo gsum lha ru bsgyur/ /gzhan don byed na 'gro la phan sems bskyed/ /rang don bsgrubs na 'du 'dzi g.yeng ba spongs/ /dgra
bgegs 'dul na rtsa bral snying rje bskyed/ /phyi ma bde 'bras 'dod na da lta dka' ba spyod/ /'gro ba dbang du sdud na bdag bas gzhan gces kyis/ /snyom las dran na 'chi
ba mi rtag bsgom/ / chags zhen 'dzin pa byung na rmi lam sgyu ma bsgom/ /bar chad bdud kyis bred na rang sems gtan la phob/ /chos bzhin byed na chos min thams cad spong
/ /nga

dang 'grogs kyang de las med/ /sangs rgyas gzhan dang mjal yang de bas med/ /ces chos skyong ba'i rgyal pos dgongs pa mngon du phyung ba dang / de nas dus de nyid du lha sras
rje 'bangs thams cad chos nyid rang shar rang grol chen po'i gling du 'bad pa dang rtsol ba med par grol lo/ /dus de nyid du bde sdug la spang blang med/ 'khor 'das la
bzang ngan med/ 'di phyi la gdams kha med par 'phags pa rnams kyi zhal mthong bya mthong byed med par mi la mis blta ba bzhin gzigs so/ /de ltar mi thams cad rig pa rang
shar rang grol gyi dgongs pa la/ bzhag bya dang bzhag byed med par byas par gyur to/ /de nas lha sras rje 'bangs thams cad rjes su yi rangs te phyi nang gi mchod pa rgya
chen pos yab rgyal po mnyes par mdzad nas shin tu drin gzo'o/ /de nas yang dar gcig yab rgyal po nyid dgongs pa la bzhugs nas ci yang mi gsung bar/ spyan bar snang la khrol
khrol mdzad nas 'di skad gsungs so/ /ag sam rgyal sras chen po gson cig /lan cig dus kyi tha ma la/ /nga yi lha sa'i gnas gzhi 'di/ /nya 'dra sbal 'dra 'jong 'dra sprel
yang 'dra/ /rim pa bzhin du chu yis gcod par byed/ /nya 'dra rgyal ba yum gyi rang bzhin yin/ /ras ris phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dngos dang 'dra/ /rgyal bas rgyal ba'i
zhabs tog mdzad pa yin/ /nya 'dra kha ru de dag su yod pa/ /rgyal ba'i yum la reg dang khyad par med/ /de yang sngon du sbyangs pa song ba yin/ /'khor ba'i sdug bsngal mtha'
ru phyin pa yin/ /'bad pa don chen yin no bod 'bangs rnams/ /rdo bang gseg ma 'jim pa bya sgong tsam/ /gang zhig de yi phyogs su spung byed pa/ /sangs rgyas

rnams la sman pa byas pa yin/ /de yang bde ba'i lam la tshud pa yin/ /nga yi rig can rnams kyis bkur ba'i tshe/ /nya 'dra'i dus su gshog ltar bsgron pa yin/ /sbal 'dra'i dus
su zhwa ltar bkon pa yin/ /'jong 'dra'i dus su gdan ltar 'ding ba yin/ /sprel 'dra'i dus su gzugs su gyur tsa na/ /rgya chen mchod pa bshams nas ni/ /mos gus gsol 'debs
gces pa yin/ /de ltar byas nas cung zhig gnas par 'gyur/ /nang gi lha rnams gsos na phyi yi rag la phan/ /phyi yi rag rnams gsos na nang gi lha rnams dgyes/ /mchod pa bshams
shing gsol ba btab byas na/ /bod 'bangs bsam pa thams cad 'grub par 'gyur/ /dus kyi tha ma sdig spyod mang mod kyang / /nga yi lha sa mthong thos reg pa yi| |'gro ba
phal cher 'khor ba'i gnas nas thar/ /de yang 'phags pa rnams kyi thugs rje ste/ /nga yi bod 'bangs rnams kyi bsod nams yin/ /de phyir nga yi skyabs gnas pho mo rnams/ /rtsol
ba ma zhen snying stobs bskyed mdzod la/ /nga yi lha sa mthong thos reg par mdzod/ /de yang thar pa'i lam la btsug pa yin/ / skyon rnams thams cad sel bar 'dod pa dang
/ /yon tan gang zhig bsgrub par 'dod pa yi/ /nga yi lha sa zhabs tog mos byas pas/ /bsam pa thams cad yid bzhin 'grub par 'gyur/ /ji ltar 'dod pa rgyal ba rnams la zhus/
/zhes yab rgyal po chen pos lha sras la bka' stsal pa/ lha sras chen po pa/ dus lan cig lha sa la chus nyen nas/ gso dgos pa yod par 'dug pas/ de'i zhig gsos kyi theb
la/ gser dngul la sogs dkor nor rnams gter du sbos shig gsungs pa dang / de nas lha sras kyis kyang lha sar zhabs tog bya thabs

dang / gser dngul dang dkor nor la sogs pa nor mang po dus de nyid du/ gnod sbyin na ga ku be ra'i brla g.yas kyi dar sham 'og tu gter du sbas nas las dang skal bar ldan pa'i
gang zag la gtad rgya smon lam btab bo/ /des kyang lho dang nub kyi phyogs su 'gro don byed par 'gyur ro/ /rgyal po srong btsan sgam pos gab pa mngon phyung du gdams pa'o/
/de nas chos kyi rgyal po de/ dgung lo bdun cu tham pa rgyal sa bzung / rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa nyi ma shar ba lta bur mdzad/ 'dod yon
dang longs spyod kyi char pa phab/ bod 'bangs thams cad bde ba la bkod/ dgung lo brgyad cu gya gnyis pa lcags pho khyi'i lo smin drug zla ba'i tshes bcu la 'phrul snang gi
btsan khang byang mar 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs kyi drung du/ sprul pa'i rgyal po srong btsan sgam po de'i g.yas su bal mo bza'/ g.yon du rgya mo bza'/ rgyab tu mang bza'
khri lcam/ zhabs drung du dbon sras mang srong mang btsan/ mdun du blon po thon mi dang mgar gnyis/ lha khang phyi'i sgo srung la/ zhang blon sna chen po dang / sbas lcang
dpal gyi pags bzang gnyis kyis sgo bsrungs/ mchod rdzas du ma thogs te/ rgyal pos yi dam gyi drung du mchod pa phul nas smon lam btab bo| |de nas rgyal pos dbon sras
la bka' stsal pa/ rigs kyi bu ngas ni rgyal khrims chos khrims su bsgyur nas/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar bar byas/ bod 'bangs bde ba la bkod pa yin no/ khyod kyis kyang
nga'i rgyal srid 'di ma nyams par chos bzhin du skyongs shig nga'i gtsug lag khang 'di gnyis kyi zhabs tog khyod kyis gyis la/ dar du chug cig nga'i pho brang lha'i gnas
dang 'dra ba 'di'i

'dzin skyong gyis shig nga'i btsun mo dang / blon po bod 'bangs thams cad re zhing ltos pa'i pha ma lta bu gyis la/ phan pa dang bde bas khyab par gyis shig nga nas gdung rabs
lnga pa la/ /'jam dpal dbyangs kyi sprul pa ste/ /rgyal po lde zhes bya ba 'byung / /des kyang dam chos rgyas par byed/ /de nas gdung rabs gnyis pa la/ /phyag na rdo
rje'i sprul pa ste/ /rgyal po khri zhes bya ba 'byung / /des kyang dam chos rgyas par byed/ /de nas bdud kyi sprul pa ste/ /rgyal po dud 'gro'i ming can 'byung / /glang dar
ma yin/ de yi thugs la gdon gsol nas/ /lha khang sgyel zhing dam chos bsnub/ /sde snod 'dzin pa'i srog kyang gcod/ /chos mdzad thams cad bsad cing bcom/ /glegs bam thams
cad me la bsregs/ / sangs rgyas bstan pa'i dkrug shing des/ /bla ma slob dpon bran du bskul/ / rab byung btsun pa chos dang phral/ /dge bshes rnams la shan pa bcol/ /
sangs rgyas na bza' chu la bskur/ /rten gsum mchod cha rdo yis brdungs/ / chos kyi ming yang med par byed/ /de nas yer pa'i brag khung na/ /phyag na rdo rje'i sprul pa ste/
/dpal zhes bya ba'i dge slong gis/ /sdig can rgyal po sgrol bar 'gyur/ /de nas lo skor brgyad kyi bar/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa med par gyur/ / e ma sems can snying re rje/
/nga yi yi dam 'di rnams kyang / /gtsug lag khang 'dir gter bzhin sbed/ /de nas lnga brgya tha ma la/ /sangs rgyas bstan pa'i me ro zhig /mdo khams sgang nas longs par
'gyur/ kha ba can pa'i sems can la| |mar me 'chi khar gsal ba bzhin/ /bstan pa dar zhing rgyas par 'gyur/ / dad can mchod pa 'bul ba dang / /phyag 'tshal bskor ba byed par
'gyur/ /

rab byung btsun pa mang po dang / /sangs rgyas bstan pa dar bar 'gyur/ /zhes gsungs te byams pa'i ting nge 'dzin la bzhugs so/ /'di dag ni zur tsam yin gyis/ ma 'ongs lung
bstan gyi zhal gdams rgyas par jo bo rjes gter nas thon pa'i ka khol ma che ba na gsal lo/ /de nas dar cig lon pa na/ rgyal po'i zhal nas nga'i phyi nang gi blon po bod 'bangs
rnams nga rgyal po srong btsan sgam po dang mjal bar 'dod do zer du 'ong gi nga dang 'phrad par 'dod na 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs la gsol ba thob cig nga dang 'phrad
pa dang khyad med do gsungs so/ /yang bal mo bza' khri btsun gyis kyang / zhal phyir log mdzad nas/ bod 'bangs blo nye ba rnams nga bal mo bza' khri btsun dang mjal bar
'dod do zer du 'ong gi nga dang 'phrad par 'dod na jo mo khro gnyer can la gsol ba thob cig nga dang 'phrad pa dang khyad med do gsungs so/ /yang rgya mo kong jo zhal phyir
log mdzad nas/ bod 'bangs nga la zhen che zhing dga' ba rnams la/ rgya mo kong jo dang mjal bar 'dod do zer du 'ong gi nga dang 'phrad par 'dod na rje btsun sgrol ma
la gsol ba thob cig nga dang 'phrad pa dang khyad med do gsungs so/ /der blon po mgar gyis rgyal po chen po 'di tsam pa'i zhal gdams gsungs pa yab yum gsum gar 'byon zhus
pas/ nged gsum po thag ring du mi 'gro gsungs te/ rgyal po yar la bzhengs nas/ phyag g.yas pa bal mo bza' khri btsun la reg pas/ khri btsun me tog utpal dkar po zhig tu
gyur nas/ rgyal po'i sku phrag g.yas su thim mo/ /phyag g.yon rgya mo kong jo la reg pas/ kong jo me tog utpal sngon po zhig tu gyur nas/ rgyal po'i sku phrag g.yon

du thim mo/ /de nas rgyal po rang byon bcu gcig zhal gyi drung du phyin te/ 'phags pa la bstod pa/ chos sku stong pa'i ngang nyid las/ /'gro ba'i don du bzhengs pa'i sku/ /zhi
ba'i zhal bzhi khro zhal bdun/ /bcu gcig zhal la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rtsa ba'i zhi zhal dkar po gsum/ /rab tu 'dzum zhing mdzes pa ste/ / las dang nyon mongs zhi mdzad
pa/ /chos sku'i zhal la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de steng btso ma gser mdog can/ /rngams pa'i zhal gsum bzhad pa'i dpal/ /tshe dang bsod nams dpal 'byor gsum/ /rgyas par mdzad la
phyag 'tshal lo/ /de steng byi ru ltar dmar ba'i/ /dbang gi las mdzad zhal gnyis po/ /rnam par gtsigs pa'i khro gnyer can/ /longs sku'i zhal la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de steng
drag po'i las mdzad pa/ /dud sprin mdog 'dra zhal gnyis po/ /'jigs shing rngams pa'i spyan gsum bgrad/ /sprul sku'i zhal la phyag 'tshal lo/ /de steng bla ma sprul pa'i
sku/ /sangs rgyas kun 'dus li khri'i mdog /'od dpag med mgon rgyal ba yi/ /gtsug rgyan can la phyag 'tshal lo/ /padma'i 'dab 'dra dang po yin/ /phyag gnyis thugs kar thal
sbyar nas/ /sangs rgyas kun gyi thugs rje rnams/ /bskul bar mdzad la phyag 'tshal lo/ /g.yas kyi phyag bzhi rim pa bzhin/ /bgrang phreng 'khor lo mchog sbyin dang / /dus
gsum sangs rgyas 'od dpag med/ /legs par bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /g.yon gyi phyag bzhi rim pa bzhin/ /pad dkar spyi blugs rin po che/ /thabs shes zung 'jug mda' dang
gzhu/ /legs par bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /g.yas kyi yan lag bcu dgu na| |rin chen zhags pa lhung bzed gri/ /rdo rje me shel chu shel gzhu/ /lcug ma

bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /rnga yab phub dang bum pa bzang / /dgra sta phreng ba padma sngo/ /spyi blugs nyi ma chu skyes dkar/ /snye ma bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ / g.yon
gyi yan lag bcu dgu na/ /sprin dkar spyi blugs padma gri/ /dung thod phreng ba dril bu dang / /rdo rje bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /lcags kyu 'khar gsil sprul pa'i sku/ khang
bzangs glegs bam 'khor lo dang / /sku gzugs shing thog ge sar bcas/ /rin chen bsnams la phyag 'tshal lo/ /chos sku'i rtsa phyag rnam pa bcu/ /longs sku'i yan lag sum
cu brgyad/ /sprul sku'i nying lag stong mnga' ba'i/ /nam mkha'i rgyal po khyod la 'dud/ /padma lta bu'i phyag mthil la/ /utpal 'dra ba'i spyan mig gis/ /rgyu skar bzhin
du rnam bkra ba'i/ /nam mkha'i rgyal po khyod la 'dud/ /dbu la rgyal ba'i gtsug rgyan bcas/ /phyag zhabs gser gyi gdu bu 'khrol/ /sku la dri zhim spos ngad ldan/ /nam mkha'i
rgyal po khyod la 'dud/ /sna tshogs dar gyi na bza' gsol/ /rin chen du ma'i rgyan gyis spras/ / blta bas mi ngoms mdzes pa'i sku/ /nam mkha'i rgyal po khyod la 'dud/
/ri dwags lpags pas nu ma bkab/ /yan lag rigs bzhi'i sbrul gyis brgyan/ / mtshan dpe gzi brjid 'bar ba'i sku/ /nam mkha'i rgyal po khyod la 'dud/ / gangs ri'i ngogs ltar
mdzes pa la/ /cung zad dmar ba'i mdangs dang ldan/ / thugs rje'i 'od dkar 'phro ba'i sku/ /nam mkha'i rgyal po khyod la 'dud/ /lha rgyal gtsug gi nor bu yis/ /legs par bzhengs
pa'i zhabs gnyis po/ /pad zla'i steng du 'gying ba'i sku/ /nam mkha'i rgyal po khyod la 'dud/ /dus gsum sangs rgyas thams cad kyi/ /thugs kyi sprul pa rin po che/ /thabs
mkhas thugs

rje ldan pa khyed/ /sems can rnams la gzigs su gsol/ /'gro ba kun gyi skyabs gnas khyed/ /sdug bsngal du mas gtses pa yi/ /nyam thag phongs pa'i sems can la/ /thugs rje'i spyan
gyis gzigs su gsol/ /ma rig 'khrul pa'i sems can rnams/ /las ngan bsags pas lus ngan blang / /ngan song gsum du lhung ba rnams/ /thugs rje'i lcags kyus gzung du gsol/
/zhes gsungs te/ dbu'i la thod phud nas/ yi dam gyi thugs kar gtugs nas/ 'phags pa khams gsum 'khor ba na 'khyams pa'i sems can nyam thag pa rnams la gzigs shig ces dad
pa'i shugs kyis spyan chab phyung nas/ gsol ba drag tu btab pa'i ngang la/ rgyal po 'od du zhu nas rang byon bcu gcig zhal gyi thugs kar thim mo/ /'phags pa'i thugs kar
phyag gnyis thal mo sbyar ba la/ kha phye nas yod pa de'ang de dus su byung ba yin no/ /de ltar thams cad kyis mngon sum du mthong yang bya thabs med par gcig gdong gcig
la blta zhing / mig hu re lus so/ /de nas mang bza' khri lcam gyis/ rgyal po yab yum gsum de ltar mdzad nas mi bzhugs na/ da ji ltar byed/ su la re thugs rjes gzung du gsol
zhes zhus pas/ rang byon gyi thugs ka nas rgyal pos dbu nyug mdzad de 'di skad ces gsungs so/ khyed rnams nyon cig skyes nas 'chi thag chod pa dang gciga'adus byas kyi
mtshan nyid mi rtag pa yin pa dang gnyis/ tshe la long med pa rtswa kha'i zil pa lta bu dang gsum/ da lta'i spyod lam 'di rnams rmi lam sgyu ma lta bur shes par gyis shig
gsungs so/ /bal mo bza' khri btsun kyang / nu ma g.yas pa'i steng nas dbu nyug mdzad de 'di skad gsungs so/ /tshe la nges pa med pa

nam mkha'i 'ja' tshon lta bu dang gcig ngag la nges pa med pa bar snang gi 'brug lta bu dang gnyis/ lus la nges pa med pa sos ka'i me tog lta bu dang gsum/ da lta'i spyod pa
'di me long nang gi gzugs brnyan lta bur shes par gyis shig gsungs so/ /rgya mo kong jo nu ma g.yon pa'i steng nas dbu nyug mdzad de 'di skad ces gsungs so/ /lus mi rtag
pa sdong rgan rtsa ba rul pa lta bu dang gcig tshe mi rtag pa nam mkha'i glog sprin lta bu dang gnyis/ nor mi rtag pa sbrang ma'i sbrang rtsi lta bu dang gsum/ da lta'i
spyod pa 'di chu'i lbu ba lta bur shes par mdzod cig gsungs te mi snang bar gyur to/ /de nas blon po gnyis kyis rgyal po chen po de ltar mdzad nas mi bzhugs na/ nged phyi
nang gi blon po/ bod 'bangs rnams ci ltar byed/ thugs rjes gzung du gsol zhes zhus pas/ yang rgyal pos dbu nyug mdzad nas 'di skad gsungs so/ /legs par nyon cig bdag gi
'khor 'bangs rnams/ /tshe 'di mi rtag rtswa kha'i zil pa 'dra/ /de la snyom las le lo ma byed cig /'chi bdag bdud ni ri gzar chu dang 'dra/ /de la long yod rtag par ma 'dzin
cig /sgyu lus phung po sos ka'i me tog 'dra/ /me tog sad kyis nam khyer nges pa med/ /tshe 'di'i bya ba spang la dam chos mdzod/ /mi rtag 'chi bar bsams la brtson 'grus
bskyed/ /nga dang khyed rnams 'bral med rtag tu 'grogs/ /gsungs te mi snang bar gyur to/ /der khong rnams gcig la gcig lta zhing / yab yum gsum sprul pa'i skur 'dug pa
la/ bzhugs pa'i dus mos gus chung 'dug ces smra zhing yod pa la/ zhang blon sna chen po dang / sbas lcang dpal gyi legs bzang gnyis byung ste/ rgyal po yab yum gsum gar

bzhud ces lan gsum zer ba la/ yab yum gsum de ltar mdzad/ yi dam la thim pa bshad kyang yid ches mi 'ong bsams te/ 'chad ma shes nas gcig gdong gcig la blta zhing mig hu re
lus so/ /der khong gnyis khros te/ rgyal po yab yum gar bzhud lan gsum dris pas mi 'chad par ngan pa khyed gnyis gsod pa yin zer nas ral gri phyung bas/ der mang bza' na
re/ rgyal po yab yum sprul pa'i skur 'dug pa/ yab yum gsum ga rang byon bcu gcig zhal gyi thugs kar thim nas bzhud do/ /zer nas ngus pas/ de la yang yid ma ches par dbon
sras la zhus pas/ der dbon sras kyis/ dang por zhal gdams rgyas par gsungs pa/ de rjes btsun mo gnyis rgyal po la thim pa/ de nas mes rgyal po yang yi dam gyi thugs kar
thim pa sogs rgyas par gsungs pas/ der khong gnyis kyang yid ches so/ /der blon po thon mis rgyal po sprul pa'i skur 'dug pa'i rgyu mtshan/ khra 'brug tu ban sprang la a
mi dhe ba'i zhal bstan pa dang / li yul gyi dge tshul gnyis la a mi dhe ba'i zhal bstan pa/ lha sa'i rab gnas mdzad dus rgyal pos gsol ba btab pas/ skad cig la sangs rgyas
dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams mngon sum du nam mkha' la byon pa la sogs pa bshad pas/ der thams cad yid ches te/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs dngos yin par 'dug pa/ yab
yum gsum bzhugs pa'i dus su mos gus chung 'dug zer te/ chos rgyal sprul pa'i sku zer zhing thams cad mya ngan gyis sa la 'gyel lo/ /der yang lha rnams kyis me tog gi char
phab ste/ sa yang rnam pa drug tu g.yos so/ /de nas rang byon bcu gcig zhal gyi thugs ka nas 'od zer kha

dog sna tshogs pa brgyad byung ste/ 'od zer gcig jo bo mi bskyod rdo rje'i thugs kar thim/ li ma/ 'od zer gcig byams pa chos kyi 'khor lo'i thugs kar thim/ li ma/ 'od zer gcig
sangs rgyas 'od dpag med kyi thugs kar thim/ 'od zer gcig sangs rgyas mi 'khrugs pa'i thugs kar thim/ 'od zer gcig khro rgyal sme ba brtsegs kyi thugs kar thim/ 'od zer
gcig sangs rgyas sman pa'i rgyal po'i thugs kar thim/ 'og khang shar lho'i g.yu rung khug na yod bris sku/ 'od zer gcig rta mgrin dkar po'i thugs kar thim/ bris sku bar
khang na yod/ 'od zer gcig rje btsun sgrol ma'i thugs kar thim/ bris sku bar khang na yod/ de rnams ni 'od zer 'phros pa'i lha brgyad yin no/ /yang lha de rnams kyi thugs
ka nas 'od zer 'phros pas lha khang nang gi lha thams cad la phog nas/ 'od zer gyi dra bas 'brel bar gyur to/ /de ni 'phrul snang gi gsang ba'i rab gnas lhun gyis grub
pa yin no/ /de nas dbon sras dang / btsun mo blon po la sogs de na yod pa thams cad mya ngan gyi sdug bsngal zhi nas/ zag med kyi bde ba la gnas par gyur to/ /de nas blon
po thams cad gros byas te/ sras gung ri gung btsan ni yab kyi gong du 'das/ dbon sras ni chung bas bang so brtsigs dgos pas/ yab yum gsum po rang byon bcu gcig zhal gyi
thugs kar thim pa gsang ste/ 'phan yul zal mo sgang du 'das pa yin no zhes phyogs bcur bsgrags nas/ yar lung 'chong po'i nang du yab yum gsum ka'i bang so/ 'gran zla dang
bral bar brtsigs so/ /rgyal po yab yum gyi mdzad pa yongs su rdzogs te/ rang byon bcu gcig zhal gyi thugs kar thim pa'i le'u ste bcu bdun pa'o/ /de ltar sprul

pa'i chos rgyal chen po de/ /dgung lo bdun cu tham pa rgyal sa bzung / /lha khang bzhengs shing dam chos rgyas par mdzad//dkon mchog zhabs tog bka' khrims chos la bsgyur/ /dgung
lo brgyad cu gya gnyis bzhengs pa na/ /le lo can rnams brtson 'grus bskyed pa dang/ /snyom las can rnams chos la bkod pa dang / / rtag par 'dzin pa skyo ba bskyed pa'i
phyir/ /'phrul snang nang gi btsan khang byang ma ru| |rgyal po yab yum 'od du rab zhu nas/ /yi dam lha yi thugs kar thim par gyur/ /sangs rgyas mi ru sprul pa'i 'gro
don can/ /spyan ras gzigs dang gnyis su med pa'i sras/ /sdig can chos la 'khod pa'i thugs rje can/ /mtha' yas sems can rnams kyi mgon gcig pu//chos rgyal sprul pa'i sku
la skyabs su mchi//'phags pa thugs rje can gyis byin gyis rlobs/ /de yi bang so 'chong po'i nang du btab/ /che chung tshad ni dpag tshad gcig tsam la/ /bang so gru bzhi dkyil
du re mig byas/ /dar dang shog bu bsres pa'i 'jim pa la/ /de la chos rgyal chen po'i sku bzhengs nas/ /shing rtar spyan drangs rol mor bcas nas ni/ /sku de bang so'i
nang du bzhugs pa mdzad/ /nang gi re mig thams cad nor gyis bkang / /bang so nang rgyan can du grags par gyur/ /nang du lha khang lnga yang bzhugs so zer/ /bang so gru bzhir
brtsigs pa de nas byung / /ming yang sku ri smug po lags so skad/ /phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas rnams dang nyan thos dang / / byang chub sems dpa' dam can chos skyong rnams/
/gnas der lhags nas bang so de la ni/ /bkra shis rab tu gnas pa'i phrin las mdzad/ /dbon sras mang srong mang btsan la sogs pa'i/ /blon po bod 'bangs 'khor dang bcas
pa

rnams/ /mchod pa'i yo byad bsam gyis mi khyab pa/ /gnas der khyer nas phyag dang mchod pa phul/ /de ltar 'gran med rgyal po'i bang so de/ /yul de'i lha srung rnams la phrin
bcol mdzad/ /gsol ba btab nas slar yang yul du byon/ / phan bde'i 'od kyis phyogs bcur khyab par mdzad/ /ces so/ /bco brgyad pa/ dbon sras mang srong mang btsan gyi skor/
des na dbon sras mang srong mang btsan gyis/ dgung lo bcu gsum lon dus rgyal srid bzung / btsun mo 'bro bza' khri ma lod bya ba khab tu bzhes/ rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur/
'di'i dus su rgya'i rgyal pos rgyal po srong btsan sgam po mi bzhugs par shes/ mgar gyis rgya yul phung bar byas pa rnams dran nas/ rgya'i dmag 'bum tsho lnga btang nas
bod 'joms pa dang / jo bo shAkya gdan 'dren zer ba la sogs kyi gtam byung ba la skrag nas/ jo bo ra mo che nas lha sar gdan drangs/ lho sgo me long can du bzhugs nas/
sgo la zha la bgyis te/ 'jam dbyangs bzhengs so/ /rgyal srid lo bco lnga bzung ste/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa bdun la gtsang gi bar snang sgang du 'das so/ /mang srong bang so
de yi g.yon na yod/ /bang so de yang rin chen nor gyis bkang / /ming ni sngo gzhe hral po zer ba lags/ /bcu dgu pa/ 'dul srong mang po rje rlung nam 'phrul gyi skor/ mang
srong mang btsan gyi sras la/ 'dul srong mang po rje rlung nam 'phrul gyi rgyal po yin te/ yab 'das zhag bdun lon dus chu pho byi ba la sgrag phu ru 'khrungs/ mgar gyi
sras gnya' btsan ldem bu dang / stag ra khong lod gnyis kyis blon po byas nas rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur/ mchims bza' btsun mo tog bya ba khab tu bzhes/

rgyal po 'di'i dus su blon po rtsal po che mi bdun byung ste/ rngog ring la nag pos glang po che theg rngog gling khams kyis g.yag grus po che khyog snon rgyal mtshan gyis
mda' ste'u kha mas bya khra rked par bcad/ dbas 'dong sgong gis mig rgyang gsum re la mda' rgyang res sleb/ 'gos g.yag chung gis sha ba'i rlud phur bye mas bkang ste glad
la bskor nus/ co ro 'brong sher gyis 'brong mthur la rgyug pa gyen la 'then thub/ snon khri bdun g.yu byin gyis rta g.yang la mchong ba gyen la 'then thub pa rnams byung
/ mnga' thang dpal 'byor ni lha dang mnyam/ stobs dang mthu rtsal gyis ni mtha' bzhi las rgyal te/ lha sar mes srong btsan sgam po'i dgongs dus kyi mchod pa btsug mtha'i
rgyal po yang dbang du 'dus pa tsam byung nas/ snga gong bod kyi rgyal po rim par byon pa rnams las mthu stobs che ba zhig byung ste/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa dgu rgyal srid
bzung nas ljang gi yul du 'das so/ /'phrul rgyal bang so mang srong g.yon na yod/ /bang so lha ri can zhes grags par gyur/ /de ni hor gyi mi sdes brtsigs pa lags/ /ming
ni seng ge brtsig pa zer ro skad/ /nyi shu pa/ khri lde gtsug brtan mes ag tshom gyi skor/ rgyal po 'dul srong mang po btsan gyi sras/ khri lde btsug brtan mes ag tshom
du grags pa ste/ lcags pho 'brug gi lo la pho brang ldan dkar du sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu la rgyal srid bzung / blon po skyi bzang stong btsan/ mchims rgyal shugs steng
/ 'bro chu bzang 'or gsum gyis blon po byas/ rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur/ ljang mo khri btsun bya ba'i btsun mo khab tu bzhes/ rgyal po des 'phyin phu nas/ mes

srong btsan sgam po'i zhal chems zangs kyi byang bu la bris pa rnyed de/ gzigs pas nga ni gdung rabs lnga na rgyal po khri dang lde zhes bya ba'i dus su dam pa'i chos dar/
paNDi ta mang po byon nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rgyas par 'gyur zhes pa de/ rgyal po khong rang yin dgongs nas/ bran kha mu le sho ka dang gnyags dznya na ku ma ra gnyis
pho nyar brdzangs te/ gangs ri ti se la paNDi ta sangs rgyas gsang ba dang / sangs rgyas zhi ba gnyis spyan 'dren du btang bas gdan ma 'drongs pa dang / theg pa chen po'i
mdo sde lnga blo la bzung nas 'ongs te/ yi ger bris nas glegs bam lnga bzhengs nas de rnams kyi bzhugs sa la lha khang lnga brtsigs te/ brag dmar ka ru/ kha che 'grin
bzang / lha sa kha brag 'phyin phu nam ral/ mang gong gi lha khang dang lnga bzhengs/ rgya yul ke ma shi nas mdo gser 'od dam pa dang / 'dul ba las rnam par 'byed pa bsgyur
ro/ /pe tsi tsandra shrIs sman dpyad mang po yang bsgyur ro/ /de rnams kyi yon tan gyis btsun mo ljang mo khri btsun la sras ljang tsha lha dbon zhes bya ba lha'i gzugs
byad lta bu shin tu mtshar ba cig 'khrungs so/ /de la bod na khab 'os pa ma rnyed nas/ mes srong btsan sgam po'i lugs su bya zer/ rgya nag gi rgyal po dzung dzung rgyal
po'i sras mo kyim shing kong jo la rin dang skyes bskur nas len du btang ngo / /der bod kyi blon pos rgya rje la rin dang skyes phul bas/ rgya rjes sras mo la 'gro'am mi
'gro gsungs pa dang / kong jos legs nyes ston pa'i me long zhig yod pa la dmod bor te legs par phyis nas bltas pas/ tshe 'di'i grogs skal bod na yod par shes shing / rgyal
bu de yang mtshar zhing yid du 'ong ba zhig mthong nas

bod du 'gro bar mos so/ /der yang rgyal po des rdzongs dpag tu med pa bskur/ rgyal po yang 'khor mang po dang bcas pa bu mo sems la 'phreng bas/ zhing pheng hen zer ba'i mkhar
rtsig chen po gcig yod pa'i sa cha bar du skyel thung mdzad do| |der gur chen po phub cing / bod kyi gser yig pa rnams la ston mo chen po byas te/ rgyal po'ang spyan
chab mang po phyung nas/ sras mo la bslab bya mang po mdzad/ mkhar de la gtogs pa'i nyes pa can thams cad thar du bcug go /lo gcig gi bar la dmag dang 'dab nor thams cad
med par mdzad de/ mkhar de'i ming kyim shing hen bya bar btags so/ /de nas blon po che ba gnyis dmag dang bcas pa'i skyel ma btang ste bod du 'ongs so/ /der rgya bod kyi
mtshams su sleb pa dang / bod du blon po rnams kyis rgyal bu gdan drangs te/ mtshan mo zla ba'i 'od la thams cad kyis rta rgyugs pa la der rgyal bus kyang rta rgyugs pas/
rtas bskyur te 'das so/ /de ltar btsun mo sleb khar/ rgyal bu grongs nas thams cad mya ngan gyis non no/ /ljang tsha lha dbon bang so mes kyi mdun/ /zlum por brtsigs nas
gter yang sbas so skad/ /de nas kong jo dpon g.yog rnams kyis/ rgya bod kyi mtshams su slebs pa dang / kong jo la glo bur du snying la mda' phog pa'i sdug bsngal 'dra ba
zhig byung nas/ de ma khad me long phyis nas bltas pas/ sngar gyi rgyal bu gzugs byad mdzes pa de med par rgad po bzhin mi sdug pa byad spus khengs pa zhig 'dug nas shin
tu yi mug par gyur te 'di skad zer ro| |me long gi brda chad mthong ba na/ /bu mo'i snying la gcong cig zhugs/ /rang yul du log pa shul thag ring / /bu mo'i pha ming snying
ring po/ /bod du 'gro ba'i

re thag chad/ /bod kyi blon po sdig po che/ /cha med yul du rgyus med 'khyam/ / las kyi me long bslu ba mkhan/ /zer te me long la brdeg cing ngus so/ /de nas bod kyi rgyal
pos pho nya btang ste/ rgya mo dpon g.yog rnams la khyod kyi skyes pa'i 'os nga'i bu lha dang 'dra ba zhig yod pa de/ rkyen ngan pas 'das/ da de khyed rang yul du log gam/
nged la bltas nas 'ong zhes yi ge btang bas/ der rgya mo na re| bu mo'i 'dun ma lan cig yin pa skyid sdug ci byung yang bod du 'gro zer 'ongs so/ /der bod du slebs pa dang
/ rgya mo na re/ nga'i a ne'i lha khang blta'o zer te/ ra mo cher phyin pas/ de na jo bo mi bzhugs par 'dug nas 'phrul snang du 'ongs pa dang / jo bo lho sgo me long
can na bzhugs par shes nas sgo phye ste| jo bo de nas bton nas/ btsan khang dbus mar bzhugs su gsol/ lha zhal mthong gi mchod pa btsug jo bo gdung rabs gsum gyi bar la mun
khang du bzhugs pa la/ rgya mos mchod pa btsugs pa yin no/ /de nas 'phyin phur byon te| mes rgyal po'i btsun mor mnga' gsol lo/ /de nas lo dus 'khor ba na/ rgyal bu lus
la zhugs pa dang / btsun mo che ba sna nam bza' bzhi stengs zer ba zhig yod pa phrag dog skyes nas/ nga la'ang rgyal po'i gdung brgyud lus la yod do zhes rdzun smras te/
der rgya mo la rgyal po khri srong lde btsan lcags pho rta'i lo la brag dmar du sku 'khrungs pas/ sna nam bza' rgya mo'i rtsar byung / shin tu blo nye ba ltar byas nas/
rgya mo'i bu chung 'phrog ste/ nga rang la skyes pa yin no zer bsnyon byas so/ /der rgya mos rang gi nu ma bstan/ smre sngags bton/ cho nges bos kyang bu chung ma btang bas/
blon po rnams sbran/ rgyal po la zhus pas/ der

sna nam bzas kyang rang gi nu ma la eds: ('o ma )rang babs kyi rdzas byug ste/ nu zho 'ongs pa byas nas blon po rnams la bstan pas/ blon po rnams kyang the tshom du gyur nas
ma shes so/ /der rgya mo'i bu chung btsun mo che bas phrogs pas/ dbang shed mos ni ma thub/ byed thabs med par song ngo / /der rgya mo'i sems la da de bu chung 'dis nga
la phan pa dka'/ bod 'di phung ba'i las zhig byed dgos bsams nas ri'i dpyad bltas pas/ rgyal po'i gdung rabs chad pa'i phyir/ rje'i bla ri seng ge gnam du mchong ba 'dra
ba'i mgo la/ mngal khrag gis 'khor lo bris nas mchod rten gyis mnan/ blon po rig pa can mi 'ong ba'i phyir/ blon po'i bla ri la khro chus sna bcad/ stag ri seng ri gnyis
gzhug eds: (mjug)ma sbrel ba'ang bcad/ mu ge 'ong ba'i phyir/ yar lung me sna'i ri 'bras kyi ljang pa 'dra ba'i rtsa ba bcad/ bod du mdze 'ong ba'i phyir/ mang mkhar gyi
ri khyung chen gnam la lding ba 'dra ba'i mchu bcad do/ /de rnams zin pa dang / sras kyis lo 'khor te| zhabs 'dzugs kyi dga' ston la/ btsun mo gnyis po'i pha ming rgya dang
sna nam nas bos so/ /der sna nam pa rnams kyis bu chung dga' bar byed pa'i yo byad/ rgyan dang / gos dang / me tog gi phreng ba rnams khyer 'ongs so/ /der rgya dang /
sna nam gnyis nas/ btsun mo gnyis po'i pha ming rnams bod du slebs so| |der rgyal po'i pho brang du rgyal po gser khri'i steng du gung la bzhugs/ g.yas na sna nam pa rnams
kyis bsdad/ g.yon na rgya rnams kyis bsdad/ der yab rgyal pos sras rgyan du mas brgyan te/ gser skyogs 'bras chang gis gang ba sras kyi lag tu gtad nas/ yab na re/ ma
gnyis las skyes pa'i bu gcig

po| |lus chung yang lha yi rnam 'phrul can/ /snod gser skyogs chang gis gang ba 'di/ /bu khyod rang gi zhang po'i lag tu gtod/ /ma gang yin gyi yid ches de la byed/ /gsungs
te/ dmod bor nas sras gom pa thub tsam de btang nas/ der sras kyi gom pa bor nas byon pa dang / sna nam pa rnams kyis gos dang / rgyan dang / me tog gi phreng ba la sogs
bstan nas bos kyang / 'gror ma nyan par rgya rnams kyi rtsar byung ste/ gser skyogs rgya la gtad nas 'di skad zer ro/ /nga khri srong lde btsan rgya tsha yin/ /sna nam zhang
gi don mi 'tshal/ /zer te/ zhang po rgya'i pang du song ngo / /der yum rgya mo shin tu dga' ste 'di skad zer ro/ /tshe sngon ma'i las kyi 'phen pa yis/ /nga rgya nas
'ongs pa'i bu mo la/ /rje 'dren eds: ('gran ) med rgyal po'i sras zhig 'khrungs/ /las gang yang srid pa'i sngon chad la/ /bu rang la skyes pa gzhan gyis phrogs/ /gtam bden
pa'i tshig la ma nyan zhing / / brang nu ma bstan kyang ma gtad pas/ /nga rgya mo'i lus sems gzhob tu thal/ / sems khong khro'i na tsha ma bzod par/ /yul bod kyi ri dpyad
nyams su bcug / dus de ring lha yi nyi ma shar/ /bu khyod kyis zhang ngo shes pa lags/ /nga a ma'i lus sems mal du bde/ /yul bod kyi ri dpyad nyams pa de/ /ri de rnams
la skyon med bcos su yod/ /ces zer ro/ /der rgya mo'i sras yin par ngo shes nas/ dga' ston gyi ston mo chen po byas so/ /der sras dgung lo lnga lon dus yum 'das so/ /yab
rgyal po mes ag tshom ni/ dgung lo drug cu re gsum la yar 'brog sba tshal mkhar gshegs so/ /de'i bang so mu ra ri la brtsigs/ / gral ni 'phrul gyi rgyal po'i g.yon na yod/
/ming ni lha ri gtsug nam bya ba

lags/ /zhes so/ /nyer gcig pa/ de nas chos rgyal khri srong lde btsan gyis dgung lo brgyad lon pa dang / rgyal srid bzung nas rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur/ rgyal po sku nar
ma son pa'i dus su ma zhang khron eds: (grom )pa skyes la sogs pa blon po chos la mi dga' ba rnams kyis chos byar mi gnang ba'i khrims bcas nas/ lha sa'i jo bo rin po che
slar rgya yul du skyel grabs byas pas/ mi stong gis kyang ma drangs/ mkhar brag tu sa thams su bcug pas/ blon po chos la mi dga' ba la la ni smyo 'bog byung nas shi la la
rgyab gas nas shi mkhar rna gdong / mu ge dang / nad yams dang / bkra mi shis pa'i ltas mang po byung bas/ ltas mkhan thams cad kha mthun par rgya'i lha bye thams eds:
(thems )su bcug pas lan 'dug zer nas/ sa 'og nas bton te/ rgya gar du skyel bar bsams pas dre'u gnyis kyi theg nas mang yul du phebs pa'i dus su/ lam la ma thar zhes glengs
nas/ jo bo mang yul du lo bcu bzhi bzhugs/ yar lung jo bos bsgrigs pa'i rgyal rabs dang / gzhan na'ang 'di ga 'dug jo bo mi bskyod rdo rje rgya yul du skyel rgyu la/ shar
phyogs do mo'i thang la bskyal/ der zhag bdun lus pa/ khong rang gi jo bo min pa ngo shes nas bzhag pa yin 'dug 'o rgyal thang zer chos lung mda'/ slar ra mo cher bzhugs
su bcug go /rgyal po chos la dga' na'ang / blon po ma zhang khron eds: (grom )pa skyes dang / stag ra klu gong la sogs dbang ches pas/ gzhan gyis rgol ma nus so/ /de
nas rgyal po sku nar son te/ rje blon rnams chos bya bar blo mthun te/ thabs sna tshogs kyis mgo bskor nas/ ma zhang stod lung brang phu ru gson por bang sor bcug stag

ra klu gong byang la spyugs go /de nas thams cad la chos bya ba'i bka' gnang nas/ thog mar mang yul nas jo bo shAkya shing rtar gdan drangs bsu ba rol mo bsam gyis mi khyab
pa dang bcas te ra sa'i gtsang khang dbus mar bzhugs su gsol/ dus der kha che skyes bzangs kyi bu A nanda zer ba de ra sa dang ra mo che gnyis kyi bar na/ dar tshags dgung
seb kyi tshong dus sar/ tshong byed kyin yod pa bos nas de la lo tsA bcol te/ chos dang bon gnyis rtsod pa 'gran pas/ bon khungs ngan par byung nas/ bon gyi chos thams
cad brag dmar la sogs par gter du sbas so/ /la la chu la bskyur/ 'phral gyi 'gal rkyen bzlog pa tsam min pa ma gnang ngo / /de nas rgyal blon thams cad gros bgyis te/ sngon
mchod rten bya rung kha shor gyi drung du/ khye'u gsum gyis smon lam btab pa'i mthu la brten nas/ sba gsal snang rgya gar du mkhan po bo dhi sa twa gdan 'dren du btang
bas/ gsal snang gis mkhan po gdan drangs te pho brang du phebs pa dang / rgyal pos sku rags ma bcings par/ gser phye bre gang phyag tu bsnams nas mkhan po'i bsu ba la byon
pas/ mkhan po'i zhal nas/ rgyal po khyed kyi dbu la la thod gsol bas/ stod du mnga' ris zhwa tsam zhig la khrims shig chags/ zhabs la chag gsol bas smad du mdo khams
lham tsam la khrims shig chags/ sku lus la sku rags ma bcings pas/ bar 'dir rgyal khrims myur du 'jig nyen yod/ 'on kyang rin po che'i phyag rten phul bas chos byar btub
gsungs so| |de nas kha che A nandas lo tsA bgyis te/ rje blon rnams la chos gsungs pas/ nag po'i phyogs 'dre srin gdug pa can ma dga' bar/ thog dang / lo

nyes/ nad yams byung bas/ 'dre srin dam la 'dogs pa'i phyir du u rgyan gyi yul nas slob dpon padma 'byung gnas gdan drangs te/ bod kyi 'dre srin dam la btags te/ rje blon chos
byed pa la 'gal rkyen med par mdzad do/ /slob dpon gyis rgyal po la rig 'dzin gyi tshe chu gnang bas/ blon po chos la mi dga' ba rnams kyis rgyal po la mon gyi smyo chu
dug yin pas/ mi gsol bar zhu zhus pas/ rgyal po yang the tshom du gyur nas ma gsol/ nad du mdze mi 'ong ba'i phyir/ klu'i rgyal po mal gro gzi chen dam la btags nas rdo
rje bsnun pas gzi chen gyis khye'u zhig tu sprul nas/ rgyal po la grogs po bcol lo/ /rgyal po la ji ltar 'dod pa'i dngos grub ster bar khas blangs nas/ rgyal pos klu'i
ngo chen mdzad nas thugs dam blang ngo / /yang slob dpon gyis ngam shod kyi bye thang thams cad ne'u thang du gtang bzhed pa la/ blon po ngan pa rnams kyis rgyal po la zhus
te/ slob dpon gyis rdzu 'phrul yin pas ring du mi gnas shing mi rung ngo zhes zer te mdzad par ma zhus/ gzhan yang slob dpon gyis rgyal po'i btsun mo mkhar chen bza' 'tsho
rgyal dbang yon du khab tu bzhes pas/ blon po thams cad ma dga' bar/ rgyal po la snyan 'phra zhus nas/ rgyal pos slob dpon gyi zhal la ma nyan pas mdzol pa chen po gsum
byung zer ba la sogs dang / slob dpon mthu che bas rgyal srid la gnod par nges/ slob dpon yul la gshegs par zhu zhus so/ /bsam yas kyi bka' gtsig na/ slob dpon slar u
rgyan yul du bzhud zer ba 'dug ste/ rgyal po dang gros mdzad nas/ tsa ri la sogs su bzhugs/ ma zhang khron (grom )pa skyes bsad rting / slar bsam yas su byon zer/ de nas
rgyal pos bod 'bangs rnams bsags te/ snga gong bod du rab tu byung ba'i dpe mi 'dug pas/ bod du rab tu byung ba e

'ong blta ba'i phyir/ blon po dang 'bangs kyi bu blo rno ba bdun/ bo dhi sa twa'i drung du rab tu byung ste/ de'ang sba sang shi'i bu ratna/ mchims a nu'i bu shAkya bra baeds:
(pra bha)/ pa gor ratna'i bu bai ro tsa na/ ngan lam rgyal ba mchog dbyangs/ rma a tsarya rin chen mchog 'khon klu'i dbang po bsrung ba/ lo rgyus zhig na/ 'khon klu'i
dbang po sad mi mi bdun la mi the zer ba'ang 'dug gtsang legs grub ste/ bdun gyis rab tu byung bas/ sad mi mi bdun zhes grags so/ /de bzhin du btsun mo dang / blon po 'bangs
la sogs pa'i bu sum brgya rab tu byung ste/ rgya gar du blo rno ba rnams brdzangs te/ sgra dang lo tsA slob tu btang ngo / /de nas rgyal po'i thugs la dpal bsam yas
mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang bzhengs par 'dod nas/ blon po 'gos la sogs pa'i chos blon rnams dang gros mdzad de/ dka' ba'i las rnams ma bsten na/ /sla ba'i
las la grub pa med/ /gsungs te/ mnga' 'og gi blon po bod 'bangs rnams bsags te/ rgyal po'i zhal nas sngon chad bod kyi rgyal po byon pa la nga che/ ngas lag rjes chen po
zhig 'jog dgos/ rgyu shel las grub pa'i mchod rten shar ri dang mnyam pa zhig 'chos sam zhang po rgya'i yul mthong ba'i mkhar zhig brtsig gam/ has po ri zangs kyis 'thum
mam/ dka' bcu thang la khron pa 'dom dgu brgya dgu bcu yod pa 'bru'am/ wa lung grog mo gser phyes 'gengs sam/ gtsang po sbubs su 'jug gam/ dkon mchog gsum kyi rten bzhugs
pa'i lha khang bre tshad tsam zhig bzhengs sam 'doms shig gsungs pas/ der thams cad kyis rgyal po'i bka' de gser gyi pha bong bzhin sems thog tu lji bar byung nas/ zhu
ma shes par mig hu re lus

so| |der blon po 'gos dang / zhang nyang bzang dang / gnyer stag btsan 'dong gzigs la sogs pa'i chos blon rnams bzhengs te/ rje gcig lags/ shel gyi mchod rten shang ri dang
mtho dma' mnyam pa ni skye ba 'di la grub pa mi srid/ rgya yul mthong ba'i mkhar bsam pas 'grub pa mi srid/ bod mnga' rigs kyi zangs thams cad bsdus kyang / has po ri 'thums
pa med/ wa lung grog mo gser phye ma'i bye mas kyang mi khengs/ khron pa 'dom dgu brgya bas brgya yang 'bru mi thub/ gtsangapo sbubs su dgun tshud kyang dbyar mi tshud/
de bas rje'i thugs dam/ 'bangs kyi skyabs gnas/ phan bde thams cad 'byung ba'i gzhi ma| gtsug lag khang bre tshad tsam zhig bzhengs pa lags zhus pas/ der thams cad kha
'cham par de bzhin legs so zhes gda'o/ /de nas rgyal po'i zhal nas/ slob dpon chen po nga'i pha ma gnyis po gang na 'dug zhus pas/ slob dpon gyi zhal nas/ rgyal po khyed
kyi yab ni/ rgya gar gyi yul na/ paNDi ta chen po zhig tu skyes 'dug ste/ khyed kyi dbon sras kyi dus su/ paNDi ta dA na shI la yin par lung bstan bod du 'byon par 'dug
khyed kyi yum ni/ zung mkhar na dbul po bza' mi gnyis kyi bu mor skyes 'dug ste/ ming dang rus ni 'di ltar ro zhes lung bstan/ de nas rgyal pos btsun mo lnga khab tu bzhes
pa la/ tshe spang eds: (spong )bza' me tog sgron/ 'khar chen bza' 'tsho rgyal/ btsun mo 'di slob dpon la dbang yon du phul lo/ /'bro bza' byang chub sgron/ mchims bza'
lha mo btsan rnams so/ /yang yum gyi drin bsab pa'i phyir/ dbul po bza' mi'i bu mo khab tu bzhes te/ pho yong bza' rgyal mo btsun zhes grags so/ /lo rgyus shig na/ rgyal
po'i yum gyi skye ba bu mo de/ 'phan yul

zur chu nas rnyed zer ba 'dug ste/ gang ltar na'ang pho yong bza' yin par don mthun no/ /de nas slob dpon gyis gtsug lag khang brtsig pa'i sa dpyad gzigs pas/ shar ri rgyal
po gdan la bzhugs pa 'dra de bzang / ri chung bya mas bu la sgab pa 'dra de bzang / sman ri rin chen spungs pa 'dra de bzang / has po ri btsun mo dar dkar gyi na bza' gsol
ba 'dra de bzang / ri nag lcags phur sa la btab pa 'dra de bzang / me yar dre'u chu 'thung ba 'dra de bzang / del thang dar dkar gyi yol ba 'then pa 'dra de bzang / sa
gzhi ni gser gzhong gur gum gyis bkang ba 'dra de bzang bas/ rje'i thugs dam 'dir bzhengs shig gsungs nas phyag bris mdzad do/ /de nas slob dpon gyis 'dre srin gdug pa can
rnams dam la btags nas 'gal rkyen med par mdzad de/ ya rabs rigs btsun zhing pha ma drug eds: (drung )ldan gyi bu dang bu mo rgyan du mas brgyan pa lnga bcu/ rin po che'i
bum par bkra shis kyi chus gang ba thogs te/ sa phur btab/ sa gzhi byin gyis brlabs so/ /de nas rgyal pos blon po dang / bod 'bangs thams cad las la bskul te/ dbus su
ri'i rgyal po ri rab la dpe blangs nas/ dbu rtse chen mo rmang bting tsam na/ rje btsun ma sgrol mas lung bstan nas/ snga sor Arya pa lo gling bzhengs te/ rten gyi gtso
bo la 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs/ de'i g.yas su sgrol ma/ g.yon du 'od zer can/ yang g.yas su yi ge drug pa/ g.yon du dpal rta mgrin la sogs pa/ gtso 'khor lnga bzhengs so/
/steng du 'od dpag med gtso 'khor lnga bzhengs so/ /de nas slob dpon gyis rgyal po la rta mgrin sgrub pa'i lung gnang nas sgrub pa mdzad pas/ rgyal pos rta mgrin 'grub
nas/

rta skad lan gsum bton pas 'dzam bu'i gling sum gnyis su thos te/ rgyal po'i chab srid kyang 'dzam gling sum gnyis la dbang bsgyur ba yin gsungs/ de nas yos kyi lo la dbu rtse
chen po'i 'og khang bzhengs te/ rten gyi gtso bo la has po ri nas spyan drangs pa'i rdo'i thub pa rang byon la rin po che'i 'jim pas g.yogs te/ mtshan dpe dang ldan par
bzhugs/ g.yas gral la byams pa/ spyan ras gzigs/ sa'i snying po/ dga' ba'i dpal/ khro bo khams gsum rnam rgyal la sogs pa'o/ /g.yon gral la kun tu bzang po/ phyag na rdo
rje/ 'jam dpal/ sgrib pa rnam sel/ dge bsnyen dri ma med pa/ khro bo mi g.yo ba dang / gtso 'khor bcu gsum rnams bod kyi lugs su bzhengs/ lte ba'i phyi lha'i ri mo mdzad
pa bcu gnyis/ kha nang lta la tog gi rgyud ris/ sngar khang rje'i thugs dam gyi rgyud ris rnams bzhengs/ mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i mgo can la gtad/ de nas bar khang bzhengs
te/ rten gyi gtso bo la sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad/ g.yas phyogs la mar me mdzad/ g.yon na byams pa / mdun na shAkya thub pa/ sman gyi lha/ snang ba mtha' yas gsum
bzhugs/ g.yas g.yon na byang sems nye ba'i sras brgyad/ dge bsnyen dri ma med pa/ byang chub sems dpa' dga' ba'i dpal/ khro bo kang dang king / bzo rgya nag gi lugs su
bzhengs/ rgyud ris la yum rgyas pa gling gzhi'i le'u gdong la rgyal chen bzhi/ bskor khang kha phyir lta la mchod rten brgyad pa/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i rgyud ris/ kha
nang lta la sprin chen po'i rgyud ris/ sngags khang la phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas dang / gshin rje gshed kyi lha tshogs/ bsam yas kyi chos skyong rnams kyi 'bag chos skyong
rgyal

po shing bya can la gtad/ steng khang gi gtso bo sangs rgyas rnam par snang mdzad kun tu zhal re re la 'khor gnyis re/ byang chub sems dpa' nye ba'i sras brgyad/ nang gi lha
byang chub sems dpa' rdo rje rgyal mtshan la sogs pa phyogs bcu'i sangs rgyas byang sems/ khro bo mi g.yo ba dang phyag na rdo rje/ bzo rgya gar gyi lugs su bzhengs/ rgyud
ris mdo sde sa bcu pa/ chos skyong rgyal po zangs ma'i 'be log can la gtad/ thog rgya phub za 'og ris su byas/ lcog bzhi na sangs rgyas dga' ba'i dpal la 'khor byang
chub sems dpas bskor ba/ chos skyong lag na rdo rje gos sngon can bzhi la gtad/ de nas 'khor sa bar pa brtsigs te/ lho phyogs klu'i bang mdzod rol chas bkang / gnod sbyin
lag na dbyug tho thogs pa mched gsum la gtad/ nub phyogs mdo rgyud chos kyi bang mdzod sum brgya dang / bod dang rgya'i dpe cha glegs bam gyis bkang ste/ a tsa ra lag na
spu gri thogs pa gsum la gtad/ byang phyogs rin chen gter gyi bang mdzod gsum gser dngul zangs la sogs pas bkang ste/ gshin rje gshed lag na be con can gsum la gtad/ rgyud
ris la rgya cher rol pa bris/ de'i bar la sangs rgyas stong dang khri la sogs pa bris so/ /de nas 'khor sa chen po bskor te/ dpal rnam par snang mdzad ngan song sbyong
ba'i dkyil 'khor bzhengs so| |mda' yab kyi ngos gsum na rigs lnga'i lder so zhal phyir blta ba/ nang du stug po brgyan pa/ nor bu bzang po chos skyong klu'i rgyal po A nanda
la gtad/ rgyab tu rdo ring btsugs chos skyong si ha mu kha la gtad/ dbu rtse'i sgo gsum rnam par thang pa'i sgo/ /gru skas drug ni pha rol phyin pa drug /'og khang rdo
la bar khang

so phag yin/ /steng khang gzhal yas rin chen shing las grub/ /bzo rnams thams cad 'dul ba'i lugs dang bstun/ /rgyud ris thams cad mdo sde'i lugs dang bstun/ /lder so thams
cad gsang sngags dag dang bstun/ /zhes so| |de nas shar lus 'phags po'i gling gsum zla gam ris su yod pa la dpe blangs nas/ shar du lha khang gsum brtsigs te/ de yang rnam
dag khrims khang gling na rten gyi gtso bo shAkya thub pa gtso 'khor lnga/ mngon par 'byung ba'i rgyud ris/ chos skyong tshangs pa dung gi thor tshugs can la gtad/ mkhyen
rab 'jam dpal gling na/ 'phags pa 'jam dpal gtso 'khor bdun/ sgo srung gshin rje gshed gnyis 'jam dpal rtsa rgyud dang / ngan song sbyong ba'i rgyud gnyis/ chos skyong
gshin rje'i 'khor lo can la gtad/ brda sbyor tshangs pa gling na shAkya thub pa gtso 'khor bdun/ mya ngan las 'das pa'i rgyud ris/ chos skyong 'brug gi glog ba can la gtad/
lho 'dzam bu gling gi gling gsum sog khar yod pa la dpe blangs nas/ lho phyogs su lha khang gsum bzhengs te/ de yang bdud 'dul sngags pa gling na/ thub pa bdud 'dul lugs
gtso 'khor lnga/ lte ba la mdo sde sa bcu pa'i rgyud ris/ 'khor sa la nam mkha'i snying po'i rgyud ris/ chos skyong dbang phyug ma nyi shu rtsa brgyad la gtad/ Arya pa
lo gling na/ kharsa pa Ni gtso 'khor lnga/ steng na snang ba mtha' yas gtso 'khor lnga/ bloeds: (glo )'bur na tsandan la dngul g.yogs pa'i rgyal po'i sku 'dra gcig mchod
rten gcig rgyud ris/ za ma tog lha mo stong rtsa gnyis chos skyong drang srong dharma rA dza la gtad/ sgra sgyur rgya gar gling na thub pa rgya gar lugs ma gtso 'khor lnga/
rgyud ris la tshe dpag med

dang / lo paN sgra bsgyur pa'i gzugs so/ /chos skyong gnod sbyin rA hu la la gtad/ nub ba lang spyod kyi gling gsum zlum por yod pa la dpe blangs nas/ nub tu lha khang gsum
brtsigs te/ de yang dpa' bo bai ro tsa na gling na rnam par snang mdzad zangs la bzhengs pa/ 'khor gsang ba yum bzhi/ rnam par snang mdzad mngon par byang chub pa'i rgyud
ris/ chos skyong gnod sbyin glang gi mgo can la gtad/ dga' ldan byams pa gling na/ mgon po byams pa gtso 'khor bdun/ sgo srung gshin rje gshed gnyis/ rgyud ris la gnas
brtan bcu drugabasam yas bzhengs lugs dang / 'jig rten gtan bzhag rnams bris/ chos skyong khro bo gos sngon can la gtad/ mi g.yo bsam gtan gling na/ rnam par snang mdzad
rigs lnga/ nyan thos bcu drug rgyud ris la gser 'od dam pa nas khye'u chu 'bebs kyi ri mo/ chos skyong rgyal po dngul mgo can la gtad/ byang sgra mi snyan gyi gling gsum
gru bzhir yod pa la dpe blangs nas/ byang du lha khang gsum bzhengs te/ de'ang rin chen sna tshogs gling na shAkya thub pa gtso 'khor lnga/ rgyud ris la dga' ldan du bcom
ldan 'das kyis yum la chos gsungs pa/ drin lan bsabs pa rnams bris/ chos skyong rgyal po lcags kyi sder mo can la gtad/ sems bskyed byang chub gling na sangs rgyas padma
can/ sgrib pa rnam sel/ phyag na rdo rje/ bdud rtsi 'khyil ba/ rgyud ris mdo sde dkon mchog sprin dang / rtag tu ngus shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa btsal ba rnams bris/
chos skyong mkha' 'gro ma seng ge'i mgo can la gtad/ pe dkar dkor mdzod gling na shAkya thub pa gtso 'khor dgu/ yab sras mjal ba'i rgyud ris/ glo 'bur rnams na bsam yas

bzhengs pa'i nor lhag ma/ 'di na 'di yod kyi rtsis yig de'i srung ma khram khang gi rgyal po la gtad/ lha khang spyi'i bstan srung la/ slob dpon gyis za hor gyi yul nas/ lha'i
dge bsnyen chen po/ bdud kyi dmag dpon chen po/ snang srid kyi lha ma srin sde brgyad la dbang byed cing / skye 'gro thams cad kyi dbugs len/ srog bdag chen po pe ha
ra la gtad cing / pe dkar gyi gling du rten btsugs so// nyi ma lha khang yag sha gong ma gang ba bzang po'i lha khang na shAkya thub pa gtso 'khor lnga/ rgyud ris sangs rgyas
stong rtsa gnyis/ zla ba lha khang yag sha 'og ma nor bu bzang po'i lha khang na/ lha khang rgyud ris gong dang mthun/ tshang mang ke'u gling na steng na ba so lha khang
/ dag byed khrus khang gling na khron pa tsandan gyis gang ba| mthu gtad klu khang gling na/ se ba phung po yal ga brgyad yod pa gcig la/ klu chen brgyad/ dbus na phyag
na rdo rje/ zhi ba 'dul byed rgyud ris/ rus sbal nya chu srin la sogs pa'o/ /de nas mchod rten dkar po byang chub chen po'i mchod rten nyan thos kyi lugs seng ges brgyan
pa/ shud pu dpal gyi seng ges lag dpon byas nas bzhengs/ chos skyong gnod sbyin skar mda' can la gtad/ mchod rten dkar po'i srog shing rgyal chen bzhis btsugs nas bzhugs
la sangs rgyas kyi ring bsrel ma ga dha'i bre'i khal gcig gnyen po gsang ba yab kyi yi dam/ mdo sde lnga rnams bzhugs pas byin rlabs che/ mchod rten dmar po chos kyi
'khor lo bskor ba'i lugs padmas brgyan pa/ sna nam rgyal tsha lha gnang gis lag dpon byas nas bzhengs/ chos skyong gza' mig dmar la gtad/ mchod rten nag po rang sangs rgyas
kyi lugs/ ngam stag sgra klu gong gis lag dpon byas nas bzhengs/ chos skyong gnod sbyin lcags kyi mchu

can la gtad/ mchod rten sngon po dpal lha las babs pa de bzhin gshegs pa'i lugs/ lha khang sgo mo bcu drug gis brgyan pa/ mchims rdo rje sprel chung gis las dpon byas nas bzhengs/
chos skyong gnod sbyin nyi ma'i gdong la gtad/ de'i tshe 'dre mo 'od can mas mi thams cad la gnod 'tshe byas pas/ slob dpon gyis byams pa gling du mchod rten 'od
'bar ba brtsigs te/ 'dre mo mnan/ gnod 'tshe med par mdzad do/ /de nas lcags ri zur mangs rdo rje 'gros ni/ mchod rten brgya rtsa brgyad kyi tshul du bzhugs nas re re la
sangs rgyas kyi ring bsrel re re bzhugs so/ /de nas btsun mo gling gsum ni/ 'gro bza' byang chub sgron gyis dge rgyas bye ma gling bzhengs te/ sangs rgyas snang ba mtha'
yas gtso 'khor bdun li ma ru bzhengs/ g.yas na rigs gsum mgon po| g.yon na sman gyi bla/ kun tu bzang po/ mi g.yo ba rnams bzhugs/ sras med pha ming thag ring bas/ ma 'ongs
pa'i dus su lha khang la zhig ral byung na/ gso mkhan ma byung dogs nas/ rtsig pa so phag la zha nye'i chus sbyar/ zangs kyis thog phub/ rol mor jang btag mar me'i tshab
tu nor bu 'od kha gdung mar btag yon chab tu khron pa bcos so/ /tshe yang bza' me tog sgron la sras gsum 'khrungs te/ mu ne btsad po/ mu rug btsad po/ mi mug btsad po
sad na legs dang gsum yod pa'i yab kyi dbu rtse rigs gsum la dpe blangs nas/ khams gsum zangs khang gling gi lha khang bzhengs so/ /pho yang bza' rgyal mo btsun gyis bu tshal
gser khar gling rdo rje dbyings kyi dkyil 'khor du bzhengs/ lha bzo la sogs pa bzo bo rnams la dus re la zas sna bcu gsum re drangs

pas/ de'i bzang lan du bzo khyad bcu gsum byas pa la/ phyi na rtsig pa med de/ rdo rje lta bur sra ba bzo'i khyad/ nang na ka ba med de/ gur lta bur mdzes pa bzo'i khyad/ sa
gzhi ra gan las byas pa/ g.yu'i gdung ma la gser gyi rta rgyug pa| gser gyi gdung ma la g.yu'i 'brug yod pa/ rgya phub eds: (phibs )kha phyi lta dang nang lta yod pa/ nang
gi lha rnams la spyi gdugs re dang/ sgos gdugs re yod pa| sgo 'byed gcod la gser gyi bye rus skad 'don pa/ mdzad pa bcu gnyis 'bur du dod pa sogs/ bzo'i khyad ngo mtshar
can bcu gsum byas so/ /de ltar dpal bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang sde skor legs par bzhengs pa'i bzo phud la/ lha sar shing bzo'i phud la/ btsan
khang dbus ma'i mdun du sgo mo che rta babs kyis brgyan pa dang / sa'i phud la sgo srung rgyal chen bzhi bzhengs su gsol/ de ltar yos kyi lo la bsam yas kyi rmang bting
nas yos kyi lo la yongs su rdzogs par tshar te/ lo skor gcig 'gor ro/ /de nas rab tu gnas par bya ba'i phyir/ bza' btung gi longs spyod dpag tu med pa bsags/ mnga' zhabs
kyi mi thams cad 'dus te/ dga' ston rgya chen po mdzad do/ /de nas rgyal pos slob dpon dang bo dhi sa twa la gser gyi phyag rten phul/ rgyal pos kyang rin po che du mas
brgyan pa'i na bza' gsol te/ dpal bsam yas mi 'gyur lhun gyis grub pa'i gtsug lag khang sde skor dang bcas pa la| rab gnas ngo mtshar che ba'i rnam grangs yod pa lan bdun
mdzad/ sprul pa'i skur bstan no/ /de'i rgyud ris kyang / dbu rtse'i sgo rgyab dang / 'khor sa'i sgo 'gram gnyis la bris yod do/ /bka'i thang yig che mo las/ de ltar dpal
gyi

bsam yas la/ /rab gnas dga' ston mdzad pa'i dus/ /mtsho mo gur gyi dkyil drung der/ /padma'i sdong po skyes pa'i gnas/ /rgyal po gser khri'i steng du bzhugs/ /yid 'ong btsun
mo lnga po yang / /mdzes pa'i rgyan dang bcas te bzhugs/ /mchod gnas lo paN thams cad kyang / /dgyes shing chos kyi sgrog gleng mdzad/ /chos blon gtso bo thams cad kyang
/ /rgyal po bzhugs pa'i mtha' la bskor/ /de ltar mnga' 'og spyod pa'i 'bangs/ /dbus gtsang sde rigs thams cad nas/ /ma 'tshogs bya ba gang yang med/ /bza' btung longs spyod
sna tshogs kyis/ /gang la ci 'dod thams cad tshims/ /dga' ba'i bro brdung skyid pa'i glu/ /nyin re bzhin du rgyun chad med/ /gdugs dang rgyal mtshan ba dan sogs/ /gung
la nyi ma grib pa tsam/ /'dab chags bya la 'phur sa med/ /mgo nag mi yis sa gzhi khengs/ /sil snyan rol mo 'brug bzhin ldir/ /gyi ling rta la rgyug sa med/ khye'u bu mo
thams cad kyis/ /chas brgyan lag na rnga ma thogs/ / rnga brdung glu len gar stabs bsgyur/ /g.yag seng dar seng stag seng dang / / 'brug dang seng phrug gar mkhan dang
/ /dpal mdzes rnga thogs 'cham po sogs/ /rgyal po'i sku la mchod pa 'bul/ /de ltar rje 'bangs thams cad kyis// dga' ba'i lus la rang dbang med/ /bro brdung nam mkha'i char
pa 'dra/ /skyid pa'i sems la dran 'dzin med/ /rang rang mos pa'i glu re len/ /de ltar mi rje lhas mdzad pa/ /chos rgyal khri srong lde btsan des/ /rin chen khri las bzhengs
nas ni/ /rgyal po dgyes pa'i glu blangs pa/ /nga yi dbu rtse rigs gsum 'di/ / rin chen lnga las grub pa ste/ /brtsigs pa mi 'dra skyes pa 'dra/ /nga yi lha khang ngo

mtshar che/ /mthong ba tsam gyis nyams re dga'/ /de phyir bsam gyi blo re bde/ / lus 'phags gling la dpe blangs nas/ /shar gyi lha khang gsum po 'di/ /rin chen lnga las grub
pa ste/ /brtsigs pa mi 'dra skyes pa 'dra/ /nga yi lha khang ngo mtshar che| |mthong ba tsam gyis nyams re dga'/ /de phyir bsam gyin blo re bde/ / 'dzam bu gling la dpe
blangs nas/ /lho yi lha khang gsum po 'di/ /rin chen lnga las grub pa ste/ /brtsigs pa mi 'dra skyes pa 'dra/ /nga yi lha khang ngo mtshar che/ / mthong ba tsam gyis nyams
re dga'/ /de phyir bsam gyin blo re bde/ /ba glang spyod la dpe blangs nas/ /nub kyi lha khang gsum po 'di/ /rin chen lnga las grub pa ste/ /brtsigs pa mi 'dra skyes pa
'dra/ /nga yi lha khang ngo mtshar che/ / mthong ba tsam gyis nyams re dga'/ /de phyir bsam gyin blo re bde/ /sgra mi snyan la dpe blangs nas/ /byang gi lha khang gsum
po 'di/ /rin chen lnga las grub pa ste/ /brtsigs pa mi 'dra skyes pa 'dra/ /nga yi lha khang ngo mtshar che/ / mthong ba tsam gyis nyams re dga'/ /de phyir bsam gyin blo
re bde/ /nga yi yakSha gong 'og 'di/ /mkha' la nyi zla shar ba 'dra/ /nga yi btsun mo gling gsum 'di/ /g.yu yi maNDal bkod pa 'dra/ /nga yi mchod rten dkar po 'di/ /dung
dkar g.yas su 'khyil ba 'dra/ /nga yi mchod rten dmar po 'di/ /me lce gnam la bsnyegs pa 'dra/ /nga yi mchod rten sngon po 'di/ /g.yu yi ka ba btsugs pa 'dra/ /nga yi mchod
rten nag po 'di/ /lcags phur sa la btab pa 'dra/ /nga yi mchod rten ngo mtshar che/ /mthong ba tsam gyis nyams re dga'/ /de phyir bsam gyin blo re bde/ /de la sogs pa
dgyes pa'i glu/ /sum cu rtsa gsum lha dbang

gis/ /lha yi glu la dpe blangs nas/ /g.yu khang gser khri bya ba blangs/ /lha sras mu ne btsan po yis/ /'jig rten sgron me bya ba blangs/ /lha sras mu tig btsan po yis/ /seng
ge 'gying ba bya ba blangs/ /btsun mo rnams kyis glu blangs pa/ / g.yu mtsho 'khyil ba bya ba blangs/ /mchod gnas rnams kyis glu blangs pa/ / mkhan po bo dhi sa twa yis/
/sgam phreng dkar po bya ba blangs/ /slob dpon padma 'byung gnas kyis/ /lha 'dre zil gnon bya ba blangs/ /mkhas pa bai ro tsa na yis/ /dbyangs yig khug pa bya ba blangs/
/gnubs ban nam mkha'i snying po yis/ /mkha' la khyung lding bya ba blangs/ /ngan lam btsun pa rgyal mchog gis/ / rta mgrin 'gying dbyangs bya ba blangs/ /mkhas pa cog
ro dpal bzang gis/ / skyid pa'i dpal dgu bya ba blangs/ /blon po rnams kyis glu blangs pa/ /chos blon chen po 'gos rgan gyis/ /drang shing dkar ba bya ba blangs/ /de sras
yab lhag khri bzangs kyis/ /mdzangs yig 'phrul gyi lde mig blangs/ /shud pu dpal gyi seng ge yis/ /ngur chung g.yu rings bya ba blangs/ /dmag dpon lha bzang klu dpal gyis/
/zar chen zar chung bya ba blangs/ /nyang bzang zhang po khri rgyal gyis// seng ge 'grel chen bya ba blangs/ /sbas kyi bstan bzang dpal legs kyis/ / 'dod pa re brgyad
bya ba blangs/ /mgar gyi khyung po dum tshugs kyis/ /bya rgod lding ba bya ba blangs/ /mchims kyi rdo rje sprel chung gis/ /mchims kyi brjed glu bya ba blangs/ /sna nam rgyal
tsha lha snang gis/ /lha shug gong ma bya ba blangs/ khri 'bring lha 'od khug chos kyis/ /mdo chod rab 'bring tha gsum blangs/ /gnyags kyi khri bzang yang bon gyis/
/zla 'od khyab gdal bya ba blangs/ /li ngam stag sgra

klu gong gis/ /lcags sprel gdong drug bya ba blangs/ /gtso bo rnams kyis glu blangs pa/ /ya mtshan gser gyi me tog blangs/ /stag shar rnams kyis glu blangs pa| |stag ru dgu
brtsegs bya ba blangs/ /mo btsun rnams kyis glu blangs pa/ / me tog phreng ba bya ba blangs/ /sman shar rnams kyis glu blangs pa/ /grong zer ring mo bya ba blangs/ /gzhan
yang brjod kyis mi long ste/ /lo skor gcig gi bar du ni| |mi res glu re blangs pa yin/ /skyid pa'i dus su dpal gyi 'dom brkyang ste/ / dga' bde skyid pa'i dpal la longs
spyad de/ /phan bde nyi zla'i 'od lta bur/ / lo skor gcig gi bar du phyogs thams cad du khyab par mdzad do/ /de nas rgyal po'i zhal nas/ tshe 'dir thar pa byang chub don
du gnyer 'dod pas/ tshe 'di'i bde skyid 'dis kyang nges par bslus gsungs te/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar zhing rgyas par bzhed nas/ rgya gar gyi yul nas paNDi ta bi ma
la mi tra la sogs pa'i mkhas pa mang po spyan drangs/ sgra bsgyur gyi lo tsA ba bai ro tsa na dang / kha che A nanda dang / 'dan ma rtse mangs dang / gnyags ku mA ra dang
/ rma a tsArya rin chen mchog dang / 'khon klu'i dbang po/ ka ba dpal brtsegs/ cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan dang / zhang sna nam ye shes sde la sogs pas lo tsA byas te/ sgra
bsgyur rgya gar gling du gzhi bzung nas/ sde snod gsum ka bod du bsgyur/ lo tsA ba snga tshar gsum/ bar tshar gsum/ phyi tshar gsum ste yongs su grags pa lo tsA ba dgu/
dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa nyi ma shar ba lta bur dar zhing rgyas par mdzad do/ /de nas bod 'bangs thams cad dge ba bcu'i khrims la gnas te/ bde skyid
dang ldan par gyur to/ /de nas mkhan po bo dhi sa twa'i zhal nas/ slob

dpon padma 'byung gnas kyis brtan ma bcu gnyis dam la btags pas/ bod du mu stegs pa mi 'ong gis/ ma 'ongs pa'i dus su nang pa dang lta ba mi mthun pa'i dus shig 'ong / de'i
dus su nga'i slob ma ka ma la shI la bya ba yod kyis de gdan drongs shig des lta ba phyogs gcig tu mthun par 'gyur ro zhes gsungs te/ mya ngan las 'das so/ /de nas rgyal
pos chos kyi ring lugs ye shes dbang po la bskos/ de nas mkhan pos ji ltar gsung ba bzhin/ rgya nag gi yul nas ha shang ma hA ya na bya ba bod du byon nas/ dbu ma'i lta
ba la ston min pa bya ba dang / tsen min pa bya ba gnyis su byung nas/ nang pa dang lta ba ma mthun par rtsod pa byed do/ /de'i tshe mkhan po'i zhal chems bzhin/ ye shes
dbang pos mkhas pa ka ma la shI la gdan drangs te bod du byon/ bsam yas kyi thad ka'i pha ri'i chu 'gram du phebs pa dang / ha shang na re/ bdag gis kyang paNDi ta byon pa
la bsu ba byed do gsungs te tshu ri'i chu 'gram du byon no/ /der ha shang byon pa ka ma la shI las gzigs te/ ka ma la shI la'i thugs la ha shang 'di rigs pa dang ldan na
bdag gis nges par thul gyis rigs pa dang mi ldan na mi thul dgongs te/ ha shang gi rigs pa brtag pa'i phyir du/ khams gsum 'khor bar 'khyam pa'i rgyu ni gang yin zhes 'dri
ba'i brda ston pa'i phyir du/ ka ma la shI las khong rang gi dbu la phyag shing lan gsum bskor bas/ de ha shang gis gzigs te/ 'khor bar 'khyam pa'i rgyu gzung 'dzin gnyis
las byung zhes lan 'debs pa'i phyir du/ ber gyi thu ba nas bzung ste/ lan gnyis sa la brdab pas/ ka ma la shI la'i thugs la ha shang rigs pa dang ldan pa zhig 'dug pas/

bdag gis thul bar 'dug go dgongs nas shin tu dgyes par gyur to/ /de nas bsam yas su phebs pa dang / rgyal po'i zhal nas/ bdag ni sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la rab tu mos nas/
gtsug lag khang sde skor dang bcas pa bzhengs/ rgya gar nas paNDi ta gdan drangs/ sde snod gsum gyi chos thams cad bsgyur zhing yang dag par gtan la phab/ dge 'dun gyi sde
btsugs/ chos la dgongs pa gcig tu mthun pa zhig yin na'ang / rgya nag nas ha shang byon te/ chos la lta ba ma mthun par so sor bye bas/ mkhas pa ka ma la shI la gdan drangs
pa yin/ bstan pa gcig la ston pa gnyis mi 'ongs pas/ sangs rgyas bcom ldan 'das kyi dgongs pa mthun par sgro gleng gi rtsod pa mdzod la nga rgyal ma mdzad par rtsod
pa su rgyal de la pham pa des me tog gtor cig gsungs so| |der sems bskyed byang chub gling du gdan khri chen po bshams te/ rgyal po gung la bzhugs/ g.yas phyogs su ha shang
dpon slob rnams bzhugs/ g.yon phyogs su ka ma la shI la dpon slob bzhugs/ rtsod pa byas pas mkhas pa ka ma la shI la rgyal bar gyur te/ ha shang gis pham blangs nas me
tog gtor ro/ /de nas ha shang slar rgya yul la bzhud pa dang / lham ya cig bod du lus pas ha shang gi zhal nas da rung bod du nga'i lta ba 'dzin pa 'ga' re yod par 'dug
gsungs so/ /de ltar yang rgya gar nas paNDi ta mkhas pa byon/ rgyal pos yon bdag mdzad/ lo tsA ba mkhas pas bsgyur zhing gtan la phab pa'i chos la 'jug par gyis shig ces
rgyal pos bka' bstsal to/ /mkhas pa rnams dgongs pa gcig tu mthun cing / dam pa'i chos dar zhing rgyas par mdzad/ sras

mu ne btsan po la rgyal srid gtad nas/ yab zung mkhar smyug ma mkhar gyi pho brang la byon te bzhugs so/ /'di dag ni zur tsam bsdus pa yin gyis/ rgyas par 'dod na bsam yas
kyi bka' gtsigs chen mo la gzigs shig de ltar chos rgyal khri srong lde btsan de dgung lo lnga bcu nga drug pa shing mo glang gi lo la zung mkhar du gshegs so/ /de'i bang
so mu ra ri la brtsigs/ /gral ni yab kyi rgyab ngos g.yas na yod/ /de ni ma grongs pa nas nyid kyis brtsigs/ /ming ni 'phrul ri btsug snang bya bar btags/ /de yi rtsa na
rdo ring zhig kyang yod/ /bang so phyi rgyan can du grags par gyur/ /zhes so/ /nyer gnyis pa/ sras mu ne btsan po ni/ chu pho stag gi lo la brag dmar du sku 'khrungs/ dgung
lo nyi shu rtsa brgyad la rgyal srid bzung / rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur/ btsun mo ru yong bza' mdo rgyal khab tu bzhes/ dge ba bcu'i khrims bzung / yab kyi thugs dgongs
rdzogs pa'i phyir du 'dul ba dang mngon pa dang / mdo sde gsum gyi mchod pa btsugs/ mchod rten chen po bzhi'i gdugs dang / dbu rtse'i bya 'dab lcags thag gis sbrel/ dar
po che/ 'phan chen po rnams 'phyar/ mchod pa dpag tu med pa phul te/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ nga'i yab kyi gtsug lag khang 'di rnams la/ khyed bod 'bangs thams cad kyis rta
phyugs dang / mtshon cha ma gtogs pa/ gzhan gser dngul/ g.yu mu tig la sogs pa'i dngos po gang 'dug phul cig gsungs pas/ rje'i bka' btsan pas/ la las ni gser dngul rin
po che mang po phul/ la las ni g.yu dang ber

dar zab phul/ la las ni gos dang rgyan phul/ la las ni gos hrul po dang / ras slag la sogs pa phul bas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ khyed bod 'bangs rnams dad pa che chung khyad re
che/ la las ni nor dpag med 'bul/ la las ni ras hrul dang ras slag min pa mi 'bul lo zhes gsungs pas/ bod 'bangs rnams na re/ dad pa che chung yod pa ma lags te/ phyug
po rnams la 'bul rgyu yod/ dbul po rnams la 'bul rgyu med pas lan zhes zhus pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ nga'i mnga' 'og 'dir mi rnams la ltogs phyug khyad 'di tsam 'ong ba
mi 'os gsungs te/ ltogs phyug lan gsum snyoms pas/ lo re tsam ma gtogs phyug po rnams ni sngar ltar phyug dbul po rnams ni sngar bzhin ltogs pas/ rgyal po'i zhal nas/ ltogs
phyug lan gsum snyoms kyang / skyid sdug la khyad 'di tsam yod pa ci yin/ gang gis lan zhes gsungs pas/ mchod gnas rnams na re| 'di dag ni sngon gyi sbyin shugs yin zhes
zhus pas/ las rgyu 'bras la rgyal po thugs ches so/ /de ltar rgyal pos sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar zhing rgyas par mdzad de/ mchod gnas rnams dang / rab tu byung ba rnams
ni dbu'i la thod bzhin khur/ 'tsho ba bla nas sbyor/ chab srid ni phan pa dang bde bas bskyangs so// btsun mo pho yong bza' rgyal mo btsun zer ba de/ yab rgyal po'i
yum rgya mo bza'i skye ba yin pas/ yab kyi thugs la 'phreng bar gyur te/ yab zung mkhar du byon dus sras la gtad mnyer mdzad pas sras kyis khab tu bzhes/ yab rgyal po grongs
dus/ pho yong bzas rgyan ma bkrol/ mya ngan ma byas zer ba la bsnyad btags nas/ yum tshe spong bza' phrag dog skyes te/ gshed ma bskos

nas gsod du btang bas/ sras rgyal pos bskyabs pas/ yum log lta skyes te sras la gsol ngan drangs te/ sras rgyal po mu ne btsan po lo gcig dang zla ba dgu la rgyal srid bzung
nas/ dgung lo nyi shu rtsa dgu la pho brang yum bur grongs so| |sras mu ne btsan po'i bang so ni/ ag tshom bang so'i g.yas ngos mdun na yod/ /ming ni lha ri ldem po zer
ro skad/ /ces so/ /nyer gsum pa/ de nas sras 'bring po mu tig btsan po la rgyal srid gtad rgyu la/ mu tig btsan pos kyang snga gong yab bzhugs dus/ blon zhang dbu ring nyes
med du bsad pa'i ngan len du sna nam pas bkrongs so/ /de'i bang so don 'khor mda' ru brtsigs/ /ming ni kya ri kyang ldem lags so skad/ /de nas sras chung ba khri lde
srong btsan sad na legs 'jing yon la rgyal srid gtad/ rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur/ dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs/ sngar med pa'i mdo dang sgra bsgyur/ mchod gnas paNDi ta bi shwa
ka ra/ bai ro tsa na mchog ces/ ka ma la shI la eds: (la )sogs pa'i mchod gnas rnams la zhabs tog byas/ snga gong yab kyis bzhengs pa'i gtsug lag khang rnams la mchod
pa dang mar me phul/ dgung lo bcu dgu lon dus btsun mo lha rtse bya ba khab tu bzhes/ de la sras gcig 'khrungs pa/ dgung lo bcu gsum lon dus yab 'das/ bang so don mkhar mda'
ru brtsigs/nyer bzhi pa/ sras ldeng khri dgung lo bcu bzhi la rgyal srid bzung / btsun mo chen ma la gsum/ btsun mo chung ma zhig la sras lha rje lhun grub gnyis te lnga
'khrungs so/ /dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs/ yab mes kyis bzhengs pa'i

gtsug lag khang rnams la zhabs tog rgyas par mdzad do/ /rgyal po de dgung lo lnga bcu nga lnga bzhes dus/ me mo bya lo la sgrags kyi phur 'das so/ /de yi bang so 'phrul rgyal
g.yon na yod/ /bang so de yang rin chen nor gyis bkang / /yum gyi chab gang bskang pas mtho ba yin/ /ming ni rgyal chen bang so zer ro skad/ /zhes zer ro/ /nyer lnga pa/
der sras che ba gtsang ma ni chos la dga' ste rab tu byung / dar ma ni sdig la dga' ste rje'i 'os min/ bar pa ral pa can la srid gtad do/ /rgyal po mnga' bdag ral pa can
de/ me pho khyi la sku 'khrungs/ dgung lo bcu gnyis la yab 'das te/ rgyal sar bton/ bka'i blon po bran kha dpal gyi yon tan gyis byas/ rgyal khams la dbang bsgyur/ btsun
mo cog ro bza' dpal gyi ngang tshul la sogs pa btsun mo che chung lnga khab tu bzhes/ dge ba bcu'i khrims bzung / rgya gar gyi paNDi ta dzi na mi tra/ shI landra bo dhi/
dA na shI la la sogs pa spyan drangs/ lo tsA ba ka ba dpal brtsegs/ cog ro klu'i rgyal mtshan/ bande ye shes sde rnams kyis chos bsgyur te/ chos thams cad skad gsar bcad
kyis gtan la phab/ bka' bcad rnam pa gsum du mdzad do/ /tha na bre srang / zho la sogs pa thams cad kyang rgya gar dang bstun/ thos bsam sgom gsum gyi sgom grwa btsugs/
'chad rtsod rtsom gsum gyi bshad grwa btsugs/ chos sde sum cu tham par dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs/ mkhas btsun bzang gsum gyi 'dul grwa btsugs/ rab tu byung ba re re'i zhabs
tog la 'bangs mi khyim bdun phul/ rgyal po gung la bzhugs pa la/ dbu'i ral pa g.yas g.yon gyi sne la dar

yug btags/ dge 'dun bzhugs pa'i gral g.yas g.yon la bting / de'i steng du dge 'dun bzhugs par mos la dge 'dun dbu sde gnyis zhes grags so| |thugs dam du 'u shang rdo dpe med
bkra shis dge 'phel gyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs par 'dod nas/ li'i yul nas rig byed la mkhas pa'i bzo bo bos/ bal po'i yul nas lha bzo dang / rdo bzo ba mang po bos nas
lha khang dgu thog tu mdzad pa la/ 'og gi thog gsum sgo dpe dang bcas pa rdo las grub/ bar gyi thog gsum sgo dpe dang bcas pa so phag las grub/ steng gi thog gsum sgo dpe
dang bcas pa shing las grub/ rgya phub dgu brtsegs yod pa/ rgya phub re re'i bya 'dab bar na/ rab tu byung ba chos nyan bshad byed pa bzhugs/ steng gi rgya phub gser 'brug
g.yu 'brug dang bcas pa/ rlung gis bskyod dus gdugs ltar 'khor ba/ bar gyi rtsig pa'i steng na/ rin po che'i pha gu la/ mda' yab dang pu shu/ dra ba dang dra ba phyed
pas mdzes pa/ gdugs dang / rgyal mtshan dang / rin po che'i phreng ba dang / dar gyi cod pan dang / dril bu g.yer kha'i sgra 'khrol ba| rgya phub rtse'i gser 'bru rgyab
ri dang mtho dman mnyam pa/ bod yul kun na 'gran zla dang bral zhing mthong ba tsam gyis dang bar byed la/ rlung chen rgya phub kyi phyogs bzhir lcags thag btang ste phyogs
bzhir rdo'i seng ge dang sbrel/ de la steng gi thog gsum na rje'i thugs dam bzhugs/ bar gyi thog gsum na mchod gnas dge 'dun bzhugs/ 'og gi thog gsum na rje blon 'khor
dang bcas pa bzhugs so/ /de ltar 'u shang rdo dpe med bkra shis dge 'phel gyi gtsug lag khang bzhengs pa'i phud la/ lha sar sa phud/ tshangs pa dang brgya byin/

shing bzo'i phud la gnam yas ka ba bzhi rin po ches brgyan pa dang / ri mo'i phud la rnying pa gso rgyu nyan pa/ be bum brgya rtsa brgyad lugs ma'i phud du ljang la sogs pa
rnams phul lo/ /gzhan yang rgyal po'i mchod gnas/ nyang sha'i spyan dang / blon po 'ga' zhig gis/ lha sa'i shar du/ ka ru dang rme ru/ lho ru dga' ba dang / dga' ba'i 'od/
byang du bran khang dang / bran khang tha ma la sogs pa'i lha khang bzhengs so/ /de ltar rgyal po khri gtsug lde btsan ral pa can de/ mkhyen pa ni 'phrul gyi tshul chags/
mdzad pa ni lha'i lugs dang mthun/ mnga' thang dpal 'byor ni lha'i dbang po brgya byin dang mnyam/ dbang dang mthu stobs kyis ni bdud sdig can skrag par byed pa/ mtha'
bzhi las rnam par rgyal te/ 'dzam bu gling gsum gnyis la dbang mdzad pa yin no/ /de ltar yang snga gong nas rgya bod kyi 'brel tshul/ btsan po dbon zhang rim bzhin byon
pa rnams kyi lo rgyus mthun nas skyes 'bul res mdzad pa dang / 'khon nas dmag 'dren res mdzad pa'i rnam grangs mang du mdzad de/ de'ang rgya'i deb ther chen po zhu thu han
chan bya ba na/ bcom ldan 'das mya ngan las 'das nas lo stong dang lnga brgya drug cu rtsa drug lon pa'i dus rgya nag gi rgyal po thang zhes bya ba byung ste/ bod kyi
rgyal po gnam ri srong btsan dang dus mnyam/ de'i sras tha'i dzun rgyal po'i dus/ srong btsan sgam po dang dus mnyam ste/ bod kyi rgyal pos rgya rje'i sras mo slong ba'i
pho nya btang bas rgya rjes bu mo ma byin par bod du log ste/ rgyal po la rdzun zhus nas/ rgya rje de nged rang la shin tu dga' nas bu mo ster bar yod pa la/ hor ser thu
lu hun gyis rgya rje la phra ma zhus pas lan zhes zhus pas/ bod kyi

rgyal po khros nas bod dmag 'bum phrag gcig khrid de/ zung ci'u bya ba'i sa cha bar du byon/ de nas blon po g.ya' thung bya ba la dmag bskur nas/ thu lu hUn gyi yul 'joms su
btang ba la/ thu lu hUn rnams gtsang kha'i mtsho sngon phan la bros/ shul du lus pa'i mi nor thams cad bod kyis khyer ro/ /de nas bod kyi rgyal pos/ blon po se le stong
btsan la rin po che sna tshogs bskur nas/ rgya rje'i sras mo slong du btang bas/ 'un shing kong jo/ jo bo shAkya/ rdzongs mang po dang bcas pa bod du sleb/ lcags pho khyi'i
lo la/ rgyal po srong btsan sgam po 'das nas/ rgya yul nas bang so mchod pa la nor mang po khyer ba'i pho nya byung ngo / / rgya'i dmag bod du byung ste/ po ta la me
la sregs/ jo bo rin po che btsal bas ma rnyed/ mi bskyod rdo rje snga dro gcig gi bar khyer zer ba sogs rgya'i deb ther na 'dug go /rgyal po 'di'i dus/ de'i dbon po mang
srong dgung lo bcu gsum la rgyal srid bzung bas na so gzhon te/ rgyal srid bya ba cher ma byung kyang / blon po mgar gyis mtha' bzhi'i khrims bsrungs/ de'i dus su rgya'i
dmag bod du byung nas 'joms pa dang / bod kyis kyang blon po mgar gyis dmag dpon byas nas/ bod dmag 'bum tsho gnyis khrid de/ rgya rnams pham par byas/ yul 'khor rnams bcom
nas/ blon po mgar kyang dmag thog tu 'das so/ /rgyal po de'i sras 'dul srong 'phrul gyi rgyal po'i dus su| yab kyi bang so mchod pa la/ rgya yul nas nor mang po khyer
ba'i pho nya byung ngo | |de rjes mgar gyi sras snyan btsan ldem bu dang / thu lu hUn gyi blon po ngo log gnyis dang bcas pas dmag khri tsho gsum khrid nas rma chu'i 'gram
na yod pa'i mkhar dang / mi sde 'joms su phyin pas/ rgya'i li kying hAe na chen gyi dmag

dang phrad nas/ 'thabs pas rgya rnams pham/ de ma khad ling kying gis rgya'i dmag sum stong bsnan nas/ bod dang 'thab tu 'ongs pas/ bod kyi dmag phyir bros so/ /bod kyi rgyal
po 'dul srong mang po rje de'i stobs dang / mnga' thang dang / dbang phyug ni gzhan las che ba yin no/ /rgyal po de'i sras/ khri lde gtsug brtan mes ag tshom gyi dus su/
rgya rje dzung dzung rgyal po dang dus mnyam ste/ rgya rje de'i sras mo kyim shing kong jo bod du byon pa yin no/ /bu mo'i rdzongs la dar zab khri tsho mang po dang /
bzo'i rigs byed sna tshang dang / rgyal po'i mdun la 'gro ba'i lag cha'i rigs gang yin byin nas za ya tha'i byang kun g.yang gu'i hen zer ba'i mi dpon gnyis kyis mgo byas
