dmag mi mang po/ skyel du btang ste mthun pa'i gtam byas so/ /byang ngos dang gha'i sa cha yang lo sum cu'i bar du bod kyis bdag byas/ de'i sras rgyal po khri srong lde
btsan gyi dus su dbon zhang ma mthun par dmag rgyag res mang du byas 'dug cing / zhang rgya tsha lha gnang / dmag dpon lha bzang klu dpal la sogs pas bod dmag 'bum tsho gnyis
tsam khrid nas/ shing kun dang / ce'u mkhar dang / sman tse'i yul rnams bcom/ dbon zhang mthun pa'i skyes phul/ 'khon med par chad na'ang bod kyi rgyal pos kha la rang
re dang mthun par bya zer kyang / sems shin tu gnag par byung zer ro| |de ltar sras mu ne btsad po dang / sad na legs kyi dus su yang / skabs re mthun nas skyes 'bul ba
dang / 'khon nas dmag 'dren res byas pa mang du 'dug go /de ltar/ mnga' bdag ral pa can gyis kyang / dbon zhang dang ma mthun par bod dmag khri tsho mang po khrid nas/
rgya'i yul mkhar thams cad

bcom/ rgya'i ha shang dang / bod kyi mchod gnas rnams kyi bar dang gna' dpang mdzad nas dbon po dgyes pa'i skyes phul/ da phyis 'khon med par chad nas/ rgya yul rme ru bya
ba'i so mtshams su btsan po dbon zhang gnyis kyis lha khang re brtsigs/ pha bong la nyi zla bris nas/ gnam la nyi zla zung gcig sa la btsan po dbon zhang / rgya'i rme ru
man la bod kyi dmag mi drangs/ de yan la rgya'i dmag mi drangs/ phan tshun du sa mtshams bsrung ste/ sa sa mal/ rdo rdo mal du gnas nas/ bod bod yul na skyid/ rgya rgya yul
na skyid pa'i khrims mdzad nas/ dkon mchog gsum dang / nyi zla dang / gza' skar dang / lha gnyan rnams dpang du btsugs te/ dbon zhang gnyis kyis dbu bsnyung dang bro bor
ro/ /de ltar chad mol gyi yi ge rdo ring gsum la byas te/ rdo ring gi zheng che ba gnyis la btsan po dbon zhang gnyis kyis chad mal la bgyis pa'i mna' tshigs kyi yi ge
bris/ zheng chung ba gnyis la bod dang rgya'i blon po/ bka' la gtogs pa'i rtsis pa rnams kyi ming rus bris nas/ rdo ring gcig lha sar btsugs/ rdo ring gcig rgya rje'i pho
brang mdun du btsugs/ rdo ring gcig rgya bod kyi mtshams rme ru ru btsugs so/ /gal te chad mol bgyis pa'i yi ge 'di la ma bsam par bod kyis rgya la dmag drangs na/ rgya
rnams kyis rgya rje'i pho brang gi mdun gyi rdo ring gi yi ge lan gsum klog na bod thams cad phung bar 'gyur la/ rgya rnams kyis bod la dmag drangs na/ lha sa'i rdo ring
gi yi ge lan gsum klog na/ rgya thams cad phung bar 'gyur ro zhes btsan po gnyis kyis ni phyag rgyas btab/ bod dang rgya'i blon po bka' la gtogs pa rnams kyis ni dmod btsugs
so/ /de dag ni

zur tsam yin gyis/ bod dang rgya'i chad mol gyi yi ge zhib par 'dod na/ lha sa'i rdo ring gi yi ge la gzigs shig de rjes sog po'i dmag dpon bod du byung ste/ blon po khyung
zhags bsad pas des rkyen nas bod dang rgya gnyis 'brel chad pa yin zer ro/ /rgya bod lo rgyus deb ther 'di/ rgya nag tha'i dzung rgyal po'i dus kyi yig mkhan su khyi han
gyis bsgrigs pa las rim pa bzhin du bcos te/ dus phyis rgya'i lo tsA ba 'u kyang dzus/ shing khun sde chen du bod skad du bsgyur ba la/ lo grangs mi mthun pa 'ga' re dang
de dus kyi mi'i ming rnams la 'dra min re 'dug na'ang bla ma gu shrI rin chen grags rgya yul na bzhugs dus/ rgya bod kyi 'brel tshul 'di rnams gtan tshigs su bzhed nas/
shing mo bya'i lo la shing kun sde chen du par du btab ste kun la rgyas par mdzad pa yin no/ /'di ni zur tsam yin gyis/ bod dang rgya'i 'brel tshul dang / dbon zhang gi
lo rgyus rnams zhib par 'dod na/ par ma de nyid la gzigs shig de ltar rgyal po mnga' bdag ral pa can des/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che la dgongs nas/ dbang dge 'dun
la gtad/ chos khrims dang / rgyal khrims gnyis gtan la phab/ lha sa/ bsam yas/ dkar chung la sogs pa'i yab mes kyis bzhengs pa'i lha khang rnams la zhabs tog mdzad/ bod
'bangs thams cad dge ba bcu'i khrims la bkod de/ rku dang / jag dang / g.yo zol sogs byed pa med par gyur nas/ blon 'bangs chos la mi dga' ba thams cad spyod pa shin tu
dog par gyur to/ /de nas 'bangs rnams kyis nged rang rnams 'di tsam pa'i spyod pa dog pa 'di gang gis lan zhes gcig la gcig gis smras pa dang / de dag ni

'di rnams kyis lan no zer te/ btsun pa rnams la mdzub mo gtad nas/ mig ngan bltas pas/ rgyal pos gsan te/ nga'i rab tu byung ba rnams la sdigs mdzub gtad nas mig ngan lta bar
mi rigs pas/ da phyis sus byas na'ang mig phyung la mdzub mo chod cig gsungs so/ /de ltar rgyal po chos la shin tu dkar ba de la/ sbas stag rna can la sogs pa sdig blon
rnams shin tu ma dga' nas/ chos khrims 'jig pa'i gros byas nas/ rgyal po ma bkrongs na chos khrims 'jig mi thub zer/ la la na re/ rgyal po bkrongs kyang / lha sras gtsang
ma dang / blon po bran kha dpal yon gnyis chos la dga' bas chos khrims 'jig mi thub zer/ der snga sor lha sras gtsang ma dang / bran kha dpal yon gnyis med pa byas/ de
rting la rgyal po bkrong bar thag bcad/ mo rtsis pa rnams la brngan pa byin nas/ thams cad kha mthun par lha sras gtsang ma 'dir bzhugs na/ sku tshe la bar chod 'ong zhing
/ rgyal srid 'jig par 'gyur zhes glengs nas/ lha sras gtsang ma dpa' gro mon la spyugs/ de'i rjes la rgyal po la sbas stag rna can gyis phra ma zhus te/ chos blon chen
po bran kha dpal gyi yon tan dang / btsun mo cog ro bza' dpal gyi ngang tshul gnyis mi 'os pa'i spyod pa byas so zer nas/ chos blon chen po nyes med la skyon phab nas bkrongs
so/ /de rjes la rgyal po dgung lo sum cu so drug pa lcags mo bya'i lo la/ rgyal po 'bras chang gsol nas gzims pa la/ sbas stag rna can dang / cog ro lha lod gnyis kyis
rgyal po ltag pa bskor nas bkrongs so/ /'di yan la skyid pa'i gdung rabs phyed dang bcu gsum dang / shin tu skyid pa'i gdung rabs lnga zer/ mnga' bdag ral

pa can gyi bang so ni/ /don mkhar mda' yi g.yon zur de ru brtsig /bang so de'ang rin chen nor gyis bkang / /ming ni khri steng rmang ri zer ro skad/ /de nas rje'i mnga' thang
ni dgun kha'i 'bab chu bzhin bri/ dge bcu'i rgyal khrims ni sog rul gyi phon thag bzhin zhig bod 'bangs kyi bsod nams ni snum zad kyi mar me bzhin song / chab srid phan
bde ni nam mkha'i 'ja' bzhin yal/ nag phyogs kyi spyod pa ni yul ngan gyi 'tshub ma bzhin langs/ bzang byed kyi bsam blo ni mdang sum gyi rmi lam bzhin brjed/ de ltar du
gyur te/ lo paN dang mchod gnas la zhabs tog med par so so'i yul la bzhud/ chos bsgyur 'phro rnams bsgyur/ blon 'bangs chos la dga' ba rnams ni mya ngan gyis non te bya
thabs med par gyur to/ /nyer drug pa/ de nas sbas stag rna can la sogs pa'i sdig blon ngan pa rnams dbang ches pas rgyal po khri glang dar ma dbu dum btsan bdud kyi sprul
pa/ chos la mi dga' zhing / sdig pa'i sems dang ldan pa de/ rgyal sar bskos te rgyal khams la dbang byas so/ /dus der paNDi ta dA na shI las lha sa'i shar rme ru lha khang
du mtshams bcad nas/ dzaM lha bsgrubs pas dka' bar byung ba dang / paNDi ta khros te/ dzaM lha 'jim gzugs de'i grod par mkhar sil gyi rting pas brgyab pas/ lcags kyi
rdo rje yin zer ba'ang 'dug grod pa nas gser mang po byung ba dang / de la rgyu byas te sku'i rten du kharsa pa Ni/ gsung gi rten du gser khri/ thugs kyi rten du dngul bya
khun bu can rnams bzhengs/ de'i nye gnas kha che utpa las dngul gyi byams pa bzhengs/ dgongs dus kyi mchod pa btsugs/ dus

der sad dang ser ba dang / btsa' dang / mu ge dang / mi nad phyugs nad la sogs pa byung bas/ de la snyad byas/ rgyal po'i thugs la gdon gsol nas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa bsnubs
so/ /rab tu byung ba rnams la la shan pa bcol/ la la rtags dang phral/ la la ri dwags bshor du bcug ma nyan pa rnams srog dang phral/ lha khang 'jig pa'i sngon ma lha
sa la byas te/ jo bo rnam gnyis chu la bskyur gsungs pa chos blon rnams kyis thabs byas te/ rang rang gi khri'i 'og tu sbas/ byams pa'i sku ras kyis dril nas/ 'o thang
gi mtsho 'gram du sbas/ nang gi lder sku rnams chu la bskyur bsams nas/ phyag na rdo rje'i mgul la thag pa btags pas/ 'dogs mkhan skad cig la khrag skyugs nas shi bas lha
khang 'jig 'phro bcad/ lha sa dang bsam yas la sogs pa'i sgo rtsigrme ru ma gtogs/ gzhan lha khang chung ba thams cad bshig glegs bam la la chu la bskyur/ la la me la sregs/
la la gter bzhin sbas so/ /blon po chos la dga' ba rnams kyis rgyal po'i thugs la gdon gsol bar shes nas mya ngan drag tu byed cing mgrin gcig tu rgyal po chen po sangs
rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che smad par mi rigs/ sngar srol bzang po la dgongs nas/ yab mes kyi yig tshangs la gzigs shig ces ngus so/ /dus der chu bo ri'i sgom grwa na/
g.yo dge 'byung / gtsang rab gsal/ dmar shAkya mu ne gsum sgom gyin yod pa la/ btsun pa gcig gis sham thabs brdzais lag tu mda' gzhu thogs/ mgo la bya sgro btsugs nas
'phral du khyi khrid nas ri dwags bshor gy-in 'dug pa g.yo dge 'byung gis mthong nas/ ban rgan 'khrul lam/ btsun pa smyo zer ci byung dris

pas/ ri dwags pa de bstan nas khong gnyis na re/ khyed cag ma 'khrul/ btsun pa smyo 'dug zer te/ btsun pa de rtsar bos nas rgyu mtshan dris pas/ btsun pa na re| khyed cag gsum
po rgyal po'i chad pa ma phog pa nyen re che zer nas/ chos snubs pa'i lo rgyus rgyas par bshad pa dang / khong gsum po shin tu skrag par gyur nas/ skad cig kyang sdod
pa'i longs med par 'dul ba'i pu sti drel rgyab gsum khyer nas/ byang lam la phyin khams su bros te/ dan tig shel gyi brag phug tu bzhugs so/ /de'i rjes la ka 'od mchog grags
pa dang rong ston seng ge rgyal mtshan gnyis kyis mngon pa dang mdzod kyi pu sti mang po khyer nas khams la bros te/ san chung gnam rdzong gi brag khung du bzhugs so/
/de'i dus su lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje yer pa'i brag khung na/ sgom byed kyin yod pa la nam phyed na lha sa'i bstan srung dpal lha mo byung nas da lta bod na grub thob
khyed las mi 'dugargyal po glang dar mas sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la bar gcod byas/ rgyal po sdig can gsod ran kho mos grogs bya yis/ snying ma chung cig zer ro/ /sang nye
gnas la rgyu mtshan dris pas bden par 'dug nas rang gi srog blos btang ste/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la bsam ste/ rgyal po gsod pa'i spobs pa bskyed nas thabs sna tshogs
byas te/ rta dkar po la sol ba byugs nas nag po byas/ ber phyi nag pa nang dkar ba byas te gon/ mgo la zhwa nag po gon/ gdong la sol snum byug phu thung du mda' gzhu bcug
rta nag la zhon te/ bdud nag po bkrag med yin no zhes zer te lha sar 'ongs so/ /der rgyal po rdo ring gi yi ge gzigs kyin 'dug pa'i drung du phyin te/ phyag byed pa ltar
byas nas yi dam la

dmod btsugs te/ phu thung nang nas mda' gzhu bton/ phyag dang po la mtheb sprad/ gnyis pa la mda' bkang / gsum pa la rgyal po'i dpral ba la mda' brgyab nas bros so/ /der rgyal
pos phyag gnyis kyis dpral ba'i mda' la 'jus te mod la grongs so/ /rgyal po glang dar ma glang lo la 'khrungs/ bya lo la rgyal sa bzung / lo lnga'i bar du chos snubs/
dgung lo sum cu so brgyad lon pa'i stag lo la grongs pa yin no/ /der ra mda' bos nas phyogs bzhir rgyugs pas/ shar phyogs pa rnams na re/ zin la khad yod pa la dga' mo gdong
nas sa sros nas ma mthong bar shor zer ro/ / lho phyogs pa rnams na re/ grib kyi chu 'gram nas sa sros nas ma mthong bar shor zer/ nub phyogs pa rnams na re/ shun gyi
'brang nas sa sros nas ma mthong bar shor zer/ byang phyogs pa rnams na re/ mdong mkhar gdong nas sa sros nas ma mthong bar shor zer/ nges pa can du grib kyi mdar gdong
gi chu la lte nyal byas pas/ rta la sol ba byugs pa dag ste dkar por song / zhwa nag bskyur/ gdong gi sol snum bkrus/ ber dkar po phyir bstan nas gon te/ nga ni lha gnam
thel dkar po yin no zer nas song ngo / /der phyogs bzhir rgyugs pa'i ra mda' ba rnams kha ma 'cham par so so'i mdun du sprul pa re re byung bas/ 'di ni lha lung dpal gyi
rdo rje yin nges zer nas yer ba'i brag la 'tshol du btang ngo | |der dpal gyi rdo rjes brag khung der/ bsam gtan la yod pa'i lugs su byas/ phug ron gcig bzung nas sa rdul
'bebs su bcug de'i steng du mug ma dang grog sbur la sogs pa btang bas de rnams kyi rjes mis mthong ba dang min par shes nas log go /mi rig pa dang ldan pa zhig nang du
byung ste/ khong gi

snying gar lag pa bzhag pa dang / snying 'dar ba shes te/ spyi'i tha ba la/ sgos su shol mi bcog zer nas song ngo / /de nas shin tu skrag par gyur te/ skad cig kyang sdod pa'i
longs med par khams la bros so/ /nyer bdun pa/ der rgyal po sdig can bkrongs pa'i rjes su btsun mo chung ba zhig la gdung brgyud kyi sras ltor zhig byung ba dang / btsun
mo che ba'i bsam pa la 'dis bdag gi mnga' thang la gnod par nges bsam ste/ lus la gos kyis dkris nas nga la'ang sras ltor zhig yod do zhes bu chung che rdzun byas so|
|der btsun mo chung ba'i zla dus thim pa dang / gdung brgyud yin nges kyi sras 'khrungs te/ sku shin tu gces pas nyin mo ni mis bskor/ mtshan mo ni mar me'i 'od kyis bsrungs
pas na mnga' bdag 'od srungs zhes zer ro/ /der btsun mo che bas kyang sprang po'i bu chung skyes ma khad cig nyos nas sha la sbyar te/ nga la'ang 'di skyes pa yin no
zer bas/ thams cad the tshom za bar gyur kyang / yum btsun mo dbang che bas smra ma nus te/ yum ji ltar gsungs pa bzhin brtan du bcug pas/ mnga' bdag yum brtan zhes zer
ro/ /mnga' bdag 'di gnyis sku nar ma son kyang / blon po chos la dga' ba rnams kyis zhus te/ jo bo rnam gnyis dang / byams mgon rnams sa 'og nas bton nas/ rang rang gi khri
la bzhugs nas mchod pa byas/ lha khang zhig pa rnams slar gsos so/ /de nas srid la ma 'cham pas/ 'od srungs kyis g.yo ru bzung nas 'khrug pa byas so/ / sa mo glang la
gyen log byung / me mo bya la bang so rnams bshig go /mnga' bdag 'od srungs kyi sras/ rje dpal 'khor btsan/ de'i chen ma'i sras skyid sde

nyi ma mgon/ 'di nas ya tshe dang mnga' ris kyi rgyal po byung / chun ma'i sras bkra shis brtsegs pa/ 'di nas la stod pa dang yar lung jo bo byung / 'di gnyis kyi srid gang
yod rnams yum brtan gyis phrogs pas/ mnga' ris la bros nas mnga' ris rgyal po mdzad pa yin no/ /sprang phrug gces par gsos pas mnga' bdag yum brtan byung / /rigs ngan dpon
du bskos pas dge bcu'i rgyal khrims med/ /sha gong nyung mas bcad pas phan bde'i nyi ma 'gribs/ /rgyal brgyud mtha' la phud pas rje yi gdung rabs chad/ /ces pa'o/ /nyer
brgyad pa/ yum brtan gyi sras la/ khri de mgon snyan/ de la sras gnyis 'khrungs pa'i che ba rig pa mgon/ chung ba nyi ma mgon/ nyi ma mgon gyi sras nyi 'od dpal mgon/ 'di'i
brgyud rlung shod/ 'phan yul/ mdo khams na mang ngo / khri rig pa mgon la sras gnyis 'khrungs pa'i che ba lde bo/ chung ba rdo rje 'bar lde po'i brgyud bug pa can pa
dang / thang la brag pa rnams so/ /rdo rje 'bar gyi sras khri dbang phyug btsan/ de'i sras tsha na ye shes rgyal mtshan/ de'i sras mnga' bdag khri pa/ yab sras 'di gnyis
kyi dus su bstan pa'i me ro mdo khams nas lang pa yin no/ /mnga' bdag khri pa la sras bzhi 'khrungs pa/ a tsa ra| dge slong / bla ma/ lha btsun bo dhi ra tsa'o/ /a tsa ra'i
brgyud/ 'phrong po ba/ lcang rgyab pa/ glag pa lam pa/ grib pa/ snye thang pa/ lus pa gtsang bo la sogs pa rnams yin no/ /bla ma la brgyud med/ dge slong gi brgyud dpe
bzhi pa/ 'on rdo mong mkhar pa rnams yin no/ /bo dhi ra tsa'i brgyud la/ lha btsun sngon mo snyug rum pa/ lha 'bri sgang pa la sogs pa bsam yas na da lta yod pa rnams yin

no| |de rnams kyi brgyud phyogs thams cad du so sor 'phel bas kyi g.yor kun na yod pa'i jo bor ming btags pa rnams yin pas/ rigs shin tu ma dag pa yin zer ro/ /nyer dgu pa
de ltar rgyal po glang dar mas lcags mo bya la chos bsnubs/ lcags mo bya la bstan pa'i me ro langs nas/ lo skor dgu'i bar du dbus gtsang na chos med do zer kyang / nges pa
can du lo skor brgyad/ lo dgu bcu go brgyad kyi bar chos kyi ming tsam yang med do/ /de ltar gong du bshad pa ltar chu bo ri nas bros pa'i g.yo dge 'byung / gtsang rab
gsal/ dmar shAkya mu ne gsum khams su bros so/ /de'i rjes la ka 'od mchog grags pa dang / rong ston seng ge rgyal mtshan/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje dang gsum snga rting du
bros so/ /de'ang thog mar khams su slob ma byung ba ni/ bon po'i bu rma za gsal gyis phyugs 'tshor phyin pas/ chu bo ri nas byon pa'i dge slong gsum po dang mjal te/ las
'phro'i dbang gis dad pa skyes nas rab tu byung bar zhus pas gnang ste/ mkhan slob song ste gsum kha'i mtshan nas dras te/ shAkya dge ba gsal du btags/ sde snod gsum la
mkhas par gyur to/ /de la brten nas khams pa'i mi bal rdo rje dbang phyug snubs dpal gyi byang chub/ yang gong ye shes g.yu ru/ sbar rin chen/ lcang ye shes seng ge co ro
shes rab byang chub/ gzhan yang shod chung ba shes rab grags/ an 'bar ba byang chub/ grum ye shes rgyal mtshan/ gnubs dpal gyi byang chub/ sgro manydzu shI la sogs pa'i
mkhas btsun mang po byon no/ / de'i tshe rgyal po sdig can gyis chos bsnubs nas lo drug cu lon pa na/ 'phan

yul zhog na rmu gsal gshen 'bar bya ba'i bon po'i bu/ rmu za 'phan bya ba'i byis pa zhig gis/ snang gsal lha khang bya ba'i nang du phyin pas/ rab tu byung ba chos nyan bshad
byed pa 'dra ba'i gzugs gyang ris la 'dug pas ci yin dris pas/ de na 'dug pa'i rgan mo zhig na re/ rab tu byung ba bya ba'i gzugs yin byas pas/ byis pa de sngon gyi las
'phro'i dbang gis dad pa skyes nas mchi ma phyung ste/ rab tu byung ba da lta e yod dris pas/ rgan mo na re/ nga bu mo'i dus na yin te/ rgyal po glang dar mas chos snubs
pa'i dus/ rab tu byung ba rnams phab pas/ rtags dang phral/ la la bsad/ la la shi da lta dbus gtsang na rab tu byung ba med do/ /chu bo ri dang yer pa la sogs nas khams
su bros pa'i rab byung mang po da lta khams na yod thag chod 'dug zer bas/ rab tu dga' ste/ lus dang srog la ma bltas par byis pa des khams su phyin pas/ lha lung dpal gyi
rdo rje dang mjal nas/ dad pa skyes nas rab tu byung bar zhus pas/ lha lung dpal gyi rdo rje'i zhal nas/ bdag gis rgyal po sdig can bsad pas nga la sdom pa med/ ngas grogs
bya yis gsungs nas/ mkhas btsun de rnams dang mjal rab tu byung bas/ ming yang bla chen dgongs pa rab gsal du grags so/ /de ltar khams na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar
zhing / bod na chos med par mun pa'i smag rum du gyur pa na/ rgyal po sdig can gyis chos bsnubs nas lo brgyad cu lon pa na bsam yas kyi mnga' bdag tsha na ye shes rgyal
mtshan des bdag rkyen mdzad nas khams su sdom pa len pa'i thog mar/ dbus gtsang gi mi bdun du grags pa ni/ klu mes shes rab tshul khrims/ 'bri ye shes yon tan/ tshong ge

shes rab seng ge lo ston rdo rje dbang phyug sum pa ye shes blo gros/ rgya blo gros shes rab/ gzhon ban chos mchog dang bdun gyis grum ye shes rgyal mtshan la mkhan po zhus/
co ro shes rab byang chub la slob dpon zhus nas bka' drin mnos so/ /de'i rting la phyin pa lnga ni/ mtha' bzhi rgyal 'phags/ rag shi tshul khrims 'byung gnas/ sba btsun
blo gros dbang phyug skyes legs nyang bran chos skyabs/ grum shing shes rab smon lam mo/ /de ltar sngon la khams su sdom pa len du phyin pa'i mi bdun po des sdom pa blangs
nas phyir 'ongs pa dang / rting la phyin pa'i mi lnga po dag lam la 'phrad de/ gar 'gro dris pas/ khams su sdom pa len du 'gro zer bas/ sngon ma rnams na re/ nged rnams
kyi sdom pa gsum ldan du blangs yod pas nged kyis sdom pa phog pas chog thag ring la 'gro mi dgos zer ba la ma nyan par khams su phyin te/ sngar gyi mkhas btsun rnams dang
mjal/ sdom pa blangs te phyir dbus gtsang du slebs nas bsam yas kyi btsad po tsha na ye shes rgyal mtshan grongs 'dug na'ang / de'i sras btsad po khri pas bdag rkyen
mdzad de/ klu mes la sogs pa rnams kyis dbus gtsang thams cad du lha khang bsam gyis mi khyab pa brtsigs dge 'dun gyi sde btsugs/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa rin po che slar
shing skam gyi phung po la me 'bar ba lta bur phyogs thams cad du dar zhing rgyas pa na bstan pa'i srog rtsa legs par bzung me ro bslangs nas bod mun pa'i gling du sgron
me 'bar bar mdzad pa gong du bshad pa'i khams dbus kyi mkhas btsun rim par byon pa de rnams dang mnga' bdag ye shes rgyal mtshan yab sras rnams sku drin shin tu che'o/ /

sum cu pa/ de ltar bstan pa rin po che la bka' drin che ba'i bod rgyal po'i gdung brgyud gong du bshad pa ltar/ rje dpal 'khor btsan gyi chen ma'i sras/ skyid lde nyi ma mgon
gyis mnga' ris kyi rgyal po mdzad/ spu rangs la'ang dbang bsgyur/ de la sras gsum che ba dpal gyi mgon gyis mang yul bzung / 'di nas jo bo ras chen gyi bar du brgyud/
bar pa bkra shis mgon gyis spu rangs bzung / chung pa lde btsun mgon gyis zhang zhung bzung / 'di gsum la stod na bzhugs pa'i mgon gsum zer/ lde btsan mgon la sras gnyis
te/ 'khor re dang srong nge gnyis so/ /srong nges sku tshe'i stod la btsun mo khab tu bzhes pas sras gnyis 'khrungs pa'i na ga ra tsa dang / dhe ba ra tsa'o/ /sku tshe'i
smad la rab tu byung nas/ lha bla ma ye shes 'od du mtshan gsol/ mthon mthing dpal gyi lha khang bzhengs/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po dang / rngog legs pa'i shes rab la sogs
pa blo rno ba nyi shu rtsa gcig rgya gar du chos slob pa la btang / paNDi ta shraddha ka ra dang warma ta gnyis spyan drangs te/ mtshan nyid kyi theg pa dang / rgyud
sde bzhi po bsgyur zhing gtan la phab/ 'dul ba stod lugs dar bar mdzad do/ /gcen po 'khor res kha char gyi lha khang bzhengs/ de'i sras lha lde pos paNDi ta su bha Shi da
dang paNDi ta rme ru spyan drangs/ lha lde po la sras gsum 'khrungs pa'i che ba zhi ba 'od/ 'bring ba lha bla ma byang chub 'od/ chung ba 'od lde'o/ /'di gsum gyi dus su
lha bla ma ye shes 'od kyis/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la dgongs nas/ rgya gar du paNDi ta gdan 'dren byon pas lam du mu stegs pa'i dmag gis bzung / dge phyogs kyi yon tan
skyed pa'i rtsa sgo thams cad me btsas bsregs te rmongs par byas so/ /

de'i gtam lha bla ma byang chub 'od kyis gsan te/ nor dpag med bskur nas blu ru btang bas/ gser lus dang ljid mnyam pa dgos zer ba dang / yang gser gang yod bskur bas rgya
ma la bteg dus dbu'i cha tsam zhig gser gyis ma long par khong na re/ da ni khyed rnams kyis bdag blus kyang yon tan med/ nga'i rtsa sgo me btsas bsregs nas dud 'gro lta
bu yod pas bdag shi na'ang bla'i/ nga blu ba'i gser rnams khyer la rgya gar na rgyal po dge ba dpal gyi sras bi kra ma la shI la'i gtsug lag khang na/ rig pa'i gnas lnga
la mkhas pa'i paNDi ta lnga brgya pa rnams kyi nang nas gtsug gi nor bur gyur pa/ jo bo rje dI paM kA ra zhes bya ba bzhugs yod par 'dug de la gser phul bod du gdan drangs
la/ sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar rgyas su mdzod cig gsungs te grongs pa dang / pur yul du spyan drangs nas mchod rten du bzhugs so/ /so gcig pa/ der khong gis lung bstan
bzhin/ jo bo gdan 'dren pa la rgya brtson seng la sogs pa la gser bskur nas btang ngo / /bod du 'byon pa la thabs du ma'i sgo nas gsol ba btab pas/ jo bos kyang bod mnga'
ris kyi gdul bya la dgongs/ rje btsun ma sgrol mas kyang lung bstan pa bzhin bod du byon nas/ slob ma nag tsho dang khu rngog 'brom gsum/ lo tsA ba rin chen bzang po|
lo chung legs pa'i shes rab la sogs pa mkhas btsun du ma byon te/ bod gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa nyi ma shar ba lta bur mdzad pas na/ lha bla ma byang
chub 'od de bod la bka' drin che ba lags so/ /

so gnyis pa/ lha bla ma byang chub 'od kyi gcung po 'od ldes paNDi ta kha che dA na shrI spyan drangs/ de'i sras btsan lde/ de'i sras bha lde/ de nas rim pa bzhin du bkra shis
lde bha re na ga lde rnams byung ba 'di rnams kyis gu ge spu rangs mang yul la sogs pa'i rgyal khams la dbang byas pa yin no/ /yang na ga lde'i sras btsan phyug ldes
ya tsher byon te rgyal po mdzad/ de'i sras bkra shis lde/ de'i sras grags btsan lde/ de'i sras grags pa lde/ de'i sras a rog lde/ de'i sras a sog lde/ de'i sras dzi dar smal
dang / a nanda smal gnyis so/ /a nanda smal gyi sras/ ri lu smal gyis lha sar jo bo rin po che'i dbu thog tu gser thog phub/ de la sras gnyis sang gha smal dang / 'dzi
thar smal gnyis so/ /'dzi thar smal gyi sras a 'dze smal/ de'i sras ka len smal/ de'i sras bar rti smal/ de nas ya tshe'i rgyal brgyud chad nas spu rangs nas mnga' bdag
bsod nams lde ya tsher gdan drangs nas rgyal sa bzung / pu Ni smal bya bar mtshan btags/ de'i sras pri ti smal dang / blon po dpal ldan grags gnyis kyis lha sar bcu gcig
zhal gyi steng du gser thog phub/ stod na bzhugs pa'i rgyal brgyud 'di rnams/ gser thog pa rin rdor gyi yig tshang las zur tsam bris pa yin gyis rgyal po re re bzhin gyi
mdzad pa phrin las rnams zhib par shes 'dod pa de nyid kyis yig tshang la gzigs shig /so gsum pa/ yang bod kyi rgyal po'i gdung brgyud gong du bshad pa ltar rje dpal 'khor
btsan gyi chun ma'i sras/ 'di nas la stod dang / gtsang stod tsong kha mdo smad yar lung jo bo la sogs bod kyi rgyal brgyud yin nges rnams yin no/ /bkra shis brtsegs pa

la sras gsum byung ba dpal lde 'od lde skyid lde gsum yin te/ 'di gsum la smad du bzhugs pa'i lde gsum zer/ sras che ba dpal lde'i sras ni sngon po tshom por thugs te/ khab
gung ba klu rgyal ba spyi pa lta rtse glang lung btsad 'khor ba rnams te/ la stod man chod pa rnams yin no/ /sras chung ba skyid lde shangs rta nag tu phog sras drug byung
ba'i lnga byang du gshegs te/ 'bro'i btsad po dang / g.yas ru ru lag gi btsad po pam dang / mus pa dang 'jang nyang stod na yod pa rnams so/ /sras 'bring po 'od lde la
sras bzhi byung ba/ pha ba de se khri lde khri chung nyag lde'o/ /pha ba de se'i brgyud snub yul dang rong dang / g.yag sde nyang stod stag tshal na yod do/ khri lde'i brgyud
ni shar tsong kha'i rgyal po spyan mnga' don chen la sogs pa mdo smad kyi btsad po da lta bzhugs pa rnams yin no/ /nyag lde'i brgyud gtsang g.yas ru na yod/ skyin mkhar
btsad po'i bar du'o/ khri chung gis/ yar lung jo bo'i yang mes/ yar lung du byon nas sku mkhar 'phying ba stag rtse bzung / de'i sras 'od skyid 'bar/ de la sras bdun
byung ba'i che ba zhang rje tsha khri 'bar/ de'i gcung po btsad pa tsha spun drug zhang rje tsha khri 'bar gyi sras drug la g.yu thog gi brgyad sna mo ba 'phying nga ba
don mkhar ba thang 'khor ba rnams so/ / gcung po btsad pa tsha spun drug ni lha spyad dang / brgyud med/ g.yu can gnyis 'di nas yar lung jo bo byung / dar dang brgyud med
lhun po gnyis brgyud med 'od lde dang gung btsan gnyis te drug go /'od btsan dang gung btsan gyi brgyud ni khra 'brug pa bying ba byar ba chu mig gog po na yod pa rnams
so/ /g.yu can ni gar mi yon tan g.yu rung gis gdan drangs nas byas sar byon te bzhugs/ de'i sras jo dga'/ de

la sras gsum yod pa'i sras che ba bya sa lha chen/ 'dis bya sa'i lha khang bzhengs/ khri dar ma gcung por rab tu byung / khri dar ma la sras bzhi byung ba gtsug lde/ sras med/
khri gtsug jo bo rnal 'byor 'di 'ban tshigs su bzhugs/ jo bo smon lam mo/ /'di rab tu byung nas spu gu'i gzims khang dkar po brtsigs te bzhugs/ khri btsug gis byas dang
dos sngon bzung / de'i sras khri btsan/ de'i sras sha kha khri/ de'i sras lha khri la sogs pa yar mda' ba rnams yin no/ /jo bo rnal 'byor la sras gsum byung ba che ba
ja 'bag byung ba/ 'bring ba lha chen no/ /'dis spyil phu'i gdan sa mdzad/ chung ba lha ngam shod pa'o/ /'di rab tu byung nas sras med/ jo 'bag la sras lnga 'khrungs pa'i
jo bo shAkya mgon po/ lha 'gro ba'i mgon po/ 'dis spyi la phu'i gdan sa mdzad pas gdul bya che| lde po 'dis 'ban tshigs bzung / lde chung 'di grongs sras med/ jo rgyal rnams
so/ /'dis srid bzung / lde po'i sras jo bo shAkya rgyal/ de'i sras jo bo shAkya dpal/ 'dis 'gro mgon 'phags pa'i drung du rab tu byung nas sras med/ jo rgyal gyi sras
jo 'bar/ de'i sras gnyis pa'i che ba lha zur khang pa/ 'dis kyang spyil phu'i gdan sa mdzad/ chung ba khrom po ba rnams kyis dpon du gdan drangs te lha khrom po par grags/
jo bo shAkya mgon pos gcung po rnams tha thang du phog nas/ khong rang gi pho brang gnas chung btab/ mnga' thang dpal 'byor nam mkha' dang mnyam/ de'i sras jo bo shAkya
bkra shis kyis pho brang rnying ma btab/ de la sras gnyis byung ba che ba lha brag kha pa/ chung ba mnga' bdag grags pa rin chen gyis 'gro mgon 'phags pa'i chag phyi la
rgya yul du byon/ se chen rgyal po'i lung blangs nas pho brang brag kha la sogs pa'i pho brang mang du btab thams cad la dbang bsgyur/ mnga' thang dpal 'byor nam

mkha' dang mnyam/ de la sras gsum 'khrungs pa'i che ba blo gros 'od/ gnyis pa mnga' bdag shAkya mgon po/ 'dis spyil phu'i gdan sa mdzad/ shAkya mgon po rting ma yin pas/ dpal
'byor che/ chung ba lha btsun tshul khrims bzang po/ gdan sa thil du rab tu byung / 'di rnams nas bzung ste/ yar lung gi jo bo da lta yan la rim par byon pa 'di rnams
bod rgyal po'i gdung brgyud zam ma chad pa yin pas rigs gzugs yon tan khyad par 'phags pa yin/ 'di dag ni zur tsam bsdus pa yin gyis/ yar lung jo bo rim par byon pa rnams
kyi mdzad pa phrin las rgyas par 'dod na/ lha btsun tshul khrims bzang pos bsgrigs pa'i rgyal rabs la gzigs shig bod gangs can gyi ljongs 'dir sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa dar
zhing rgyas pa'i lo rgyus dang / rgya dkar nag gi rgyal po dang / hor dang mi nyag gi rgyal rabs dang / khyad par du'ang bod kyi chos rgyal rim par byon pa rnams kyi rnam
thar bsdus te zur tsam yin no/ /'di dag ni gzhan gyi kha rgyug dang rang gi blo tshod dang rnam rtog gis kun nas bslangs pa'i yid dpyod rnams spangs te/ sangs rgyas kyi
bka' mdo rgyud dang / rgyal po'i bka' 'bum lha sa dang bsam yas kyi bka' gtsigs chen mo/ jo bo rje'i gter yig che chung / chos 'byung gi yi ge che chung / rgyal po bka'i
thang yig hor gyi yig tshang / gzhan yang tshal pa la sogs pa'i sde dpon/ bstan bcos la mkhas pa'i gang zag rnams kyis bsgrigs pa'i rgyal rabs kyi yi ge mang po bsags
nas/ re re bzhin zhib mor bltas/ yin min gyi the tshom rnams bsal/ snang eds: (gna' )skad dang / brda skad go dka' ba rnams bcos te gsal bar byas/ snyan ngag dang sdeb sbyor
gyi rgyan gyis ma bsgrigs

par rang gzhan thams cad kyis go sla bar byas nas dad ldan bstan pa'i eds: (lo ) rgyus 'dod pa rnams mos gus dang / spro ba skye ba'i phyir du legs par bkod pa 'di bden par
shes pa mdzod cig gzhan yang dus phyis kyi gang zag 'di dag la don gnyer byed pa rnams kyis yin min gyi cha mtshon the tshom du gyur na/ sngar gyi yi ge rnying pa rnams
la zhib mor gzigs la 'jug tu rung ngo / /mi shes pa rnams kyis eds: (ma )'chos shig 'di ni gangs can bstan pa'i dar tshul te/ /bstan pa rgyas mdzad chos rgyal mes dbon gyis/
/ston pa'i bstan pa phyogs bcur spel ba 'dis/ /bstan pa dar rgyas yun du gnas par shog /tshogs gnyis lhun po'i khyon ltar mngon mtho zhing / khrims gnyis chos bzhin skyong
ba'i dgongs pa can/ /bstan pa'i sbyin bdag sa skyong rje rnams kyi/ /chab srid phan bde'i dpal la spyod par mdzod/ /chos rgyal rnams kyi rnam thar mdor bsdus 'di/ /lha
btsun rin chen dpal gyis bskul ba'i ngor/ /rdo rje 'dzin pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyis/ /'gal 'khrul spangs te legs par bsgrigs pa yin// 'di yi dge bas sprin med nam
mkha' la/ /thub bstan rgyas pa'i rta bdun 'od stong gis/ /gsung rab phan bde'i pad tshal kha phyes nas/ /dad ldan bung ba'i dga' ston rgyas par mdzod/ /bod yul mtha' 'khob
kha ba can gyi ljongs 'dir ston pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas des zhabs kyis ma bcags kyang gsung gi 'od zer gyis khyab par mdzad nas/ 'phags pa spyan ras gzigs
dbang phyug des/ gang la gang 'dul gyis sems can thams cad thar pa byang

chub kyi lam la 'god par mdzad cing / khyad par 'phags pa de'i thugs kyi sprul pa chos skyong ba'i rgyal po srong btsan sgam po la sogs pa bod kyi chos rgyal rim par byon pa
